00339   public static function LOGICAL_AND() {
00340     // Return value
00341     $returnValue = True;
00342 
00343     // Loop through the arguments
00344     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
00345     $argCount = 0;
00346     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
00347       // Is it a boolean value?
00348       if (is_bool($arg)) {
00349         $returnValue = $returnValue && $arg;
00350       } elseif ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
00351         $returnValue = $returnValue && ($arg != 0);
00352       } elseif (is_string($arg)) {
00353         $arg = strtoupper($arg);
00354         if ($arg == 'TRUE') {
00355           $arg = 1;
00356         } elseif ($arg == 'FALSE') {
00357           $arg = 0;
00358         } else {
00359           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
00360         }
00361         $returnValue = $returnValue && ($arg != 0);
00362       }
00363       ++$argCount;
00364     }
00365 
00366     // Return
00367     if ($argCount == 0) {
00368       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
00369     }
00370     return $returnValue;
00371   } //  function LOGICAL_AND()

00533   public static function STATEMENT_IF($condition = true, $returnIfTrue = 0, $returnIfFalse = False) {
00534     $condition    = (is_null($condition))   ? True :  (boolean) self::flattenSingleValue($condition);
00535     $returnIfTrue = (is_null($returnIfTrue))  ? 0 :   self::flattenSingleValue($returnIfTrue);
00536     $returnIfFalse  = (is_null($returnIfFalse)) ? False : self::flattenSingleValue($returnIfFalse);
00537

00574   public static function HYPERLINK($linkURL = '', $displayName = null, PHPExcel_Cell $pCell = null) {
00575     $args = func_get_args();
00576     $pCell = array_pop($args);
00577 
00578     $linkURL    = (is_null($linkURL))   ? '' :  self::flattenSingleValue($linkURL);
00579     $displayName  = (is_null($displayName)) ? '' :  self::flattenSingleValue($displayName);
00580 
00581     if ((!is_object($pCell)) || (trim($linkURL) == '')) {
00582       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
00583     }
00584 
00585     if ((is_object($displayName)) || trim($displayName) == '') {
00586       $displayName = $linkURL;
00587     }
00588

00590 
00591     return $displayName;

00617   public static function REVERSE_ATAN2($xCoordinate, $yCoordinate) {

00883   public static function MINIF($aArgs,$condition,$sumArgs = array()) {
00884     // Return value
00885     $returnValue = null;
00886 
00887     $aArgs = self::flattenArray($aArgs);
00888     $sumArgs = self::flattenArray($sumArgs);
00889     if (count($sumArgs) == 0) {
00890       $sumArgs = $aArgs;
00891     }
00892     $condition = self::_ifCondition($condition);
00893     // Loop through arguments
00894     foreach ($aArgs as $key => $arg) {
00895       if (!is_numeric($arg)) { $arg = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($arg)); }
00896       $testCondition = '='.$arg.$condition;
00897       if (PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->_calculateFormulaValue($testCondition)) {
00898         if ((is_null($returnValue)) || ($arg < $returnValue)) {
00899           $returnValue = $arg;
00900         }
00901       }
00902     }
00903 
00904     // Return
00905     return $returnValue;
00906   } //  function MINIF()

00924   public static function SMALL() {
00925     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
00926 
00927     // Calculate
00928     $entry = array_pop($aArgs);
00929 
00930     if ((is_numeric($entry)) && (!is_string($entry))) {
00931       $mArgs = array();
00932       foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
00933         // Is it a numeric value?
00934         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
00935           $mArgs[] = $arg;
00936         }
00937       }
00938       $count = self::COUNT($mArgs);
00939       $entry = floor(--$entry);
00940       if (($entry < 0) || ($entry >= $count) || ($count == 0)) {
00941         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
00942       }
00943       sort($mArgs);
00944       return $mArgs[$entry];
00945     }
00946     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
00947   } //  function SMALL()

01028   private static function _ifCondition($condition) {
01029     $condition  = self::flattenSingleValue($condition);
01030     if (!in_array($condition{0},array('>', '<', '='))) {
01031       if (!is_numeric($condition)) { $condition = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($condition)); }
01032       return '='.$condition;
01033     } else {
01034       preg_match('/([<>=]+)(.*)/',$condition,$matches);
01035       list(,$operator,$operand) = $matches;
01036       if (!is_numeric($operand)) { $operand = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($operand)); }
01037       return $operator.$operand;
01038     }
01039   } //  function _ifCondition()

01058

01060     $sumArgs = self::flattenArray($sumArgs);

01062       $sumArgs = $aArgs;

01064     $condition = self::_ifCondition($condition);
01065     // Loop through arguments
01066     foreach ($aArgs as $key => $arg) {
01067       if (!is_numeric($arg)) { $arg = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($arg)); }
01068       $testCondition = '='.$arg.$condition;
01069       if (PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->_calculateFormulaValue($testCondition)) {
01070         if ((is_null($returnValue)) || ($arg > $returnValue)) {
01071           $returnValue = $arg;
01072         }
01073       }
01074     }
01075

01097   public static function LARGE() {
01098     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01099 
01100     // Calculate
01101     $entry = floor(array_pop($aArgs));
01102 
01103     if ((is_numeric($entry)) && (!is_string($entry))) {
01104       $mArgs = array();
01105       foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01106         // Is it a numeric value?
01107         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01108           $mArgs[] = $arg;
01109         }
01110       }
01111       $count = self::COUNT($mArgs);
01112       $entry = floor(--$entry);
01113       if (($entry < 0) || ($entry >= $count) || ($count == 0)) {
01114         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01115       }
01116       rsort($mArgs);
01117       return $mArgs[$entry];
01118     }
01119     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];

01137   public static function PERCENTILE() {
01138     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01139 
01140     // Calculate
01141     $entry = array_pop($aArgs);
01142 
01143     if ((is_numeric($entry)) && (!is_string($entry))) {
01144       if (($entry < 0) || ($entry > 1)) {
01145         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01146       }
01147       $mArgs = array();
01148       foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01149         // Is it a numeric value?
01150         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01151           $mArgs[] = $arg;
01152         }
01153       }
01154       $mValueCount = count($mArgs);
01155       if ($mValueCount > 0) {
01156         sort($mArgs);
01157         $count = self::COUNT($mArgs);
01158         $index = $entry * ($count-1);
01159         $iBase = floor($index);
01160         if ($index == $iBase) {
01161           return $mArgs[$index];
01162         } else {
01163           $iNext = $iBase + 1;
01164           $iProportion = $index - $iBase;
01165           return $mArgs[$iBase] + (($mArgs[$iNext] - $mArgs[$iBase]) * $iProportion) ;
01166         }
01167       }
01168     }
01169     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
01170   } //  function PERCENTILE()

01187   public static function QUARTILE() {
01188     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01189 
01190     // Calculate
01191     $entry = floor(array_pop($aArgs));
01192 
01193     if ((is_numeric($entry)) && (!is_string($entry))) {
01194       $entry /= 4;
01195       if (($entry < 0) || ($entry > 1)) {
01196         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01197       }
01198       return self::PERCENTILE($aArgs,$entry);
01199     }
01200     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
01201   } //  function QUARTILE()

01254     $returnValue = 0;
01255 
01256     // Loop through arguments
01257     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01258     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01259       // Is it a blank cell?
01260       if ((is_null($arg)) || ((is_string($arg)) && ($arg == ''))) {
01261         ++$returnValue;
01262       }
01263     }
01264 
01265     // Return
01266     return $returnValue;
01267   } //  function COUNTBLANK()

01292         ++$returnValue;

01315   public static function COUNTIF($aArgs,$condition) {
01316     // Return value
01317     $returnValue = 0;
01318 
01319     $aArgs = self::flattenArray($aArgs);
01320     $condition = self::_ifCondition($condition);
01321     // Loop through arguments
01322     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01323       if (!is_numeric($arg)) { $arg = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($arg)); }
01324       $testCondition = '='.$arg.$condition;
01325       if (PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->_calculateFormulaValue($testCondition)) {
01326         // Is it a value within our criteria
01327         ++$returnValue;
01328       }
01329     }
01330 
01331     // Return
01332     return $returnValue;
01333   } //  function COUNTIF()

01350   public static function SUMIF($aArgs,$condition,$sumArgs = array()) {
01351     // Return value
01352     $returnValue = 0;
01353 
01354     $aArgs = self::flattenArray($aArgs);
01355     $sumArgs = self::flattenArray($sumArgs);
01356     if (count($sumArgs) == 0) {
01357       $sumArgs = $aArgs;
01358     }
01359     $condition = self::_ifCondition($condition);
01360     // Loop through arguments
01361     foreach ($aArgs as $key => $arg) {
01362       if (!is_numeric($arg)) { $arg = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($arg)); }
01363       $testCondition = '='.$arg.$condition;
01364       if (PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->_calculateFormulaValue($testCondition)) {
01365         // Is it a value within our criteria
01366         $returnValue += $sumArgs[$key];
01367       }
01368     }
01369 
01370     // Return
01371     return $returnValue;
01372   } //  function SUMIF()

01388   public static function AVERAGE() {
01389     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
01390 
01391     $returnValue = $aCount = 0;
01392     // Loop through arguments
01393     foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
01394       if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
01395         ((!self::isCellValue($k)) || (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE))) {
01396         $arg = (integer) $arg;
01397       }
01398       // Is it a numeric value?
01399       if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01400         if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01401           $returnValue = $arg;
01402         } else {
01403           $returnValue += $arg;
01404         }
01405         ++$aCount;
01406       }
01407     }
01408 
01409     // Return
01410     if ($aCount > 0) {
01411       return $returnValue / $aCount;
01412     } else {
01413       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
01414     }
01415   } //  function AVERAGE()

01431   public static function AVERAGEA() {
01432     // Return value
01433     $returnValue = null;
01434 
01435     // Loop through arguments
01436     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
01437     $aCount = 0;
01438     foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
01439       if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
01440         (!self::isMatrixValue($k))) {
01441       } else {
01442         if ((is_numeric($arg)) || (is_bool($arg)) || ((is_string($arg) && ($arg != '')))) {
01443           if (is_bool($arg)) {
01444             $arg = (integer) $arg;
01445           } elseif (is_string($arg)) {
01446             $arg = 0;
01447           }
01448           if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01449             $returnValue = $arg;
01450           } else {
01451             $returnValue += $arg;
01452           }
01453           ++$aCount;
01454         }
01455       }
01456     }
01457 
01458     // Return
01459     if ($aCount > 0) {
01460       return $returnValue / $aCount;
01461     } else {
01462       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
01463     }
01464   } //  function AVERAGEA()

01481   public static function AVERAGEIF($aArgs,$condition,$averageArgs = array()) {
01482     // Return value
01483     $returnValue = 0;
01484 
01485     $aArgs = self::flattenArray($aArgs);
01486     $averageArgs = self::flattenArray($averageArgs);
01487     if (count($averageArgs) == 0) {
01488       $averageArgs = $aArgs;
01489     }
01490     $condition = self::_ifCondition($condition);
01491     // Loop through arguments
01492     $aCount = 0;
01493     foreach ($aArgs as $key => $arg) {
01494       if (!is_numeric($arg)) { $arg = PHPExcel_Calculation::_wrapResult(strtoupper($arg)); }
01495       $testCondition = '='.$arg.$condition;
01496       if (PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->_calculateFormulaValue($testCondition)) {
01497         if ((is_null($returnValue)) || ($arg > $returnValue)) {
01498           $returnValue += $arg;
01499           ++$aCount;
01500         }
01501       }
01502     }
01503 
01504     // Return
01505     if ($aCount > 0) {
01506       return $returnValue / $aCount;
01507     } else {
01508       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
01509     }
01510   } //  function AVERAGEIF()

01526   public static function MEDIAN() {
01527     // Return value
01528     $returnValue = self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01529 
01530     $mArgs = array();
01531     // Loop through arguments
01532     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01533     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01534       // Is it a numeric value?
01535       if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01536         $mArgs[] = $arg;
01537       }
01538     }
01539 
01540     $mValueCount = count($mArgs);
01541     if ($mValueCount > 0) {
01542       sort($mArgs,SORT_NUMERIC);
01543       $mValueCount = $mValueCount / 2;
01544       if ($mValueCount == floor($mValueCount)) {
01545         $returnValue = ($mArgs[$mValueCount--] + $mArgs[$mValueCount]) / 2;
01546       } else {
01547         $mValueCount == floor($mValueCount);
01548         $returnValue = $mArgs[$mValueCount];
01549       }
01550     }
01551 
01552     // Return
01553     return $returnValue;
01554   } //  function MEDIAN()
01555 
01556 
01557   //
01558   //  Special variant of array_count_values that isn't limited to strings and integers,
01559   //    but can work with floating point numbers as values
01560   //
01561   private static function _modeCalc($data) {
01562     $frequencyArray = array();
01563     foreach($data as $datum) {
01564       $found = False;
01565       foreach($frequencyArray as $key => $value) {
01566         if ((string) $value['value'] == (string) $datum) {
01567           ++$frequencyArray[$key]['frequency'];
01568           $found = True;
01569           break;
01570         }
01571       }
01572       if (!$found) {
01573         $frequencyArray[] = array('value'   => $datum,
01574                       'frequency' =>  1 );
01575       }
01576     }
01577 
01578     foreach($frequencyArray as $key => $value) {
01579       $frequencyList[$key] = $value['frequency'];
01580       $valueList[$key] = $value['value'];
01581     }
01582     array_multisort($frequencyList, SORT_DESC, $valueList, SORT_ASC, SORT_NUMERIC, $frequencyArray);
01583 
01584     if ($frequencyArray[0]['frequency'] == 1) {
01585       return self::NA();
01586     }
01587     return $frequencyArray[0]['value'];
01588   } //  function _modeCalc()

01604   public static function MODE() {
01605     // Return value
01606     $returnValue = self::NA();
01607 
01608     // Loop through arguments
01609     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01610 
01611     $mArgs = array();
01612     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01613       // Is it a numeric value?
01614       if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01615         $mArgs[] = $arg;
01616       }
01617     }
01618 
01619     if (count($mArgs) > 0) {
01620       return self::_modeCalc($mArgs);
01621     }
01622 
01623     // Return
01624     return $returnValue;
01625   } //  function MODE()

01641   public static function DEVSQ() {
01642     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
01643 
01644     // Return value
01645     $returnValue = null;
01646 
01647     $aMean = self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
01648     if ($aMean != self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero']) {
01649       $aCount = -1;
01650       foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
01651         // Is it a numeric value?
01652         if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
01653           ((!self::isCellValue($k)) || (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE))) {
01654           $arg = (integer) $arg;
01655         }
01656         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01657           if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01658             $returnValue = pow(($arg - $aMean),2);
01659           } else {
01660             $returnValue += pow(($arg - $aMean),2);
01661           }
01662           ++$aCount;
01663         }
01664       }
01665 
01666       // Return
01667       if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01668         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01669       } else {
01670         return $returnValue;
01671       }
01672     }
01673     return self::NA();
01674   } //  function DEVSQ()

01691   public static function AVEDEV() {
01692     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
01693 
01694     // Return value
01695     $returnValue = null;
01696 
01697     $aMean = self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
01698     if ($aMean != self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero']) {
01699       $aCount = 0;
01700       foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
01701         if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
01702           ((!self::isCellValue($k)) || (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE))) {
01703           $arg = (integer) $arg;
01704         }
01705         // Is it a numeric value?
01706         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01707           if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01708             $returnValue = abs($arg - $aMean);
01709           } else {
01710             $returnValue += abs($arg - $aMean);
01711           }
01712           ++$aCount;
01713         }
01714       }
01715 
01716       // Return
01717       if ($aCount == 0) {
01718         return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
01719       }
01720       return $returnValue / $aCount;
01721     }
01722     return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01723   } //  function AVEDEV()

01741   public static function GEOMEAN() {
01742     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01743 
01744     $aMean = self::PRODUCT($aArgs);
01745     if (is_numeric($aMean) && ($aMean > 0)) {
01746       $aCount = self::COUNT($aArgs) ;
01747       if (self::MIN($aArgs) > 0) {
01748         return pow($aMean, (1 / $aCount));
01749       }
01750     }
01751     return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01752   } //  GEOMEAN()

01769   public static function HARMEAN() {
01770     // Return value
01771     $returnValue = self::NA();
01772 
01773     // Loop through arguments
01774     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01775     if (self::MIN($aArgs) < 0) {
01776       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01777     }
01778     $aCount = 0;
01779     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01780       // Is it a numeric value?
01781       if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01782         if ($arg <= 0) {
01783           return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01784         }
01785         if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01786           $returnValue = (1 / $arg);
01787         } else {
01788           $returnValue += (1 / $arg);
01789         }
01790         ++$aCount;
01791       }
01792     }
01793 
01794     // Return
01795     if ($aCount > 0) {
01796       return 1 / ($returnValue / $aCount);
01797     } else {
01798       return $returnValue;
01799     }
01800   } //  function HARMEAN()

01819   public static function TRIMMEAN() {
01820     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
01821 
01822     // Calculate
01823     $percent = array_pop($aArgs);
01824 
01825     if ((is_numeric($percent)) && (!is_string($percent))) {
01826       if (($percent < 0) || ($percent > 1)) {
01827         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
01828       }
01829       $mArgs = array();
01830       foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
01831         // Is it a numeric value?
01832         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01833           $mArgs[] = $arg;
01834         }
01835       }
01836       $discard = floor(self::COUNT($mArgs) * $percent / 2);
01837       sort($mArgs);
01838       for ($i=0; $i < $discard; ++$i) {
01839         array_pop($mArgs);
01840         array_shift($mArgs);
01841       }
01842       return self::AVERAGE($mArgs);
01843     }
01844     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
01845   } //  function TRIMMEAN()

01862   public static function STDEV() {
01863     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
01864 
01865     // Return value
01866     $returnValue = null;
01867 
01868     $aMean = self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
01869     if (!is_null($aMean)) {
01870       $aCount = -1;
01871       foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
01872         if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
01873           ((!self::isCellValue($k)) || (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE))) {
01874           $arg = (integer) $arg;
01875         }
01876         // Is it a numeric value?
01877         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
01878           if (is_null($returnValue)) {
01879             $returnValue = pow(($arg - $aMean),2);
01880           } else {
01881             $returnValue += pow(($arg - $aMean),2);
01882           }
01883           ++$aCount;
01884         }
01885       }
01886 
01887       // Return
01888       if (($aCount > 0) && ($returnValue >= 0)) {
01889         return sqrt($returnValue / $aCount);
01890       }
01891     }
01892     return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
01893   } //  function STDEV()

02060   public static function VARFunc() {
02061     // Return value
02062     $returnValue = self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
02063 
02064     $summerA = $summerB = 0;
02065 
02066     // Loop through arguments
02067     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
02068     $aCount = 0;
02069     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
02070       if (is_bool($arg)) { $arg = (integer) $arg; }
02071       // Is it a numeric value?
02072       if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
02073         $summerA += ($arg * $arg);
02074         $summerB += $arg;
02075         ++$aCount;
02076       }
02077     }
02078 
02079     // Return
02080     if ($aCount > 1) {
02081       $summerA *= $aCount;
02082       $summerB *= $summerB;
02083       $returnValue = ($summerA - $summerB) / ($aCount * ($aCount - 1));
02084     }
02085     return $returnValue;
02086   } //  function VARFunc()

02229       $summerA *= $aCount;
02230       $summerB *= $summerB;
02231       $returnValue = ($summerA - $summerB) / ($aCount * $aCount);
02232     }
02233     return $returnValue;
02234   } //  function VARPA()
02235 
02236 
02247   public static function RANK($value,$valueSet,$order=0) {
02248     $value = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
02249     $valueSet = self::flattenArray($valueSet);
02250     $order  = (is_null($order)) ? 0 : (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($order);
02251 
02252     foreach($valueSet as $key => $valueEntry) {
02253       if (!is_numeric($valueEntry)) {
02254         unset($valueSet[$key]);
02255       }
02256     }
02257 
02258     if ($order == 0) {
02259       rsort($valueSet,SORT_NUMERIC);
02260     } else {
02261       sort($valueSet,SORT_NUMERIC);
02262     }
02263     $pos = array_search($value,$valueSet);
02264     if ($pos === False) {
02265       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
02266     }
02267 
02268     return ++$pos;
02269   } //  function RANK()
02270 
02271 
02282   public static function PERCENTRANK($valueSet,$value,$significance=3) {
02283     $valueSet = self::flattenArray($valueSet);
02284     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
02285     $significance = (is_null($significance))  ? 3 : (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($significance);
02286 
02287     foreach($valueSet as $key => $valueEntry) {
02288       if (!is_numeric($valueEntry)) {
02289         unset($valueSet[$key]);
02290       }
02291     }
02292     sort($valueSet,SORT_NUMERIC);
02293     $valueCount = count($valueSet);
02294     if ($valueCount == 0) {
02295       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02296     }
02297 
02298     $valueAdjustor = $valueCount - 1;
02299     if (($value < $valueSet[0]) || ($value > $valueSet[$valueAdjustor])) {
02300       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
02301     }
02302 
02303     $pos = array_search($value,$valueSet);
02304     if ($pos === False) {
02305       $pos = 0;
02306       $testValue = $valueSet[0];
02307       while ($testValue < $value) {
02308         $testValue = $valueSet[++$pos];
02309       }
02310       --$pos;
02311       $pos += (($value - $valueSet[$pos]) / ($testValue - $valueSet[$pos]));
02312     }
02313 
02314     return round($pos / $valueAdjustor,$significance);
02315   } //  function PERCENTRANK()

02318   private static function _checkTrendArrays(&$array1,&$array2) {
02319     if (!is_array($array1)) { $array1 = array($array1); }
02320     if (!is_array($array2)) { $array2 = array($array2); }
02321 
02322     $array1 = self::flattenArray($array1);
02323     $array2 = self::flattenArray($array2);
02324     foreach($array1 as $key => $value) {
02325       if ((is_bool($value)) || (is_string($value)) || (is_null($value))) {
02326         unset($array1[$key]);
02327         unset($array2[$key]);
02328       }
02329     }
02330     foreach($array2 as $key => $value) {
02331       if ((is_bool($value)) || (is_string($value)) || (is_null($value))) {
02332         unset($array1[$key]);
02333         unset($array2[$key]);
02334       }
02335     }
02336     $array1 = array_merge($array1);
02337     $array2 = array_merge($array2);
02338 
02339     return True;
02340   } //  function _checkTrendArrays()

02520   public static function LINEST($yValues,$xValues=null,$const=True,$stats=False) {
02521     $const  = (is_null($const)) ? True :  (boolean) self::flattenSingleValue($const);
02522     $stats  = (is_null($stats)) ? False : (boolean) self::flattenSingleValue($stats);
02523     if (is_null($xValues)) $xValues = range(1,count(self::flattenArray($yValues)));
02524 
02525     if (!self::_checkTrendArrays($yValues,$xValues)) {
02526       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02527     }
02528     $yValueCount = count($yValues);
02529     $xValueCount = count($xValues);
02530 
02531 
02532     if (($yValueCount == 0) || ($yValueCount != $xValueCount)) {
02533       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
02534     } elseif ($yValueCount == 1) {
02535       return 0;
02536     }
02537 
02538     $bestFitLinear = trendClass::calculate(trendClass::TREND_LINEAR,$yValues,$xValues,$const);
02539     if ($stats) {
02540       return array( array( $bestFitLinear->getSlope(),
02541                  $bestFitLinear->getSlopeSE(),
02542                  $bestFitLinear->getGoodnessOfFit(),
02543                  $bestFitLinear->getF(),
02544                  $bestFitLinear->getSSRegression(),
02545                  ),
02546               array( $bestFitLinear->getIntersect(),
02547                  $bestFitLinear->getIntersectSE(),
02548                  $bestFitLinear->getStdevOfResiduals(),
02549                  $bestFitLinear->getDFResiduals(),
02550                  $bestFitLinear->getSSResiduals()
02551                  )
02552             );
02553     } else {
02554       return array( $bestFitLinear->getSlope(),
02555               $bestFitLinear->getIntersect()
02556             );
02557     }
02558   } //  function LINEST()

02573   public static function LOGEST($yValues,$xValues=null,$const=True,$stats=False) {
02574     $const  = (is_null($const)) ? True :  (boolean) self::flattenSingleValue($const);
02575     $stats  = (is_null($stats)) ? False : (boolean) self::flattenSingleValue($stats);
02576     if (is_null($xValues)) $xValues = range(1,count(self::flattenArray($yValues)));
02577 
02578     if (!self::_checkTrendArrays($yValues,$xValues)) {
02579       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02580     }
02581     $yValueCount = count($yValues);
02582     $xValueCount = count($xValues);
02583 
02584     foreach($yValues as $value) {
02585       if ($value <= 0.0) {
02586         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02587       }
02588     }
02589 
02590 
02591     if (($yValueCount == 0) || ($yValueCount != $xValueCount)) {
02592       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
02593     } elseif ($yValueCount == 1) {
02594       return 1;
02595     }
02596 
02597     $bestFitExponential = trendClass::calculate(trendClass::TREND_EXPONENTIAL,$yValues,$xValues,$const);
02598     if ($stats) {
02599       return array( array( $bestFitExponential->getSlope(),
02600                  $bestFitExponential->getSlopeSE(),
02601                  $bestFitExponential->getGoodnessOfFit(),
02602                  $bestFitExponential->getF(),
02603                  $bestFitExponential->getSSRegression(),
02604                  ),
02605               array( $bestFitExponential->getIntersect(),
02606                  $bestFitExponential->getIntersectSE(),
02607                  $bestFitExponential->getStdevOfResiduals(),
02608                  $bestFitExponential->getDFResiduals(),
02609                  $bestFitExponential->getSSResiduals()
02610                  )
02611             );
02612     } else {
02613       return array( $bestFitExponential->getSlope(),
02614               $bestFitExponential->getIntersect()
02615             );
02616     }
02617   } //  function LOGEST()

02715   private static function _romanCut($num, $n) {
02716     return ($num - ($num % $n ) ) / $n;
02717   } //  function _romanCut()

02720   public static function ROMAN($aValue, $style=0) {
02721     $aValue = (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($aValue);
02722     $style  = (is_null($style)) ? 0 : (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($style);
02723     if ((!is_numeric($aValue)) || ($aValue < 0) || ($aValue >= 4000)) {
02724       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02725     }
02726     if ($aValue == 0) {
02727       return '';
02728     }
02729 
02730     $mill = Array('', 'M', 'MM', 'MMM', 'MMMM', 'MMMMM');
02731     $cent = Array('', 'C', 'CC', 'CCC', 'CD', 'D', 'DC', 'DCC', 'DCCC', 'CM');
02732     $tens = Array('', 'X', 'XX', 'XXX', 'XL', 'L', 'LX', 'LXX', 'LXXX', 'XC');
02733     $ones = Array('', 'I', 'II', 'III', 'IV', 'V', 'VI', 'VII', 'VIII', 'IX');
02734 
02735     $roman = '';
02736     while ($aValue > 5999) {
02737       $roman .= 'M';
02738       $aValue -= 1000;
02739     }
02740     $m = self::_romanCut($aValue, 1000);  $aValue %= 1000;
02741     $c = self::_romanCut($aValue, 100);   $aValue %= 100;
02742     $t = self::_romanCut($aValue, 10);    $aValue %= 10;
02743 
02744     return $roman.$mill[$m].$cent[$c].$tens[$t].$ones[$aValue];
02745   } //  function ROMAN()

02758   public static function SUBTOTAL() {
02759     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
02760 
02761     // Calculate
02762     $subtotal = array_shift($aArgs);
02763 
02764     if ((is_numeric($subtotal)) && (!is_string($subtotal))) {
02765       switch($subtotal) {
02766         case 1  :
02767           return self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
02768           break;
02769         case 2  :
02770           return self::COUNT($aArgs);
02771           break;
02772         case 3  :
02773           return self::COUNTA($aArgs);
02774           break;
02775         case 4  :
02776           return self::MAX($aArgs);
02777           break;
02778         case 5  :
02779           return self::MIN($aArgs);
02780           break;
02781         case 6  :
02782           return self::PRODUCT($aArgs);
02783           break;
02784         case 7  :
02785           return self::STDEV($aArgs);
02786           break;
02787         case 8  :
02788           return self::STDEVP($aArgs);
02789           break;
02790         case 9  :
02791           return self::SUM($aArgs);
02792           break;
02793         case 10 :
02794           return self::VARFunc($aArgs);
02795           break;
02796         case 11 :
02797           return self::VARP($aArgs);
02798           break;
02799       }
02800     }
02801     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02802   } //  function SUBTOTAL()

02813   public static function SQRTPI($number) {

02815 
02816     if (is_numeric($number)) {
02817       if ($number < 0) {
02818         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02819       }
02820       return sqrt($number * M_PI) ;
02821     }
02822     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02823   } //  function SQRTPI()

02834   public static function FACT($factVal) {
02835     $factVal  = self::flattenSingleValue($factVal);
02836 
02837     if (is_numeric($factVal)) {
02838       if ($factVal < 0) {
02839         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02840       }
02841       $factLoop = floor($factVal);
02842       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
02843         if ($factVal > $factLoop) {
02844           return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02845         }
02846       }
02847 
02848       $factorial = 1;
02849       while ($factLoop > 1) {
02850         $factorial *= $factLoop--;
02851       }
02852       return $factorial ;
02853     }
02854     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02855   } //  function FACT()
02856 
02857 
02866   public static function FACTDOUBLE($factVal) {
02867     $factLoop = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($factVal));
02868 
02869     if (is_numeric($factLoop)) {
02870       if ($factVal < 0) {
02871         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02872       }
02873       $factorial = 1;
02874       while ($factLoop > 1) {
02875         $factorial *= $factLoop--;
02876         --$factLoop;
02877       }
02878       return $factorial ;
02879     }
02880     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02881   } //  function FACTDOUBLE()
02882 
02883 
02892   public static function MULTINOMIAL() {
02893     // Loop through arguments
02894     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
02895     $summer = 0;
02896     $divisor = 1;
02897     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
02898       // Is it a numeric value?
02899       if (is_numeric($arg)) {
02900         if ($arg < 1) {
02901           return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02902         }
02903         $summer += floor($arg);
02904         $divisor *= self::FACT($arg);
02905       } else {
02906         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02907       }
02908     }
02909 
02910     // Return
02911     if ($summer > 0) {
02912       $summer = self::FACT($summer);
02913       return $summer / $divisor;
02914     }
02915     return 0;
02916   } //  function MULTINOMIAL()

02918 
02928   public static function CEILING($number,$significance=null) {
02929     $number     = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
02930     $significance = self::flattenSingleValue($significance);
02931 
02932     if ((is_null($significance)) && (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC)) {
02933       $significance = $number/abs($number);
02934     }
02935 
02936     if ((is_numeric($number)) && (is_numeric($significance))) {
02937       if (self::SIGN($number) == self::SIGN($significance)) {
02938         if ($significance == 0.0) {
02939           return 0;
02940         }
02941         return ceil($number / $significance) * $significance;
02942       } else {
02943         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
02944       }
02945     }
02946     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02947   } //  function CEILING()
02948

02958   public static function EVEN($number) {
02959     $number = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
02960 
02961     if (is_numeric($number)) {
02962       $significance = 2 * self::SIGN($number);
02963       return self::CEILING($number,$significance);
02964     }
02965     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02966   } //  function EVEN()
02967 
02968 
02977   public static function ODD($number) {
02978     $number = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
02979 
02980     if (is_numeric($number)) {
02981       $significance = self::SIGN($number);
02982       if ($significance == 0) {
02983         return 1;
02984       }
02985       $result = self::CEILING($number,$significance);
02986       if (self::IS_EVEN($result)) {
02987         $result += $significance;
02988       }
02989       return $result;
02990     }
02991     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
02992   } //  function ODD()

03022   public static function ROUNDUP($number,$digits) {
03023     $number = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
03024     $digits = self::flattenSingleValue($digits);
03025 
03026     if ((is_numeric($number)) && (is_numeric($digits))) {
03027       $significance = pow(10,$digits);
03028       if ($number < 0.0) {
03029         return floor($number * $significance) / $significance;
03030       } else {
03031         return ceil($number * $significance) / $significance;
03032       }
03033     }
03034     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03035   } //  function ROUNDUP()

03047   public static function ROUNDDOWN($number,$digits) {
03048     $number = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
03049     $digits = self::flattenSingleValue($digits);
03050 
03051     if ((is_numeric($number)) && (is_numeric($digits))) {
03052       $significance = pow(10,$digits);
03053       if ($number < 0.0) {
03054         return ceil($number * $significance) / $significance;
03055       } else {
03056         return floor($number * $significance) / $significance;
03057       }
03058     }
03059     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03060   } //  function ROUNDDOWN()

03072   public static function MROUND($number,$multiple) {
03073     $number   = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
03074     $multiple = self::flattenSingleValue($multiple);
03075 
03076     if ((is_numeric($number)) && (is_numeric($multiple))) {
03077       if ($multiple == 0) {
03078         return 0;
03079       }
03080       if ((self::SIGN($number)) == (self::SIGN($multiple))) {
03081         $multiplier = 1 / $multiple;
03082         return round($number * $multiplier) / $multiplier;
03083       }
03084       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03085     }
03086     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03087   } //  function MROUND()

03099   public static function SIGN($number) {
03100     $number = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
03101 
03102     if (is_numeric($number)) {
03103       if ($number == 0.0) {
03104         return 0;
03105       }
03106       return $number / abs($number);
03107     }
03108     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03109   } //  function SIGN()

03121   public static function FLOOR($number,$significance=null) {
03122     $number     = self::flattenSingleValue($number);
03123     $significance = self::flattenSingleValue($significance);
03124 
03125     if ((is_null($significance)) && (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC)) {
03126       $significance = $number/abs($number);
03127     }
03128 
03129     if ((is_numeric($number)) && (is_numeric($significance))) {
03130       if ((float) $significance == 0.0) {
03131         return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
03132       }
03133       if (self::SIGN($number) == self::SIGN($significance)) {
03134         return floor($number / $significance) * $significance;
03135       } else {
03136         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03137       }
03138     }
03139     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03140   } //  function FLOOR()

03156   public static function PERMUT($numObjs,$numInSet) {
03157     $numObjs  = self::flattenSingleValue($numObjs);
03158     $numInSet = self::flattenSingleValue($numInSet);
03159 
03160     if ((is_numeric($numObjs)) && (is_numeric($numInSet))) {
03161       $numInSet = floor($numInSet);
03162       if ($numObjs < $numInSet) {
03163         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03164       }
03165       return round(self::FACT($numObjs) / self::FACT($numObjs - $numInSet));
03166     }
03167     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03168   } //  function PERMUT()

03181   public static function COMBIN($numObjs,$numInSet) {
03182     $numObjs  = self::flattenSingleValue($numObjs);
03183     $numInSet = self::flattenSingleValue($numInSet);
03184 
03185     if ((is_numeric($numObjs)) && (is_numeric($numInSet))) {
03186       if ($numObjs < $numInSet) {
03187         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03188       } elseif ($numInSet < 0) {
03189         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03190       }
03191       return round(self::FACT($numObjs) / self::FACT($numObjs - $numInSet)) / self::FACT($numInSet);
03192     }
03193     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03194   } //  function COMBIN()

03208   public static function SERIESSUM() {
03209     // Return value
03210     $returnValue = 0;
03211 
03212     // Loop through arguments
03213     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
03214 
03215     $x = array_shift($aArgs);
03216     $n = array_shift($aArgs);
03217     $m = array_shift($aArgs);
03218 
03219     if ((is_numeric($x)) && (is_numeric($n)) && (is_numeric($m))) {
03220       // Calculate
03221       $i = 0;
03222       foreach($aArgs as $arg) {
03223         // Is it a numeric value?
03224         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
03225           $returnValue += $arg * pow($x,$n + ($m * $i++));
03226         } else {
03227           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03228         }
03229       }
03230       // Return
03231       return $returnValue;
03232     }
03233     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03234   } //  function SERIESSUM()

03247   public static function STANDARDIZE($value,$mean,$stdDev) {
03248     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
03249     $mean = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
03250     $stdDev = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
03251 
03252     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($mean)) && (is_numeric($stdDev))) {
03253       if ($stdDev <= 0) {
03254         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03255       }
03256       return ($value - $mean) / $stdDev ;
03257     }
03258     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03259   } //  function STANDARDIZE()

03261 
03262   //
03263   //  Private method to return an array of the factors of the input value
03264   //
03265   private static function _factors($value) {
03266     $startVal = floor(sqrt($value));
03267 
03268     $factorArray = array();
03269     for ($i = $startVal; $i > 1; --$i) {
03270       if (($value % $i) == 0) {
03271         $factorArray = array_merge($factorArray,self::_factors($value / $i));
03272         $factorArray = array_merge($factorArray,self::_factors($i));
03273         if ($i <= sqrt($value)) {
03274           break;
03275         }
03276       }
03277     }
03278     if (count($factorArray) > 0) {
03279       rsort($factorArray);
03280       return $factorArray;
03281     } else {
03282       return array((integer) $value);
03283     }
03284   } //  function _factors()

03286 
03295   public static function LCM() {
03296     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
03297 
03298     $returnValue = 1;
03299     $allPoweredFactors = array();
03300     foreach($aArgs as $value) {
03301       if (!is_numeric($value)) {
03302         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03303       }
03304       if ($value == 0) {
03305         return 0;
03306       } elseif ($value < 0) {
03307         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03308       }
03309       $myFactors = self::_factors(floor($value));
03310       $myCountedFactors = array_count_values($myFactors);
03311       $myPoweredFactors = array();
03312       foreach($myCountedFactors as $myCountedFactor => $myCountedPower) {
03313         $myPoweredFactors[$myCountedFactor] = pow($myCountedFactor,$myCountedPower);
03314       }
03315       foreach($myPoweredFactors as $myPoweredValue => $myPoweredFactor) {
03316         if (array_key_exists($myPoweredValue,$allPoweredFactors)) {
03317           if ($allPoweredFactors[$myPoweredValue] < $myPoweredFactor) {
03318             $allPoweredFactors[$myPoweredValue] = $myPoweredFactor;
03319           }
03320         } else {
03321           $allPoweredFactors[$myPoweredValue] = $myPoweredFactor;
03322         }
03323       }
03324     }
03325     foreach($allPoweredFactors as $allPoweredFactor) {
03326       $returnValue *= (integer) $allPoweredFactor;
03327     }
03328     return $returnValue;
03329   } //  function LCM()
03330 
03331 
03340   public static function GCD() {
03341     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
03342 
03343     $returnValue = 1;
03344     $allPoweredFactors = array();
03345     foreach($aArgs as $value) {
03346       if ($value == 0) {
03347         break;
03348       }
03349       $myFactors = self::_factors($value);
03350       $myCountedFactors = array_count_values($myFactors);
03351       $allValuesFactors[] = $myCountedFactors;
03352     }
03353     $allValuesCount = count($allValuesFactors);
03354     $mergedArray = $allValuesFactors[0];
03355     for ($i=1;$i < $allValuesCount; ++$i) {
03356       $mergedArray = array_intersect_key($mergedArray,$allValuesFactors[$i]);
03357     }
03358     $mergedArrayValues = count($mergedArray);
03359     if ($mergedArrayValues == 0) {
03360       return $returnValue;
03361     } elseif ($mergedArrayValues > 1) {
03362       foreach($mergedArray as $mergedKey => $mergedValue) {
03363         foreach($allValuesFactors as $highestPowerTest) {
03364           foreach($highestPowerTest as $testKey => $testValue) {
03365             if (($testKey == $mergedKey) && ($testValue < $mergedValue)) {
03366               $mergedArray[$mergedKey] = $testValue;
03367               $mergedValue = $testValue;
03368             }
03369           }
03370         }
03371       }
03372 
03373       $returnValue = 1;
03374       foreach($mergedArray as $key => $value) {
03375         $returnValue *= pow($key,$value);
03376       }
03377       return $returnValue;
03378     } else {
03379       $keys = array_keys($mergedArray);
03380       $key = $keys[0];
03381       $value = $mergedArray[$key];
03382       foreach($allValuesFactors as $testValue) {
03383         foreach($testValue as $mergedKey => $mergedValue) {
03384           if (($mergedKey == $key) && ($mergedValue < $value)) {
03385             $value = $mergedValue;
03386           }
03387         }
03388       }
03389       return pow($key,$value);
03390     }
03391   } //  function GCD()

03412   public static function BINOMDIST($value, $trials, $probability, $cumulative) {
03413     $value      = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($value));
03414     $trials     = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($trials));
03415     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
03416 
03417     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($trials)) && (is_numeric($probability))) {
03418       if (($value < 0) || ($value > $trials)) {
03419         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03420       }
03421       if (($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
03422         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03423       }
03424       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
03425         if ($cumulative) {
03426           $summer = 0;
03427           for ($i = 0; $i <= $value; ++$i) {
03428             $summer += self::COMBIN($trials,$i) * pow($probability,$i) * pow(1 - $probability,$trials - $i);
03429           }
03430           return $summer;
03431         } else {
03432           return self::COMBIN($trials,$value) * pow($probability,$value) * pow(1 - $probability,$trials - $value) ;
03433         }
03434       }
03435     }
03436     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03437   } //  function BINOMDIST()

03455   public static function NEGBINOMDIST($failures, $successes, $probability) {
03456     $failures   = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($failures));
03457     $successes    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($successes));
03458     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
03459 
03460     if ((is_numeric($failures)) && (is_numeric($successes)) && (is_numeric($probability))) {
03461       if (($failures < 0) || ($successes < 1)) {
03462         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03463       }
03464       if (($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
03465         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03466       }
03467       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
03468         if (($failures + $successes - 1) <= 0) {
03469           return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03470         }
03471       }
03472       return (self::COMBIN($failures + $successes - 1,$successes - 1)) * (pow($probability,$successes)) * (pow(1 - $probability,$failures)) ;
03473     }
03474     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03475   } //  function NEGBINOMDIST()

03477 
03497   public static function CRITBINOM($trials, $probability, $alpha) {
03498     $trials     = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($trials));
03499     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
03500     $alpha      = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
03501 
03502     if ((is_numeric($trials)) && (is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($alpha))) {
03503       if ($trials < 0) {
03504         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03505       }
03506       if (($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
03507         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03508       }
03509       if (($alpha < 0) || ($alpha > 1)) {
03510         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03511       }
03512       if ($alpha <= 0.5) {
03513         $t = sqrt(log(1 / ($alpha * $alpha)));
03514         $trialsApprox = 0 - ($t + (2.515517 + 0.802853 * $t + 0.010328 * $t * $t) / (1 + 1.432788 * $t + 0.189269 * $t * $t + 0.001308 * $t * $t * $t));
03515       } else {
03516         $t = sqrt(log(1 / pow(1 - $alpha,2)));
03517         $trialsApprox = $t - (2.515517 + 0.802853 * $t + 0.010328 * $t * $t) / (1 + 1.432788 * $t + 0.189269 * $t * $t + 0.001308 * $t * $t * $t);
03518       }
03519       $Guess = floor($trials * $probability + $trialsApprox * sqrt($trials * $probability * (1 - $probability)));
03520       if ($Guess < 0) {
03521         $Guess = 0;
03522       } elseif ($Guess > $trials) {
03523         $Guess = $trials;
03524       }
03525 
03526       $TotalUnscaledProbability = $UnscaledPGuess = $UnscaledCumPGuess = 0.0;
03527       $EssentiallyZero = 10e-12;
03528 
03529       $m = floor($trials * $probability);
03530       ++$TotalUnscaledProbability;
03531       if ($m == $Guess) { ++$UnscaledPGuess; }
03532       if ($m <= $Guess) { ++$UnscaledCumPGuess; }
03533 
03534       $PreviousValue = 1;
03535       $Done = False;
03536       $k = $m + 1;
03537       while ((!$Done) && ($k <= $trials)) {
03538         $CurrentValue = $PreviousValue * ($trials - $k + 1) * $probability / ($k * (1 - $probability));
03539         $TotalUnscaledProbability += $CurrentValue;
03540         if ($k == $Guess) { $UnscaledPGuess += $CurrentValue; }
03541         if ($k <= $Guess) { $UnscaledCumPGuess += $CurrentValue; }
03542         if ($CurrentValue <= $EssentiallyZero) { $Done = True; }
03543         $PreviousValue = $CurrentValue;
03544         ++$k;
03545       }
03546 
03547       $PreviousValue = 1;
03548       $Done = False;
03549       $k = $m - 1;
03550       while ((!$Done) && ($k >= 0)) {
03551         $CurrentValue = $PreviousValue * $k + 1 * (1 - $probability) / (($trials - $k) * $probability);
03552         $TotalUnscaledProbability += $CurrentValue;
03553         if ($k == $Guess) { $UnscaledPGuess += $CurrentValue; }
03554         if ($k <= $Guess) { $UnscaledCumPGuess += $CurrentValue; }
03555         if ($CurrentValue <= $EssentiallyZero) { $Done = True; }
03556         $PreviousValue = $CurrentValue;
03557         --$k;
03558       }
03559 
03560       $PGuess = $UnscaledPGuess / $TotalUnscaledProbability;
03561       $CumPGuess = $UnscaledCumPGuess / $TotalUnscaledProbability;
03562 
03563 //      $CumPGuessMinus1 = $CumPGuess - $PGuess;
03564       $CumPGuessMinus1 = $CumPGuess - 1;
03565 
03566       while (True) {
03567         if (($CumPGuessMinus1 < $alpha) && ($CumPGuess >= $alpha)) {
03568           return $Guess;
03569         } elseif (($CumPGuessMinus1 < $alpha) && ($CumPGuess < $alpha)) {
03570           $PGuessPlus1 = $PGuess * ($trials - $Guess) * $probability / $Guess / (1 - $probability);
03571           $CumPGuessMinus1 = $CumPGuess;
03572           $CumPGuess = $CumPGuess + $PGuessPlus1;
03573           $PGuess = $PGuessPlus1;
03574           ++$Guess;
03575         } elseif (($CumPGuessMinus1 >= $alpha) && ($CumPGuess >= $alpha)) {
03576           $PGuessMinus1 = $PGuess * $Guess * (1 - $probability) / ($trials - $Guess + 1) / $probability;
03577           $CumPGuess = $CumPGuessMinus1;
03578           $CumPGuessMinus1 = $CumPGuessMinus1 - $PGuess;
03579           $PGuess = $PGuessMinus1;
03580           --$Guess;
03581         }
03582       }
03583     }
03584     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03585   } //  function CRITBINOM()

03597   public static function CHIDIST($value, $degrees) {
03598     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
03599     $degrees  = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($degrees));
03600 
03601     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($degrees))) {
03602       if ($degrees < 1) {
03603         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03604       }
03605       if ($value < 0) {
03606         if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
03607           return 1;
03608         }
03609         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03610       }
03611       return 1 - (self::_incompleteGamma($degrees/2,$value/2) / self::_gamma($degrees/2));
03612     }
03613     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03614   } //  function CHIDIST()

03616 
03626   public static function CHIINV($probability, $degrees) {
03627     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
03628     $degrees    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($degrees));
03629 
03630     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($degrees))) {
03631 
03632       $xLo = 100;
03633       $xHi = 0;
03634 
03635       $x = $xNew = 1;
03636       $dx = 1;
03637       $i = 0;
03638 
03639       while ((abs($dx) > PRECISION) && ($i++ < MAX_ITERATIONS)) {
03640         // Apply Newton-Raphson step
03641         $result = self::CHIDIST($x, $degrees);
03642         $error = $result - $probability;
03643         if ($error == 0.0) {
03644           $dx = 0;
03645         } elseif ($error < 0.0) {
03646           $xLo = $x;
03647         } else {
03648           $xHi = $x;
03649         }
03650         // Avoid division by zero
03651         if ($result != 0.0) {
03652           $dx = $error / $result;
03653           $xNew = $x - $dx;
03654         }
03655         // If the NR fails to converge (which for example may be the
03656         // case if the initial guess is too rough) we apply a bisection
03657         // step to determine a more narrow interval around the root.
03658         if (($xNew < $xLo) || ($xNew > $xHi) || ($result == 0.0)) {
03659           $xNew = ($xLo + $xHi) / 2;
03660           $dx = $xNew - $x;
03661         }
03662         $x = $xNew;
03663       }
03664       if ($i == MAX_ITERATIONS) {
03665         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
03666       }
03667       return round($x,12);
03668     }
03669     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03670   } //  function CHIINV()

03685   public static function EXPONDIST($value, $lambda, $cumulative) {
03686     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
03687     $lambda = self::flattenSingleValue($lambda);
03688     $cumulative = self::flattenSingleValue($cumulative);
03689 
03690     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($lambda))) {
03691       if (($value < 0) || ($lambda < 0)) {
03692         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03693       }
03694       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
03695         if ($cumulative) {
03696           return 1 - exp(0-$value*$lambda);
03697         } else {
03698           return $lambda * exp(0-$value*$lambda);
03699         }
03700       }
03701     }
03702     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03703   } //  function EXPONDIST()

03716   public static function FISHER($value) {
03717     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
03718 
03719     if (is_numeric($value)) {
03720       if (($value <= -1) || ($value >= 1)) {
03721         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
03722       }
03723       return 0.5 * log((1+$value)/(1-$value));
03724     }
03725     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03726   } //  function FISHER()

03739   public static function FISHERINV($value) {
03740     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
03741 
03742     if (is_numeric($value)) {
03743       return (exp(2 * $value) - 1) / (exp(2 * $value) + 1);
03744     }
03745     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
03746   } //  function FISHERINV()

03749   // Function cache for _logBeta function
03750   private static $_logBetaCache_p     = 0.0;
03751   private static $_logBetaCache_q     = 0.0;
03752   private static $_logBetaCache_result  = 0.0;
03753 
03761   private static function _logBeta($p, $q) {
03762     if ($p != self::$_logBetaCache_p || $q != self::$_logBetaCache_q) {
03763       self::$_logBetaCache_p = $p;
03764       self::$_logBetaCache_q = $q;
03765       if (($p <= 0.0) || ($q <= 0.0) || (($p + $q) > LOG_GAMMA_X_MAX_VALUE)) {
03766         self::$_logBetaCache_result = 0.0;
03767       } else {
03768         self::$_logBetaCache_result = self::_logGamma($p) + self::_logGamma($q) - self::_logGamma($p + $q);
03769       }
03770     }
03771     return self::$_logBetaCache_result;
03772   } //  function _logBeta()

03774 
03780   private static function _betaFraction($x, $p, $q) {
03781     $c = 1.0;
03782     $sum_pq = $p + $q;
03783     $p_plus = $p + 1.0;
03784     $p_minus = $p - 1.0;
03785     $h = 1.0 - $sum_pq * $x / $p_plus;
03786     if (abs($h) < XMININ) {
03787       $h = XMININ;
03788     }
03789     $h = 1.0 / $h;
03790     $frac = $h;
03791     $m   = 1;
03792     $delta = 0.0;
03793     while ($m <= MAX_ITERATIONS && abs($delta-1.0) > PRECISION ) {
03794       $m2 = 2 * $m;
03795       // even index for d
03796       $d = $m * ($q - $m) * $x / ( ($p_minus + $m2) * ($p + $m2));
03797       $h = 1.0 + $d * $h;
03798       if (abs($h) < XMININ) {
03799         $h = XMININ;
03800       }
03801       $h = 1.0 / $h;
03802       $c = 1.0 + $d / $c;
03803       if (abs($c) < XMININ) {
03804         $c = XMININ;
03805       }
03806       $frac *= $h * $c;
03807       // odd index for d
03808       $d = -($p + $m) * ($sum_pq + $m) * $x / (($p + $m2) * ($p_plus + $m2));
03809       $h = 1.0 + $d * $h;
03810       if (abs($h) < XMININ) {
03811         $h = XMININ;
03812       }
03813       $h = 1.0 / $h;
03814       $c = 1.0 + $d / $c;
03815       if (abs($c) < XMININ) {
03816         $c = XMININ;
03817       }
03818       $delta = $h * $c;
03819       $frac *= $delta;
03820       ++$m;
03821     }
03822     return $frac;
03823   } //  function _betaFraction()

03869   // Function cache for logGamma
03870   private static $_logGammaCache_result = 0.0;
03871   private static $_logGammaCache_x    = 0.0;
03872 
03873   private static function _logGamma($x) {
03874     // Log Gamma related constants
03875     static $lg_d1 = -0.5772156649015328605195174;
03876     static $lg_d2 = 0.4227843350984671393993777;
03877     static $lg_d4 = 1.791759469228055000094023;
03878 
03879     static $lg_p1 = array(  4.945235359296727046734888,
03880                 201.8112620856775083915565,
03881                 2290.838373831346393026739,
03882                 11319.67205903380828685045,
03883                 28557.24635671635335736389,
03884                 38484.96228443793359990269,
03885                 26377.48787624195437963534,
03886                 7225.813979700288197698961 );
03887     static $lg_p2 = array(  4.974607845568932035012064,
03888                 542.4138599891070494101986,
03889                 15506.93864978364947665077,
03890                 184793.2904445632425417223,
03891                 1088204.76946882876749847,
03892                 3338152.967987029735917223,
03893                 5106661.678927352456275255,
03894                 3074109.054850539556250927 );
03895     static $lg_p4 = array(  14745.02166059939948905062,
03896                 2426813.369486704502836312,
03897                 121475557.4045093227939592,
03898                 2663432449.630976949898078,
03899                 29403789566.34553899906876,
03900                 170266573776.5398868392998,
03901                 492612579337.743088758812,
03902                 560625185622.3951465078242 );
03903 
03904     static $lg_q1 = array(  67.48212550303777196073036,
03905                 1113.332393857199323513008,
03906                 7738.757056935398733233834,
03907                 27639.87074403340708898585,
03908                 54993.10206226157329794414,
03909                 61611.22180066002127833352,
03910                 36351.27591501940507276287,
03911                 8785.536302431013170870835 );
03912     static $lg_q2 = array(  183.0328399370592604055942,
03913                 7765.049321445005871323047,
03914                 133190.3827966074194402448,
03915                 1136705.821321969608938755,
03916                 5267964.117437946917577538,
03917                 13467014.54311101692290052,
03918                 17827365.30353274213975932,
03919                 9533095.591844353613395747 );
03920     static $lg_q4 = array(  2690.530175870899333379843,
03921                 639388.5654300092398984238,
03922                 41355999.30241388052042842,
03923                 1120872109.61614794137657,
03924                 14886137286.78813811542398,
03925                 101680358627.2438228077304,
03926                 341747634550.7377132798597,
03927                 446315818741.9713286462081 );
03928 
03929     static $lg_c  = array(  -0.001910444077728,
03930                 8.4171387781295e-4,
03931                 -5.952379913043012e-4,
03932                 7.93650793500350248e-4,
03933                 -0.002777777777777681622553,
03934                 0.08333333333333333331554247,
03935                 0.0057083835261 );
03936 
03937   // Rough estimate of the fourth root of logGamma_xBig
03938   static $lg_frtbig = 2.25e76;
03939   static $pnt68  = 0.6796875;
03940 
03941 
03942   if ($x == self::$_logGammaCache_x) {
03943     return self::$_logGammaCache_result;
03944   }
03945   $y = $x;
03946   if ($y > 0.0 && $y <= LOG_GAMMA_X_MAX_VALUE) {
03947     if ($y <= EPS) {
03948       $res = -log(y);
03949     } elseif ($y <= 1.5) {
03950       // ---------------------
03951       //  EPS .LT. X .LE. 1.5
03952       // ---------------------
03953       if ($y < $pnt68) {
03954         $corr = -log($y);
03955         $xm1 = $y;
03956       } else {
03957         $corr = 0.0;
03958         $xm1 = $y - 1.0;
03959       }
03960       if ($y <= 0.5 || $y >= $pnt68) {
03961         $xden = 1.0;
03962         $xnum = 0.0;
03963         for ($i = 0; $i < 8; ++$i) {
03964           $xnum = $xnum * $xm1 + $lg_p1[$i];
03965           $xden = $xden * $xm1 + $lg_q1[$i];
03966         }
03967         $res = $corr + $xm1 * ($lg_d1 + $xm1 * ($xnum / $xden));
03968       } else {
03969         $xm2 = $y - 1.0;
03970         $xden = 1.0;
03971         $xnum = 0.0;
03972         for ($i = 0; $i < 8; ++$i) {
03973           $xnum = $xnum * $xm2 + $lg_p2[$i];
03974           $xden = $xden * $xm2 + $lg_q2[$i];
03975         }
03976         $res = $corr + $xm2 * ($lg_d2 + $xm2 * ($xnum / $xden));
03977       }
03978     } elseif ($y <= 4.0) {
03979       // ---------------------
03980       //  1.5 .LT. X .LE. 4.0
03981       // ---------------------
03982       $xm2 = $y - 2.0;
03983       $xden = 1.0;
03984       $xnum = 0.0;
03985       for ($i = 0; $i < 8; ++$i) {
03986         $xnum = $xnum * $xm2 + $lg_p2[$i];
03987         $xden = $xden * $xm2 + $lg_q2[$i];
03988       }
03989       $res = $xm2 * ($lg_d2 + $xm2 * ($xnum / $xden));
03990     } elseif ($y <= 12.0) {
03991       // ----------------------
03992       //  4.0 .LT. X .LE. 12.0
03993       // ----------------------
03994       $xm4 = $y - 4.0;
03995       $xden = -1.0;
03996       $xnum = 0.0;
03997       for ($i = 0; $i < 8; ++$i) {
03998         $xnum = $xnum * $xm4 + $lg_p4[$i];
03999         $xden = $xden * $xm4 + $lg_q4[$i];
04000       }
04001       $res = $lg_d4 + $xm4 * ($xnum / $xden);
04002     } else {
04003       // ---------------------------------
04004       //  Evaluate for argument .GE. 12.0
04005       // ---------------------------------
04006       $res = 0.0;
04007       if ($y <= $lg_frtbig) {
04008         $res = $lg_c[6];
04009         $ysq = $y * $y;
04010         for ($i = 0; $i < 6; ++$i)
04011           $res = $res / $ysq + $lg_c[$i];
04012         }
04013         $res /= $y;
04014         $corr = log($y);
04015         $res = $res + log(SQRT2PI) - 0.5 * $corr;
04016         $res += $y * ($corr - 1.0);
04017       }
04018     } else {
04019       // --------------------------
04020       //  Return for bad arguments
04021       // --------------------------
04022       $res = MAX_VALUE;
04023     }
04024     // ------------------------------
04025     //  Final adjustments and return
04026     // ------------------------------
04027     self::$_logGammaCache_x = $x;
04028     self::$_logGammaCache_result = $res;
04029     return $res;
04030   } //  function _logGamma()
04031 
04032 
04042   private static function _beta($p, $q) {
04043     if ($p <= 0.0 || $q <= 0.0 || ($p + $q) > LOG_GAMMA_X_MAX_VALUE) {
04044       return 0.0;
04045     } else {
04046       return exp(self::_logBeta($p, $q));
04047     }
04048   } //  function _beta()
04049 
04050 
04063   private static function _incompleteBeta($x, $p, $q) {
04064     if ($x <= 0.0) {
04065       return 0.0;
04066     } elseif ($x >= 1.0) {
04067       return 1.0;
04068     } elseif (($p <= 0.0) || ($q <= 0.0) || (($p + $q) > LOG_GAMMA_X_MAX_VALUE)) {
04069       return 0.0;
04070     }
04071     $beta_gam = exp((0 - self::_logBeta($p, $q)) + $p * log($x) + $q * log(1.0 - $x));
04072     if ($x < ($p + 1.0) / ($p + $q + 2.0)) {
04073       return $beta_gam * self::_betaFraction($x, $p, $q) / $p;
04074     } else {
04075       return 1.0 - ($beta_gam * self::_betaFraction(1 - $x, $q, $p) / $q);
04076     }
04077   } //  function _incompleteBeta()
04078 
04079 
04092   public static function BETADIST($value,$alpha,$beta,$rMin=0,$rMax=1) {
04093     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04094     $alpha  = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
04095     $beta = self::flattenSingleValue($beta);
04096     $rMin = self::flattenSingleValue($rMin);
04097     $rMax = self::flattenSingleValue($rMax);
04098 
04099     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($alpha)) && (is_numeric($beta)) && (is_numeric($rMin)) && (is_numeric($rMax))) {
04100       if (($value < $rMin) || ($value > $rMax) || ($alpha <= 0) || ($beta <= 0) || ($rMin == $rMax)) {
04101         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04102       }
04103       if ($rMin > $rMax) {
04104         $tmp = $rMin;
04105         $rMin = $rMax;
04106         $rMax = $tmp;
04107       }
04108       $value -= $rMin;
04109       $value /= ($rMax - $rMin);
04110       return self::_incompleteBeta($value,$alpha,$beta);
04111     }
04112     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04113   } //  function BETADIST()
04114 
04115 
04128   public static function BETAINV($probability,$alpha,$beta,$rMin=0,$rMax=1) {
04129     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
04130     $alpha      = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
04131     $beta     = self::flattenSingleValue($beta);
04132     $rMin     = self::flattenSingleValue($rMin);
04133     $rMax     = self::flattenSingleValue($rMax);
04134 
04135     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($alpha)) && (is_numeric($beta)) && (is_numeric($rMin)) && (is_numeric($rMax))) {
04136       if (($alpha <= 0) || ($beta <= 0) || ($rMin == $rMax) || ($probability <= 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
04137         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04138       }
04139       if ($rMin > $rMax) {
04140         $tmp = $rMin;
04141         $rMin = $rMax;
04142         $rMax = $tmp;
04143       }
04144       $a = 0;
04145       $b = 2;
04146 
04147       $i = 0;
04148       while ((($b - $a) > PRECISION) && ($i++ < MAX_ITERATIONS)) {
04149         $guess = ($a + $b) / 2;
04150         $result = self::BETADIST($guess, $alpha, $beta);
04151         if (($result == $probability) || ($result == 0)) {
04152           $b = $a;
04153         } elseif ($result > $probability) {
04154           $b = $guess;
04155         } else {
04156           $a = $guess;
04157         }
04158       }
04159       if ($i == MAX_ITERATIONS) {
04160         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
04161       }
04162       return round($rMin + $guess * ($rMax - $rMin),12);
04163     }
04164     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04165   } //  function BETAINV()
04166 
04167 
04168   //
04169   //  Private implementation of the incomplete Gamma function
04170   //
04171   private static function _incompleteGamma($a,$x) {
04172     static $max = 32;
04173     $summer = 0;
04174     for ($n=0; $n<=$max; ++$n) {
04175       $divisor = $a;
04176       for ($i=1; $i<=$n; ++$i) {
04177         $divisor *= ($a + $i);
04178       }
04179       $summer += (pow($x,$n) / $divisor);
04180     }
04181     return pow($x,$a) * exp(0-$x) * $summer;
04182   } //  function _incompleteGamma()
04183 
04184 
04185   //
04186   //  Private implementation of the Gamma function
04187   //
04188   private static function _gamma($data) {
04189     if ($data == 0.0) return 0;
04190 
04191     static $p0 = 1.000000000190015;
04192     static $p = array ( 1 => 76.18009172947146,
04193               2 => -86.50532032941677,
04194               3 => 24.01409824083091,
04195               4 => -1.231739572450155,
04196               5 => 1.208650973866179e-3,
04197               6 => -5.395239384953e-6
04198               );
04199 
04200     $y = $x = $data;
04201     $tmp = $x + 5.5;
04202     $tmp -= ($x + 0.5) * log($tmp);
04203 
04204     $summer = $p0;
04205     for ($j=1;$j<=6;++$j) {
04206       $summer += ($p[$j] / ++$y);
04207     }
04208     return exp(0 - $tmp + log(SQRT2PI * $summer / $x));
04209   } //  function _gamma()
04210 
04211 
04224   public static function GAMMADIST($value,$a,$b,$cumulative) {
04225     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04226     $a    = self::flattenSingleValue($a);
04227     $b    = self::flattenSingleValue($b);
04228 
04229     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($a)) && (is_numeric($b))) {
04230       if (($value < 0) || ($a <= 0) || ($b <= 0)) {
04231         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04232       }
04233       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
04234         if ($cumulative) {
04235           return self::_incompleteGamma($a,$value / $b) / self::_gamma($a);
04236         } else {
04237           return (1 / (pow($b,$a) * self::_gamma($a))) * pow($value,$a-1) * exp(0-($value / $b));
04238         }
04239       }
04240     }
04241     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04242   } //  function GAMMADIST()
04243 
04244 
04256   public static function GAMMAINV($probability,$alpha,$beta) {
04257     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
04258     $alpha      = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
04259     $beta     = self::flattenSingleValue($beta);
04260 
04261     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($alpha)) && (is_numeric($beta))) {
04262       if (($alpha <= 0) || ($beta <= 0) || ($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
04263         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04264       }
04265 
04266       $xLo = 0;
04267       $xHi = $alpha * $beta * 5;
04268 
04269       $x = $xNew = 1;
04270       $error = $pdf = 0;
04271       $dx = 1024;
04272       $i = 0;
04273 
04274       while ((abs($dx) > PRECISION) && ($i++ < MAX_ITERATIONS)) {
04275         // Apply Newton-Raphson step
04276         $error = self::GAMMADIST($x, $alpha, $beta, True) - $probability;
04277         if ($error < 0.0) {
04278           $xLo = $x;
04279         } else {
04280           $xHi = $x;
04281         }
04282         $pdf = self::GAMMADIST($x, $alpha, $beta, False);
04283         // Avoid division by zero
04284         if ($pdf != 0.0) {
04285           $dx = $error / $pdf;
04286           $xNew = $x - $dx;
04287         }
04288         // If the NR fails to converge (which for example may be the
04289         // case if the initial guess is too rough) we apply a bisection
04290         // step to determine a more narrow interval around the root.
04291         if (($xNew < $xLo) || ($xNew > $xHi) || ($pdf == 0.0)) {
04292           $xNew = ($xLo + $xHi) / 2;
04293           $dx = $xNew - $x;
04294         }
04295         $x = $xNew;
04296       }
04297       if ($i == MAX_ITERATIONS) {
04298         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
04299       }
04300       return $x;
04301     }
04302     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04303   } //  function GAMMAINV()
04304 
04305 
04314   public static function GAMMALN($value) {
04315     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04316 
04317     if (is_numeric($value)) {
04318       if ($value <= 0) {
04319         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04320       }
04321       return log(self::_gamma($value));
04322     }
04323     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04324   } //  function GAMMALN()

04341   public static function NORMDIST($value, $mean, $stdDev, $cumulative) {
04342     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04343     $mean = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
04344     $stdDev = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
04345 
04346     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($mean)) && (is_numeric($stdDev))) {
04347       if ($stdDev < 0) {
04348         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04349       }
04350       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
04351         if ($cumulative) {
04352           return 0.5 * (1 + self::_erfVal(($value - $mean) / ($stdDev * sqrt(2))));
04353         } else {
04354           return (1 / (SQRT2PI * $stdDev)) * exp(0 - (pow($value - $mean,2) / (2 * ($stdDev * $stdDev))));
04355         }
04356       }
04357     }
04358     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04359   } //  function NORMDIST()
04360 
04361 
04372   public static function NORMSDIST($value) {
04373     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04374 
04375     return self::NORMDIST($value, 0, 1, True);
04376   } //  function NORMSDIST()
04377

04388   public static function LOGNORMDIST($value, $mean, $stdDev) {
04389     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04390     $mean = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
04391     $stdDev = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
04392 
04393     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($mean)) && (is_numeric($stdDev))) {
04394       if (($value <= 0) || ($stdDev <= 0)) {
04395         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04396       }
04397       return self::NORMSDIST((log($value) - $mean) / $stdDev);
04398     }
04399     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04400   } //  function LOGNORMDIST()
