04402 
04403   /***************************************************************************
04404    *                inverse_ncdf.php
04405    *              -------------------
04406    *  begin       : Friday, January 16, 2004
04407    *  copyright     : (C) 2004 Michael Nickerson
04408    *  email       : nickersonm@yahoo.com
04409    *
04410    ***************************************************************************/
04411   private static function _inverse_ncdf($p) {
04412     //  Inverse ncdf approximation by Peter J. Acklam, implementation adapted to
04413     //  PHP by Michael Nickerson, using Dr. Thomas Ziegler's C implementation as
04414     //  a guide. http://home.online.no/~pjacklam/notes/invnorm/index.html
04415     //  I have not checked the accuracy of this implementation. Be aware that PHP
04416     //  will truncate the coeficcients to 14 digits.
04417 
04418     //  You have permission to use and distribute this function freely for
04419     //  whatever purpose you want, but please show common courtesy and give credit
04420     //  where credit is due.
04421 
04422     //  Input paramater is $p - probability - where 0 < p < 1.
04423 
04424     //  Coefficients in rational approximations
04425     static $a = array(  1 => -3.969683028665376e+01,
04426               2 => 2.209460984245205e+02,
04427               3 => -2.759285104469687e+02,
04428               4 => 1.383577518672690e+02,
04429               5 => -3.066479806614716e+01,
04430               6 => 2.506628277459239e+00
04431              );
04432 
04433     static $b = array(  1 => -5.447609879822406e+01,
04434               2 => 1.615858368580409e+02,
04435               3 => -1.556989798598866e+02,
04436               4 => 6.680131188771972e+01,
04437               5 => -1.328068155288572e+01
04438              );
04439 
04440     static $c = array(  1 => -7.784894002430293e-03,
04441               2 => -3.223964580411365e-01,
04442               3 => -2.400758277161838e+00,
04443               4 => -2.549732539343734e+00,
04444               5 => 4.374664141464968e+00,
04445               6 => 2.938163982698783e+00
04446              );
04447 
04448     static $d = array(  1 => 7.784695709041462e-03,
04449               2 => 3.224671290700398e-01,
04450               3 => 2.445134137142996e+00,
04451               4 => 3.754408661907416e+00
04452              );
04453 
04454     //  Define lower and upper region break-points.
04455     $p_low = 0.02425;     //Use lower region approx. below this
04456     $p_high = 1 - $p_low;   //Use upper region approx. above this
04457 
04458     if (0 < $p && $p < $p_low) {
04459       //  Rational approximation for lower region.
04460       $q = sqrt(-2 * log($p));
04461       return ((((($c[1] * $q + $c[2]) * $q + $c[3]) * $q + $c[4]) * $q + $c[5]) * $q + $c[6]) /
04462           (((($d[1] * $q + $d[2]) * $q + $d[3]) * $q + $d[4]) * $q + 1);
04463     } elseif ($p_low <= $p && $p <= $p_high) {
04464       //  Rational approximation for central region.
04465       $q = $p - 0.5;
04466       $r = $q * $q;
04467       return ((((($a[1] * $r + $a[2]) * $r + $a[3]) * $r + $a[4]) * $r + $a[5]) * $r + $a[6]) * $q /
04468            ((((($b[1] * $r + $b[2]) * $r + $b[3]) * $r + $b[4]) * $r + $b[5]) * $r + 1);
04469     } elseif ($p_high < $p && $p < 1) {
04470       //  Rational approximation for upper region.
04471       $q = sqrt(-2 * log(1 - $p));
04472       return -((((($c[1] * $q + $c[2]) * $q + $c[3]) * $q + $c[4]) * $q + $c[5]) * $q + $c[6]) /
04473            (((($d[1] * $q + $d[2]) * $q + $d[3]) * $q + $d[4]) * $q + 1);
04474     }
04475     //  If 0 < p < 1, return a null value
04476     return self::$_errorCodes['null'];
04477   } //  function _inverse_ncdf()
04478 
04479 
04480   private static function _inverse_ncdf2($prob) {
04481     //  Approximation of inverse standard normal CDF developed by
04482     //  B. Moro, "The Full Monte," Risk 8(2), Feb 1995, 57-58.
04483 
04484     $a1 = 2.50662823884;
04485     $a2 = -18.61500062529;
04486     $a3 = 41.39119773534;
04487     $a4 = -25.44106049637;
04488 
04489     $b1 = -8.4735109309;
04490     $b2 = 23.08336743743;
04491     $b3 = -21.06224101826;
04492     $b4 = 3.13082909833;
04493 
04494     $c1 = 0.337475482272615;
04495     $c2 = 0.976169019091719;
04496     $c3 = 0.160797971491821;
04497     $c4 = 2.76438810333863E-02;
04498     $c5 = 3.8405729373609E-03;
04499     $c6 = 3.951896511919E-04;
04500     $c7 = 3.21767881768E-05;
04501     $c8 = 2.888167364E-07;
04502     $c9 = 3.960315187E-07;
04503 
04504     $y = $prob - 0.5;
04505     if (abs($y) < 0.42) {
04506       $z = ($y * $y);
04507       $z = $y * ((($a4 * $z + $a3) * $z + $a2) * $z + $a1) / (((($b4 * $z + $b3) * $z + $b2) * $z + $b1) * $z + 1);
04508     } else {
04509       if ($y > 0) {
04510         $z = log(-log(1 - $prob));
04511       } else {
04512         $z = log(-log($prob));
04513       }
04514       $z = $c1 + $z * ($c2 + $z * ($c3 + $z * ($c4 + $z * ($c5 + $z * ($c6 + $z * ($c7 + $z * ($c8 + $z * $c9)))))));
04515       if ($y < 0) {
04516         $z = -$z;
04517       }
04518     }
04519     return $z;
04520   } //  function _inverse_ncdf2()
04521 
04522 
04523   private static function _inverse_ncdf3($p) {
04524     //  ALGORITHM AS241 APPL. STATIST. (1988) VOL. 37, NO. 3.
04525     //  Produces the normal deviate Z corresponding to a given lower
04526     //  tail area of P; Z is accurate to about 1 part in 10**16.
04527     //
04528     //  This is a PHP version of the original FORTRAN code that can
04529     //  be found at http://lib.stat.cmu.edu/apstat/
04530     $split1 = 0.425;
04531     $split2 = 5;
04532     $const1 = 0.180625;
04533     $const2 = 1.6;
04534 
04535     //  coefficients for p close to 0.5
04536     $a0 = 3.3871328727963666080;
04537     $a1 = 1.3314166789178437745E+2;
04538     $a2 = 1.9715909503065514427E+3;
04539     $a3 = 1.3731693765509461125E+4;
04540     $a4 = 4.5921953931549871457E+4;
04541     $a5 = 6.7265770927008700853E+4;
04542     $a6 = 3.3430575583588128105E+4;
04543     $a7 = 2.5090809287301226727E+3;
04544 
04545     $b1 = 4.2313330701600911252E+1;
04546     $b2 = 6.8718700749205790830E+2;
04547     $b3 = 5.3941960214247511077E+3;
04548     $b4 = 2.1213794301586595867E+4;
04549     $b5 = 3.9307895800092710610E+4;
04550     $b6 = 2.8729085735721942674E+4;
04551     $b7 = 5.2264952788528545610E+3;
04552 
04553     //  coefficients for p not close to 0, 0.5 or 1.
04554     $c0 = 1.42343711074968357734;
04555     $c1 = 4.63033784615654529590;
04556     $c2 = 5.76949722146069140550;
04557     $c3 = 3.64784832476320460504;
04558     $c4 = 1.27045825245236838258;
04559     $c5 = 2.41780725177450611770E-1;
04560     $c6 = 2.27238449892691845833E-2;
04561     $c7 = 7.74545014278341407640E-4;
04562 
04563     $d1 = 2.05319162663775882187;
04564     $d2 = 1.67638483018380384940;
04565     $d3 = 6.89767334985100004550E-1;
04566     $d4 = 1.48103976427480074590E-1;
04567     $d5 = 1.51986665636164571966E-2;
04568     $d6 = 5.47593808499534494600E-4;
04569     $d7 = 1.05075007164441684324E-9;
04570 
04571     //  coefficients for p near 0 or 1.
04572     $e0 = 6.65790464350110377720;
04573     $e1 = 5.46378491116411436990;
04574     $e2 = 1.78482653991729133580;
04575     $e3 = 2.96560571828504891230E-1;
04576     $e4 = 2.65321895265761230930E-2;
04577     $e5 = 1.24266094738807843860E-3;
04578     $e6 = 2.71155556874348757815E-5;
04579     $e7 = 2.01033439929228813265E-7;
04580 
04581     $f1 = 5.99832206555887937690E-1;
04582     $f2 = 1.36929880922735805310E-1;
04583     $f3 = 1.48753612908506148525E-2;
04584     $f4 = 7.86869131145613259100E-4;
04585     $f5 = 1.84631831751005468180E-5;
04586     $f6 = 1.42151175831644588870E-7;
04587     $f7 = 2.04426310338993978564E-15;
04588 
04589     $q = $p - 0.5;
04590 
04591     //  computation for p close to 0.5
04592     if (abs($q) <= split1) {
04593       $R = $const1 - $q * $q;
04594       $z = $q * ((((((($a7 * $R + $a6) * $R + $a5) * $R + $a4) * $R + $a3) * $R + $a2) * $R + $a1) * $R + $a0) /
04595             ((((((($b7 * $R + $b6) * $R + $b5) * $R + $b4) * $R + $b3) * $R + $b2) * $R + $b1) * $R + 1);
04596     } else {
04597       if ($q < 0) {
04598         $R = $p;
04599       } else {
04600         $R = 1 - $p;
04601       }
04602       $R = pow(-log($R),2);
04603 
04604       //  computation for p not close to 0, 0.5 or 1.
04605       If ($R <= $split2) {
04606         $R = $R - $const2;
04607         $z = ((((((($c7 * $R + $c6) * $R + $c5) * $R + $c4) * $R + $c3) * $R + $c2) * $R + $c1) * $R + $c0) /
04608            ((((((($d7 * $R + $d6) * $R + $d5) * $R + $d4) * $R + $d3) * $R + $d2) * $R + $d1) * $R + 1);
04609       } else {
04610       //  computation for p near 0 or 1.
04611         $R = $R - $split2;
04612         $z = ((((((($e7 * $R + $e6) * $R + $e5) * $R + $e4) * $R + $e3) * $R + $e2) * $R + $e1) * $R + $e0) /
04613            ((((((($f7 * $R + $f6) * $R + $f5) * $R + $f4) * $R + $f3) * $R + $f2) * $R + $f1) * $R + 1);
04614       }
04615       if ($q < 0) {
04616         $z = -$z;
04617       }
04618     }
04619     return $z;
04620   } //  function _inverse_ncdf3()
04621

04634   public static function NORMINV($probability,$mean,$stdDev) {
04635     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
04636     $mean     = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
04637     $stdDev     = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
04638 
04639     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($mean)) && (is_numeric($stdDev))) {
04640       if (($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1)) {
04641         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04642       }
04643       if ($stdDev < 0) {
04644         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04645       }
04646       return (self::_inverse_ncdf($probability) * $stdDev) + $mean;
04647     }
04648     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04649   } //  function NORMINV()

04660   public static function NORMSINV($value) {
04661     return self::NORMINV($value, 0, 1);
04662   } //  function NORMSINV()

04677   public static function LOGINV($probability, $mean, $stdDev) {
04678     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
04679     $mean     = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
04680     $stdDev     = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
04681 
04682     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($mean)) && (is_numeric($stdDev))) {
04683       if (($probability < 0) || ($probability > 1) || ($stdDev <= 0)) {
04684         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04685       }
04686       return exp($mean + $stdDev * self::NORMSINV($probability));
04687     }
04688     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04689   } //  function LOGINV()

04705   public static function HYPGEOMDIST($sampleSuccesses, $sampleNumber, $populationSuccesses, $populationNumber) {
04706     $sampleSuccesses    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($sampleSuccesses));
04707     $sampleNumber     = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($sampleNumber));
04708     $populationSuccesses  = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($populationSuccesses));
04709     $populationNumber   = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($populationNumber));
04710 
04711     if ((is_numeric($sampleSuccesses)) && (is_numeric($sampleNumber)) && (is_numeric($populationSuccesses)) && (is_numeric($populationNumber))) {
04712       if (($sampleSuccesses < 0) || ($sampleSuccesses > $sampleNumber) || ($sampleSuccesses > $populationSuccesses)) {
04713         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04714       }
04715       if (($sampleNumber <= 0) || ($sampleNumber > $populationNumber)) {
04716         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04717       }
04718       if (($populationSuccesses <= 0) || ($populationSuccesses > $populationNumber)) {
04719         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04720       }
04721       return self::COMBIN($populationSuccesses,$sampleSuccesses) *
04722            self::COMBIN($populationNumber - $populationSuccesses,$sampleNumber - $sampleSuccesses) /
04723            self::COMBIN($populationNumber,$sampleNumber);
04724     }
04725     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04726   } //  function HYPGEOMDIST()

04728 
04739   public static function TDIST($value, $degrees, $tails) {
04740     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04741     $degrees  = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($degrees));
04742     $tails    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($tails));
04743 
04744     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($degrees)) && (is_numeric($tails))) {
04745       if (($value < 0) || ($degrees < 1) || ($tails < 1) || ($tails > 2)) {
04746         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04747       }
04748       //  tdist, which finds the probability that corresponds to a given value
04749       //  of t with k degrees of freedom. This algorithm is translated from a
04750       //  pascal function on p81 of "Statistical Computing in Pascal" by D
04751       //  Cooke, A H Craven & G M Clark (1985: Edward Arnold (Pubs.) Ltd:
04752       //  London). The above Pascal algorithm is itself a translation of the
04753       //  fortran algoritm "AS 3" by B E Cooper of the Atlas Computer
04754       //  Laboratory as reported in (among other places) "Applied Statistics
04755       //  Algorithms", editied by P Griffiths and I D Hill (1985; Ellis
04756       //  Horwood Ltd.; W. Sussex, England).
04757       $tterm = $degrees;
04758       $ttheta = atan2($value,sqrt($tterm));
04759       $tc = cos($ttheta);
04760       $ts = sin($ttheta);
04761       $tsum = 0;
04762 
04763       if (($degrees % 2) == 1) {
04764         $ti = 3;
04765         $tterm = $tc;
04766       } else {
04767         $ti = 2;
04768         $tterm = 1;
04769       }
04770 
04771       $tsum = $tterm;
04772       while ($ti < $degrees) {
04773         $tterm *= $tc * $tc * ($ti - 1) / $ti;
04774         $tsum += $tterm;
04775         $ti += 2;
04776       }
04777       $tsum *= $ts;
04778       if (($degrees % 2) == 1) { $tsum = M_2DIVPI * ($tsum + $ttheta); }
04779       $tValue = 0.5 * (1 + $tsum);
04780       if ($tails == 1) {
04781         return 1 - abs($tValue);
04782       } else {
04783         return 1 - abs((1 - $tValue) - $tValue);
04784       }
04785     }
04786     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04787   } //  function TDIST()
04788 
04789 
04799   public static function TINV($probability, $degrees) {
04800     $probability  = self::flattenSingleValue($probability);
04801     $degrees    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($degrees));
04802 
04803     if ((is_numeric($probability)) && (is_numeric($degrees))) {
04804       $xLo = 100;
04805       $xHi = 0;
04806 
04807       $x = $xNew = 1;
04808       $dx = 1;
04809       $i = 0;
04810 
04811       while ((abs($dx) > PRECISION) && ($i++ < MAX_ITERATIONS)) {
04812         // Apply Newton-Raphson step
04813         $result = self::TDIST($x, $degrees, 2);
04814         $error = $result - $probability;
04815         if ($error == 0.0) {
04816           $dx = 0;
04817         } elseif ($error < 0.0) {
04818           $xLo = $x;
04819         } else {
04820           $xHi = $x;
04821         }
04822         // Avoid division by zero
04823         if ($result != 0.0) {
04824           $dx = $error / $result;
04825           $xNew = $x - $dx;
04826         }
04827         // If the NR fails to converge (which for example may be the
04828         // case if the initial guess is too rough) we apply a bisection
04829         // step to determine a more narrow interval around the root.
04830         if (($xNew < $xLo) || ($xNew > $xHi) || ($result == 0.0)) {
04831           $xNew = ($xLo + $xHi) / 2;
04832           $dx = $xNew - $x;
04833         }
04834         $x = $xNew;
04835       }
04836       if ($i == MAX_ITERATIONS) {
04837         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
04838       }
04839       return round($x,12);
04840     }
04841     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04842   } //  function TINV()
04843 
04844 
04856   public static function CONFIDENCE($alpha,$stdDev,$size) {
04857     $alpha  = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
04858     $stdDev = self::flattenSingleValue($stdDev);
04859     $size = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($size));
04860 
04861     if ((is_numeric($alpha)) && (is_numeric($stdDev)) && (is_numeric($size))) {
04862       if (($alpha <= 0) || ($alpha >= 1)) {
04863         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04864       }
04865       if (($stdDev <= 0) || ($size < 1)) {
04866         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04867       }
04868       return self::NORMSINV(1 - $alpha / 2) * $stdDev / sqrt($size);
04869     }
04870     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04871   } //  function CONFIDENCE()

04873 
04887   public static function POISSON($value, $mean, $cumulative) {
04888     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04889     $mean = self::flattenSingleValue($mean);
04890 
04891     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($mean))) {
04892       if (($value <= 0) || ($mean <= 0)) {
04893         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04894       }
04895       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
04896         if ($cumulative) {
04897           $summer = 0;
04898           for ($i = 0; $i <= floor($value); ++$i) {
04899             $summer += pow($mean,$i) / self::FACT($i);
04900           }
04901           return exp(0-$mean) * $summer;
04902         } else {
04903           return (exp(0-$mean) * pow($mean,$value)) / self::FACT($value);
04904         }
04905       }
04906     }
04907     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04908   } //  function POISSON()

04924   public static function WEIBULL($value, $alpha, $beta, $cumulative) {
04925     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
04926     $alpha  = self::flattenSingleValue($alpha);
04927     $beta = self::flattenSingleValue($beta);
04928 
04929     if ((is_numeric($value)) && (is_numeric($alpha)) && (is_numeric($beta))) {
04930       if (($value < 0) || ($alpha <= 0) || ($beta <= 0)) {
04931         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
04932       }
04933       if ((is_numeric($cumulative)) || (is_bool($cumulative))) {
04934         if ($cumulative) {
04935           return 1 - exp(0 - pow($value / $beta,$alpha));
04936         } else {
04937           return ($alpha / pow($beta,$alpha)) * pow($value,$alpha - 1) * exp(0 - pow($value / $beta,$alpha));
04938         }
04939       }
04940     }
04941     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
04942   } //  function WEIBULL()

04958   public static function ZTEST($dataSet, $m0, $sigma=null) {
04959     $dataSet  = self::flattenArrayIndexed($dataSet);
04960     $m0     = self::flattenSingleValue($m0);
04961     $sigma    = self::flattenSingleValue($sigma);
04962 
04963     if (is_null($sigma)) {
04964       $sigma = self::STDEV($dataSet);
04965     }
04966     $n = count($dataSet);
04967 
04968     return 1 - self::NORMSDIST((self::AVERAGE($dataSet) - $m0)/($sigma/SQRT($n)));
04969   } //  function ZTEST()

04983   public static function SKEW() {
04984     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
04985     $mean = self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
04986     $stdDev = self::STDEV($aArgs);
04987 
04988     $count = $summer = 0;
04989     // Loop through arguments
04990     foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
04991       if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
04992         (!self::isMatrixValue($k))) {
04993       } else {
04994         // Is it a numeric value?
04995         if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
04996           $summer += pow((($arg - $mean) / $stdDev),3) ;
04997           ++$count;
04998         }
04999       }
05000     }
05001 
05002     // Return
05003     if ($count > 2) {
05004       return $summer * ($count / (($count-1) * ($count-2)));
05005     }
05006     return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
05007   } //  function SKEW()
05008 
05009 
05021   public static function KURT() {
05022     $aArgs = self::flattenArrayIndexed(func_get_args());
05023     $mean = self::AVERAGE($aArgs);
05024     $stdDev = self::STDEV($aArgs);
05025 
05026     if ($stdDev > 0) {
05027       $count = $summer = 0;
05028       // Loop through arguments
05029       foreach ($aArgs as $k => $arg) {
05030         if ((is_bool($arg)) &&
05031           (!self::isMatrixValue($k))) {
05032         } else {
05033           // Is it a numeric value?
05034           if ((is_numeric($arg)) && (!is_string($arg))) {
05035             $summer += pow((($arg - $mean) / $stdDev),4) ;
05036             ++$count;
05037           }
05038         }
05039       }
05040 
05041       // Return
05042       if ($count > 3) {
05043         return $summer * ($count * ($count+1) / (($count-1) * ($count-2) * ($count-3))) - (3 * pow($count-1,2) / (($count-2) * ($count-3)));
05044       }
05045     }
05046     return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
05047   } //  function KURT()

05057   public static function RAND($min = 0, $max = 0) {
05058     $min    = self::flattenSingleValue($min);
05059     $max    = self::flattenSingleValue($max);
05060 
05061     if ($min == 0 && $max == 0) {
05062       return (rand(0,10000000)) / 10000000;
05063     } else {
05064       return rand($min, $max);
05065     }
05066   } //  function RAND()

05076   public static function MOD($a = 1, $b = 1) {
05077     $a    = self::flattenSingleValue($a);
05078     $b    = self::flattenSingleValue($b);
05079 
05080     if ($b == 0.0) {
05081       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
05082     } elseif (($a < 0.0) && ($b > 0.0)) {
05083       return $b - fmod(abs($a),$b);
05084     } elseif (($a > 0.0) && ($b < 0.0)) {
05085       return $b + fmod($a,abs($b));
05086     }
05087 
05088     return fmod($a,$b);
05089   } //  function MOD()

05098   public static function CHARACTER($character) {
05099     $character  = self::flattenSingleValue($character);
05100 
05101     if ((!is_numeric($character)) || ($character < 0)) {
05102       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05103     }
05104 
05105     if (function_exists('mb_convert_encoding')) {
05106       return mb_convert_encoding('&#'.intval($character).';', 'UTF-8', 'HTML-ENTITIES');
05107     } else {
05108       return chr(intval($character));
05109     }
05110   }

05113   private static function _uniord($c) {
05114     if (ord($c{0}) >=0 && ord($c{0}) <= 127)
05115       return ord($c{0});
05116     if (ord($c{0}) >= 192 && ord($c{0}) <= 223)
05117       return (ord($c{0})-192)*64 + (ord($c{1})-128);
05118     if (ord($c{0}) >= 224 && ord($c{0}) <= 239)
05119       return (ord($c{0})-224)*4096 + (ord($c{1})-128)*64 + (ord($c{2})-128);
05120     if (ord($c{0}) >= 240 && ord($c{0}) <= 247)
05121       return (ord($c{0})-240)*262144 + (ord($c{1})-128)*4096 + (ord($c{2})-128)*64 + (ord($c{3})-128);
05122     if (ord($c{0}) >= 248 && ord($c{0}) <= 251)
05123       return (ord($c{0})-248)*16777216 + (ord($c{1})-128)*262144 + (ord($c{2})-128)*4096 + (ord($c{3})-128)*64 + (ord($c{4})-128);
05124     if (ord($c{0}) >= 252 && ord($c{0}) <= 253)
05125       return (ord($c{0})-252)*1073741824 + (ord($c{1})-128)*16777216 + (ord($c{2})-128)*262144 + (ord($c{3})-128)*4096 + (ord($c{4})-128)*64 + (ord($c{5})-128);
05126     if (ord($c{0}) >= 254 && ord($c{0}) <= 255) //error
05127       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05128     return 0;
05129   } //  function _uniord()
05130 
05137   public static function ASCIICODE($characters) {
05138     $characters = self::flattenSingleValue($characters);
05139     if (is_bool($characters)) {
05140       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
05141         $characters = (int) $characters;
05142       } else {
05143         if ($characters) {
05144           $characters = 'True';
05145         } else {
05146           $characters = 'False';
05147         }
05148       }
05149     }
05150 
05151     $character = $characters;
05152     if ((function_exists('mb_strlen')) && (function_exists('mb_substr'))) {
05153       if (mb_strlen($characters, 'UTF-8') > 1) { $character = mb_substr($characters, 0, 1, 'UTF-8'); }
05154       return self::_uniord($character);
05155     } else {
05156       if (strlen($characters) > 0) { $character = substr($characters, 0, 1); }
05157       return ord($character);
05158     }
05159   } //  function ASCIICODE()

05167   public static function CONCATENATE() {
05168     // Return value
05169     $returnValue = '';
05170 
05171     // Loop through arguments
05172     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
05173     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
05174       if (is_bool($arg)) {
05175         if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
05176           $arg = (int) $arg;
05177         } else {
05178           if ($arg) {
05179             $arg = 'TRUE';
05180           } else {
05181             $arg = 'FALSE';
05182           }
05183         }
05184       }
05185       $returnValue .= $arg;
05186     }
05187 
05188     // Return
05189     return $returnValue;
05190   } //  function CONCATENATE()

05200   public static function STRINGLENGTH($value = '') {
05201     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
05202 
05203     if (is_bool($value)) {
05204       $value = ($value) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05205     }
05206 
05207     if (function_exists('mb_strlen')) {
05208       return mb_strlen($value, 'UTF-8');
05209     } else {
05210       return strlen($value);
05211     }

05214 
05223   public static function SEARCHSENSITIVE($needle,$haystack,$offset=1) {
05224     $needle   = self::flattenSingleValue($needle);
05225     $haystack = self::flattenSingleValue($haystack);
05226     $offset   = self::flattenSingleValue($offset);
05227 
05228     if (!is_bool($needle)) {
05229       if (is_bool($haystack)) {
05230         $haystack = ($haystack) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05231       }
05232 
05233       if (($offset > 0) && (strlen($haystack) > $offset)) {
05234         if (function_exists('mb_strpos')) {
05235           $pos = mb_strpos($haystack, $needle, --$offset,'UTF-8');
05236         } else {
05237           $pos = strpos($haystack, $needle, --$offset);
05238         }
05239         if ($pos !== false) {
05240           return ++$pos;
05241         }
05242       }
05243     }
05244     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05245   } //  function SEARCHSENSITIVE()
05246 
05247 
05256   public static function SEARCHINSENSITIVE($needle,$haystack,$offset=1) {
05257     $needle   = self::flattenSingleValue($needle);
05258     $haystack = self::flattenSingleValue($haystack);
05259     $offset   = self::flattenSingleValue($offset);
05260 
05261     if (!is_bool($needle)) {
05262       if (is_bool($haystack)) {
05263         $haystack = ($haystack) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05264       }
05265 
05266       if (($offset > 0) && (strlen($haystack) > $offset)) {
05267         if (function_exists('mb_stripos')) {
05268           $pos = mb_stripos($haystack, $needle, --$offset,'UTF-8');
05269         } else {
05270           $pos = stripos($haystack, $needle, --$offset);
05271         }
05272         if ($pos !== false) {
05273           return ++$pos;
05274         }
05275       }
05276     }
05277     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05278   } //  function SEARCHINSENSITIVE()

05288   public static function LEFT($value = '', $chars = 1) {
05289     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
05290     $chars    = self::flattenSingleValue($chars);
05291 
05292     if ($chars < 0) {
05293       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05294     }
05295 
05296     if (is_bool($value)) {
05297       $value = ($value) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05298     }
05299 
05300     if (function_exists('mb_substr')) {
05301       return mb_substr($value, 0, $chars, 'UTF-8');
05302     } else {
05303       return substr($value, 0, $chars);
05304     }
05305   } //  function LEFT()
05306 
05307 
05315   public static function RIGHT($value = '', $chars = 1) {
05316     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
05317     $chars    = self::flattenSingleValue($chars);
05318 
05319     if ($chars < 0) {
05320       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05321     }
05322 
05323     if (is_bool($value)) {
05324       $value = ($value) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05325     }
05326 
05327     if ((function_exists('mb_substr')) && (function_exists('mb_strlen'))) {
05328       return mb_substr($value, mb_strlen($value, 'UTF-8') - $chars, $chars, 'UTF-8');
05329     } else {
05330       return substr($value, strlen($value) - $chars);
05331     }
05332   } //  function RIGHT()
05333

05343   public static function MID($value = '', $start = 1, $chars = null) {
05344     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
05345     $start    = self::flattenSingleValue($start);
05346     $chars    = self::flattenSingleValue($chars);
05347 
05348     if (($start < 1) || ($chars < 0)) {
05349       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05350     }
05351 
05352     if (is_bool($value)) {
05353       $value = ($value) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05354     }
05355 
05356     if (function_exists('mb_substr')) {
05357       return mb_substr($value, --$start, $chars, 'UTF-8');
05358     } else {
05359       return substr($value, --$start, $chars);
05360     }
05361   } //  function MID()

05363 
05372   public static function REPLACE($oldText = '', $start = 1, $chars = null, $newText) {
05373     $oldText  = self::flattenSingleValue($oldText);
05374     $start    = self::flattenSingleValue($start);
05375     $chars    = self::flattenSingleValue($chars);
05376     $newText  = self::flattenSingleValue($newText);
05377 
05378     $left = self::LEFT($oldText,$start-1);
05379     $right = self::RIGHT($oldText,self::STRINGLENGTH($oldText)-($start+$chars)+1);
05380 
05381     return $left.$newText.$right;
05382   } //  function REPLACE()
05383 
05384 
05394   public static function SUBSTITUTE($text = '', $fromText = '', $toText = '', $instance = 0) {
05395     $text   = self::flattenSingleValue($text);
05396     $fromText = self::flattenSingleValue($fromText);
05397     $toText   = self::flattenSingleValue($toText);
05398     $instance = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($instance));
05399 
05400     if ($instance == 0) {
05401       if(function_exists('mb_str_replace')) {
05402         return mb_str_replace($fromText,$toText,$text);
05403       } else {
05404         return str_replace($fromText,$toText,$text);
05405       }
05406     } else {
05407       $pos = -1;
05408       while($instance > 0) {
05409         if (function_exists('mb_strpos')) {
05410           $pos = mb_strpos($text, $fromText, $pos+1, 'UTF-8');
05411         } else {
05412           $pos = strpos($text, $fromText, $pos+1);
05413         }
05414         if ($pos === false) {
05415           break;
05416         }
05417         --$instance;
05418       }
05419       if ($pos !== false) {
05420         if (function_exists('mb_strlen')) {
05421           return self::REPLACE($text,++$pos,mb_strlen($fromText, 'UTF-8'),$toText);
05422         } else {
05423           return self::REPLACE($text,++$pos,strlen($fromText),$toText);
05424         }
05425       }
05426     }
05427 
05428     return $left.$newText.$right;
05429   } //  function SUBSTITUTE()

05442       return $testValue;
05443     }
05444     return Null;
05445   } //  function RETURNSTRING()

05457     $no_commas    = self::flattenSingleValue($no_commas);

05460     if ($decimals < 0) { $decimals = 0; }
05461     if (!$no_commas) {

05511   public static function TRIMNONPRINTABLE($stringValue = '') {
05512     $stringValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($stringValue);
05513 
05514     if (is_bool($stringValue)) {
05515       $stringValue = ($stringValue) ? 'TRUE' : 'FALSE';
05516     }

05519       self::$_invalidChars = range(chr(0),chr(31));
05520     }
05521

05523       return str_replace(self::$_invalidChars,'',trim($stringValue,"\x00..\x1F"));
05524     }
05525     return Null;
05526   } //  function TRIMNONPRINTABLE()

05707   public static function DATE($year = 0, $month = 1, $day = 1) {
05708     $year = (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($year);
05709     $month  = (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($month);
05710     $day  = (integer) self::flattenSingleValue($day);
05711 
05712     $baseYear = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::getExcelCalendar();
05713     // Validate parameters
05714     if ($year < ($baseYear-1900)) {
05715       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
05716     }
05717     if ((($baseYear-1900) != 0) && ($year < $baseYear) && ($year >= 1900)) {
05718       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
05719     }
05720 
05721     if (($year < $baseYear) && ($year >= ($baseYear-1900))) {
05722       $year += 1900;
05723     }
05724 
05725     if ($month < 1) {
05726       //  Handle year/month adjustment if month < 1
05727       --$month;
05728       $year += ceil($month / 12) - 1;
05729       $month = 13 - abs($month % 12);
05730     } elseif ($month > 12) {
05731       //  Handle year/month adjustment if month > 12
05732       $year += floor($month / 12);
05733       $month = ($month % 12);
05734     }
05735 
05736     // Re-validate the year parameter after adjustments
05737     if (($year < $baseYear) || ($year >= 10000)) {
05738       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
05739     }
05740 
05741     // Execute function
05742     $excelDateValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel($year, $month, $day);
05743     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
05744       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) $excelDateValue;
05745                           break;
05746       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($excelDateValue);
05747                           break;
05748       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($excelDateValue);
05749                           break;
05750     }
05751   } //  function DATE()
05752 
05753 
05763   public static function TIME($hour = 0, $minute = 0, $second = 0) {
05764     $hour = self::flattenSingleValue($hour);
05765     $minute = self::flattenSingleValue($minute);
05766     $second = self::flattenSingleValue($second);
05767 
05768     if ($hour == '') { $hour = 0; }
05769     if ($minute == '') { $minute = 0; }
05770     if ($second == '') { $second = 0; }
05771 
05772     if ((!is_numeric($hour)) || (!is_numeric($minute)) || (!is_numeric($second))) {
05773       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05774     }
05775     $hour = (integer) $hour;
05776     $minute = (integer) $minute;
05777     $second = (integer) $second;
05778 
05779     if ($second < 0) {
05780       $minute += floor($second / 60);
05781       $second = 60 - abs($second % 60);
05782       if ($second == 60) { $second = 0; }
05783     } elseif ($second >= 60) {
05784       $minute += floor($second / 60);
05785       $second = $second % 60;
05786     }
05787     if ($minute < 0) {
05788       $hour += floor($minute / 60);
05789       $minute = 60 - abs($minute % 60);
05790       if ($minute == 60) { $minute = 0; }
05791     } elseif ($minute >= 60) {
05792       $hour += floor($minute / 60);
05793       $minute = $minute % 60;
05794     }
05795 
05796     if ($hour > 23) {
05797       $hour = $hour % 24;
05798     } elseif ($hour < 0) {
05799       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
05800     }
05801 
05802     // Execute function
05803     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
05804       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : $date = 0;
05805                           $calendar = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::getExcelCalendar();
05806                           if ($calendar != PHPExcel_Shared_Date::CALENDAR_WINDOWS_1900) {
05807                            $date = 1;
05808                           }
05809                           return (float) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel($calendar, 1, $date, $hour, $minute, $second);
05810                           break;
05811       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP(PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel(1970, 1, 1, $hour-1, $minute, $second));  // -2147468400; //  -2147472000 + 3600
05812                           break;
05813       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : $dayAdjust = 0;
05814                           if ($hour < 0) {
05815                            $dayAdjust = floor($hour / 24);
05816                            $hour = 24 - abs($hour % 24);
05817                            if ($hour == 24) { $hour = 0; }
05818                           } elseif ($hour >= 24) {
05819                            $dayAdjust = floor($hour / 24);
05820                            $hour = $hour % 24;
05821                           }
05822                           $phpDateObject = new DateTime('1900-01-01 '.$hour.':'.$minute.':'.$second);
05823                           if ($dayAdjust != 0) {
05824                            $phpDateObject->modify($dayAdjust.' days');
05825                           }
05826                           return $phpDateObject;
05827                           break;
05828     }
05829   } //  function TIME()
05830 
05831 
05839   public static function DATEVALUE($dateValue = 1) {
05840     $dateValue = trim(self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue),'"');
05841     //  Strip any ordinals because they're allowed in Excel (English only)
05842     $dateValue = preg_replace('/(\d)(st|nd|rd|th)([ -\/])/Ui','$1$3',$dateValue);
05843     //  Convert separators (/ . or space) to hyphens (should also handle dot used for ordinals in some countries, e.g. Denmark, Germany)
05844     $dateValue  = str_replace(array('/','.','-','  '),array(' ',' ',' ',' '),$dateValue);
05845 
05846     $yearFound = false;
05847     $t1 = explode(' ',$dateValue);
05848     foreach($t1 as &$t) {
05849       if ((is_numeric($t)) && ($t > 31)) {
05850         if ($yearFound) {
05851           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05852         } else {
05853           if ($t < 100) { $t += 1900; }
05854           $yearFound = true;
05855         }
05856       }
05857     }
05858     if ((count($t1) == 1) && (strpos($t,':') != false)) {
05859       //  We've been fed a time value without any date
05860       return 0.0;
05861     } elseif (count($t1) == 2) {
05862       //  We only have two parts of the date: either day/month or month/year
05863       if ($yearFound) {
05864         array_unshift($t1,1);
05865       } else {
05866         array_push($t1,date('Y'));
05867       }
05868     }
05869     unset($t);
05870     $dateValue = implode(' ',$t1);
05871 
05872     $PHPDateArray = date_parse($dateValue);
05873     if (($PHPDateArray === False) || ($PHPDateArray['error_count'] > 0)) {
05874       $testVal1 = strtok($dateValue,'- ');
05875       if ($testVal1 !== False) {
05876         $testVal2 = strtok('- ');
05877         if ($testVal2 !== False) {
05878           $testVal3 = strtok('- ');
05879           if ($testVal3 === False) {
05880             $testVal3 = strftime('%Y');
05881           }
05882         } else {
05883           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05884         }
05885       } else {
05886         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05887       }
05888       $PHPDateArray = date_parse($testVal1.'-'.$testVal2.'-'.$testVal3);
05889       if (($PHPDateArray === False) || ($PHPDateArray['error_count'] > 0)) {
05890         $PHPDateArray = date_parse($testVal2.'-'.$testVal1.'-'.$testVal3);
05891         if (($PHPDateArray === False) || ($PHPDateArray['error_count'] > 0)) {
05892           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05893         }
05894       }
05895     }
05896 
05897     if (($PHPDateArray !== False) && ($PHPDateArray['error_count'] == 0)) {
05898       // Execute function
05899       if ($PHPDateArray['year'] == '')  { $PHPDateArray['year'] = strftime('%Y'); }
05900       if ($PHPDateArray['month'] == '') { $PHPDateArray['month'] = strftime('%m'); }
05901       if ($PHPDateArray['day'] == '')   { $PHPDateArray['day'] = strftime('%d'); }
05902       $excelDateValue = floor(PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel($PHPDateArray['year'],$PHPDateArray['month'],$PHPDateArray['day'],$PHPDateArray['hour'],$PHPDateArray['minute'],$PHPDateArray['second']));
05903 
05904       switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
05905         case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) $excelDateValue;
05906                             break;
05907         case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($excelDateValue);
05908                             break;
05909         case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return new DateTime($PHPDateArray['year'].'-'.$PHPDateArray['month'].'-'.$PHPDateArray['day'].' 00:00:00');
05910                             break;
05911       }
05912     }
05913     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05914   } //  function DATEVALUE()
05915 
05916 
05923   private static function _getDateValue($dateValue) {
05924     if (!is_numeric($dateValue)) {
05925       if ((is_string($dateValue)) && (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC)) {
05926         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05927       }
05928       if ((is_object($dateValue)) && ($dateValue instanceof PHPExcel_Shared_Date::$dateTimeObjectType)) {
05929         $dateValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($dateValue);
05930       } else {
05931         $saveReturnDateType = self::getReturnDateType();
05932         self::setReturnDateType(self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL);
05933         $dateValue = self::DATEVALUE($dateValue);
05934         self::setReturnDateType($saveReturnDateType);
05935       }
05936     }
05937     return $dateValue;
05938   } //  function _getDateValue()

05948   public static function TIMEVALUE($timeValue) {
05949     $timeValue = trim(self::flattenSingleValue($timeValue),'"');
05950     $timeValue  = str_replace(array('/','.'),array('-','-'),$timeValue);
05951 
05952     $PHPDateArray = date_parse($timeValue);
05953     if (($PHPDateArray !== False) && ($PHPDateArray['error_count'] == 0)) {
05954       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
05955         $excelDateValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel($PHPDateArray['year'],$PHPDateArray['month'],$PHPDateArray['day'],$PHPDateArray['hour'],$PHPDateArray['minute'],$PHPDateArray['second']);
05956       } else {
05957         $excelDateValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::FormattedPHPToExcel(1900,1,1,$PHPDateArray['hour'],$PHPDateArray['minute'],$PHPDateArray['second']) - 1;
05958       }
05959 
05960       switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
05961         case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) $excelDateValue;
05962                             break;
05963         case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) $phpDateValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($excelDateValue+25569) - 3600;;
05964                             break;
05965         case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return new DateTime('1900-01-01 '.$PHPDateArray['hour'].':'.$PHPDateArray['minute'].':'.$PHPDateArray['second']);
05966                             break;
05967       }
05968     }
05969     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
05970   } //  function TIMEVALUE()
05971

05979   private static function _getTimeValue($timeValue) {
05980     $saveReturnDateType = self::getReturnDateType();
05981     self::setReturnDateType(self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL);
05982     $timeValue = self::TIMEVALUE($timeValue);
05983     self::setReturnDateType($saveReturnDateType);
05984     return $timeValue;
05985   } //  function _getTimeValue()

05994   public static function DATETIMENOW() {
05995     $saveTimeZone = date_default_timezone_get();
05996     date_default_timezone_set('UTC');
05997     $retValue = False;
05998     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
05999       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : $retValue = (float) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel(time());
06000                           break;
06001       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : $retValue = (integer) time();
06002                           break;
06003       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : $retValue = new DateTime();
06004                           break;
06005     }
06006     date_default_timezone_set($saveTimeZone);
06007 
06008     return $retValue;
06009   } //  function DATETIMENOW()
06010 
06011 
06018   public static function DATENOW() {
06019     $saveTimeZone = date_default_timezone_get();
06020     date_default_timezone_set('UTC');
06021     $retValue = False;
06022     $excelDateTime = floor(PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel(time()));
06023     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
06024       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : $retValue = (float) $excelDateTime;
06025                           break;
06026       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : $retValue = (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($excelDateTime) - 3600;
06027                           break;
06028       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : $retValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($excelDateTime);
06029                           break;
06030     }
06031     date_default_timezone_set($saveTimeZone);
06032 
06033     return $retValue;
06034   } //  function DATENOW()

06037   private static function _isLeapYear($year) {
06038     return ((($year % 4) == 0) && (($year % 100) != 0) || (($year % 400) == 0));
06039   } //  function _isLeapYear()
06040 
06041 
06042   private static function _dateDiff360($startDay, $startMonth, $startYear, $endDay, $endMonth, $endYear, $methodUS) {
06043     if ($startDay == 31) {
06044       --$startDay;
06045     } elseif ($methodUS && ($startMonth == 2 && ($startDay == 29 || ($startDay == 28 && !self::_isLeapYear($startYear))))) {
06046       $startDay = 30;
06047     }
06048     if ($endDay == 31) {
06049       if ($methodUS && $startDay != 30) {
06050         $endDay = 1;
06051         if ($endMonth == 12) {
06052           ++$endYear;
06053           $endMonth = 1;
06054         } else {
06055           ++$endMonth;
06056         }
06057       } else {
06058         $endDay = 30;
06059       }
06060     }
06061 
06062     return $endDay + $endMonth * 30 + $endYear * 360 - $startDay - $startMonth * 30 - $startYear * 360;
06063   } //  function _dateDiff360()
06064 
06065 
06074   public static function DAYS360($startDate = 0, $endDate = 0, $method = false) {
06075     $startDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($startDate);
06076     $endDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($endDate);
06077 
06078     if (is_string($startDate = self::_getDateValue($startDate))) {
06079       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06080     }
06081     if (is_string($endDate = self::_getDateValue($endDate))) {
06082       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06083     }
06084 
06085     // Execute function
06086     $PHPStartDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($startDate);
06087     $startDay = $PHPStartDateObject->format('j');
06088     $startMonth = $PHPStartDateObject->format('n');
06089     $startYear = $PHPStartDateObject->format('Y');
06090 
06091     $PHPEndDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($endDate);
06092     $endDay = $PHPEndDateObject->format('j');
06093     $endMonth = $PHPEndDateObject->format('n');
06094     $endYear = $PHPEndDateObject->format('Y');
06095 
06096     return self::_dateDiff360($startDay, $startMonth, $startYear, $endDay, $endMonth, $endYear, !$method);
06097   } //  function DAYS360()

06099 
06108   public static function DATEDIF($startDate = 0, $endDate = 0, $unit = 'D') {
06109     $startDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($startDate);
06110     $endDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($endDate);
06111     $unit   = strtoupper(self::flattenSingleValue($unit));
06112 
06113     if (is_string($startDate = self::_getDateValue($startDate))) {
06114       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06115     }
06116     if (is_string($endDate = self::_getDateValue($endDate))) {
06117       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06118     }
06119 
06120     // Validate parameters
06121     if ($startDate >= $endDate) {
06122       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06123     }
06124 
06125     // Execute function
06126     $difference = $endDate - $startDate;
06127 
06128     $PHPStartDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($startDate);
06129     $startDays = $PHPStartDateObject->format('j');
06130     $startMonths = $PHPStartDateObject->format('n');
06131     $startYears = $PHPStartDateObject->format('Y');
06132 
06133     $PHPEndDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($endDate);
06134     $endDays = $PHPEndDateObject->format('j');
06135     $endMonths = $PHPEndDateObject->format('n');
06136     $endYears = $PHPEndDateObject->format('Y');
06137 
06138     $retVal = self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06139     switch ($unit) {
06140       case 'D':
06141         $retVal = intval($difference);
06142         break;
06143       case 'M':
06144         $retVal = intval($endMonths - $startMonths) + (intval($endYears - $startYears) * 12);
06145         //  We're only interested in full months
06146         if ($endDays < $startDays) {
06147           --$retVal;
06148         }
06149         break;
06150       case 'Y':
06151         $retVal = intval($endYears - $startYears);
06152         //  We're only interested in full months
06153         if ($endMonths < $startMonths) {
06154           --$retVal;
06155         } elseif (($endMonths == $startMonths) && ($endDays < $startDays)) {
06156           --$retVal;
06157         }
06158         break;
06159       case 'MD':
06160         if ($endDays < $startDays) {
06161           $retVal = $endDays;
06162           $PHPEndDateObject->modify('-'.$endDays.' days');
06163           $adjustDays = $PHPEndDateObject->format('j');
06164           if ($adjustDays > $startDays) {
06165             $retVal += ($adjustDays - $startDays);
06166           }
06167         } else {
06168           $retVal = $endDays - $startDays;
06169         }
06170         break;
06171       case 'YM':
06172         $retVal = intval($endMonths - $startMonths);
06173         if ($retVal < 0) $retVal = 12 + $retVal;
06174         //  We're only interested in full months
06175         if ($endDays < $startDays) {
06176           --$retVal;
06177         }
06178         break;
06179       case 'YD':
06180         $retVal = intval($difference);
06181         if ($endYears > $startYears) {
06182           while ($endYears > $startYears) {
06183             $PHPEndDateObject->modify('-1 year');
06184             $endYears = $PHPEndDateObject->format('Y');
06185           }
06186           $retVal = $PHPEndDateObject->format('z') - $PHPStartDateObject->format('z');
06187           if ($retVal < 0) { $retVal += 365; }
06188         }
06189         break;
06190     }
06191     return $retVal;
06192   } //  function DATEDIF()
06193 
06194 
06212   public static function YEARFRAC($startDate = 0, $endDate = 0, $method = 0) {
06213     $startDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($startDate);
06214     $endDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($endDate);
06215     $method   = self::flattenSingleValue($method);
06216 
06217     if (is_string($startDate = self::_getDateValue($startDate))) {
06218       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06219     }
06220     if (is_string($endDate = self::_getDateValue($endDate))) {
06221       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06222     }
06223 
06224     if (((is_numeric($method)) && (!is_string($method))) || ($method == '')) {
06225       switch($method) {
06226         case 0  :
06227           return self::DAYS360($startDate,$endDate) / 360;
06228           break;
06229         case 1  :
06230           $days = self::DATEDIF($startDate,$endDate);
06231           $startYear = self::YEAR($startDate);
06232           $endYear = self::YEAR($endDate);
06233           $years = $endYear - $startYear + 1;
06234           $leapDays = 0;
06235           if ($years == 1) {
06236             if (self::_isLeapYear($endYear)) {
06237               $startMonth = self::MONTHOFYEAR($startDate);
06238               $endMonth = self::MONTHOFYEAR($endDate);
06239               $endDay = self::DAYOFMONTH($endDate);
06240               if (($startMonth < 3) ||
06241                 (($endMonth * 100 + $endDay) >= (2 * 100 + 29))) {
06242                   $leapDays += 1;
06243               }
06244             }
06245           } else {
06246             for($year = $startYear; $year <= $endYear; ++$year) {
06247               if ($year == $startYear) {
06248                 $startMonth = self::MONTHOFYEAR($startDate);
06249                 $startDay = self::DAYOFMONTH($startDate);
06250                 if ($startMonth < 3) {
06251                   $leapDays += (self::_isLeapYear($year)) ? 1 : 0;
06252                 }
06253               } elseif($year == $endYear) {
06254                 $endMonth = self::MONTHOFYEAR($endDate);
06255                 $endDay = self::DAYOFMONTH($endDate);
06256                 if (($endMonth * 100 + $endDay) >= (2 * 100 + 29)) {
06257                   $leapDays += (self::_isLeapYear($year)) ? 1 : 0;
06258                 }
06259               } else {
06260                 $leapDays += (self::_isLeapYear($year)) ? 1 : 0;
06261               }
06262             }
06263             if ($years == 2) {
06264               if (($leapDays == 0) && (self::_isLeapYear($startYear)) && ($days > 365)) {
06265                 $leapDays = 1;
06266               } elseif ($days < 366) {
06267                 $years = 1;
06268               }
06269             }
06270             $leapDays /= $years;
06271           }
06272           return $days / (365 + $leapDays);
06273           break;
06274         case 2  :
06275           return self::DATEDIF($startDate,$endDate) / 360;
06276           break;
06277         case 3  :
06278           return self::DATEDIF($startDate,$endDate) / 365;
06279           break;
06280         case 4  :
06281           return self::DAYS360($startDate,$endDate,True) / 360;
06282           break;
06283       }
06284     }
06285     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06286   } //  function YEARFRAC()
06287 
06288 
06297   public static function NETWORKDAYS($startDate,$endDate) {
06298     //  Retrieve the mandatory start and end date that are referenced in the function definition
06299     $startDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($startDate);
06300     $endDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($endDate);
06301     //  Flush the mandatory start and end date that are referenced in the function definition, and get the optional days
06302     $dateArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
06303     array_shift($dateArgs);
06304     array_shift($dateArgs);
06305 
06306     //  Validate the start and end dates
06307     if (is_string($startDate = $sDate = self::_getDateValue($startDate))) {
06308       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06309     }
06310     $startDate = (float) floor($startDate);
06311     if (is_string($endDate = $eDate = self::_getDateValue($endDate))) {
06312       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06313     }
06314     $endDate = (float) floor($endDate);
06315 
06316     if ($sDate > $eDate) {
06317       $startDate = $eDate;
06318       $endDate = $sDate;
06319     }
06320 
06321     // Execute function
06322     $startDoW = 6 - self::DAYOFWEEK($startDate,2);
06323     if ($startDoW < 0) { $startDoW = 0; }
06324     $endDoW = self::DAYOFWEEK($endDate,2);
06325     if ($endDoW >= 6) { $endDoW = 0; }
06326 
06327     $wholeWeekDays = floor(($endDate - $startDate) / 7) * 5;
06328     $partWeekDays = $endDoW + $startDoW;
06329     if ($partWeekDays > 5) {
06330       $partWeekDays -= 5;
06331     }
06332 
06333     //  Test any extra holiday parameters
06334     $holidayCountedArray = array();
06335     foreach ($dateArgs as $holidayDate) {
06336       if (is_string($holidayDate = self::_getDateValue($holidayDate))) {
06337         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06338       }
06339       if (($holidayDate >= $startDate) && ($holidayDate <= $endDate)) {
06340         if ((self::DAYOFWEEK($holidayDate,2) < 6) && (!in_array($holidayDate,$holidayCountedArray))) {
06341           --$partWeekDays;
06342           $holidayCountedArray[] = $holidayDate;
06343         }
06344       }
06345     }
06346 
06347     if ($sDate > $eDate) {
06348       return 0 - ($wholeWeekDays + $partWeekDays);
06349     }
06350     return $wholeWeekDays + $partWeekDays;
06351   } //  function NETWORKDAYS()
06352 
06353 
06362   public static function WORKDAY($startDate,$endDays) {
06363     //  Retrieve the mandatory start date and days that are referenced in the function definition
06364     $startDate  = self::flattenSingleValue($startDate);
06365     $endDays  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($endDays);
06366     //  Flush the mandatory start date and days that are referenced in the function definition, and get the optional days
06367     $dateArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
06368     array_shift($dateArgs);
06369     array_shift($dateArgs);
06370 
06371     if ((is_string($startDate = self::_getDateValue($startDate))) || (!is_numeric($endDays))) {
06372       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06373     }
06374     $startDate = (float) floor($startDate);
06375     //  If endDays is 0, we always return startDate
06376     if ($endDays == 0) { return $startDate; }
06377 
06378     $decrementing = ($endDays < 0) ? True : False;
06379 
06380     //  Adjust the start date if it falls over a weekend
06381 
06382     $startDoW = self::DAYOFWEEK($startDate,3);
06383     if (self::DAYOFWEEK($startDate,3) >= 5) {
06384       $startDate += ($decrementing) ? -$startDoW + 4: 7 - $startDoW;
06385       ($decrementing) ? $endDays++ : $endDays--;
06386     }
06387 
06388     //  Add endDays
06389     $endDate = (float) $startDate + (intval($endDays / 5) * 7) + ($endDays % 5);
06390 
06391     //  Adjust the calculated end date if it falls over a weekend
06392     $endDoW = self::DAYOFWEEK($endDate,3);
06393     if ($endDoW >= 5) {
06394       $endDate += ($decrementing) ? -$endDoW + 4: 7 - $endDoW;
06395     }
06396 
06397     //  Test any extra holiday parameters
06398     if (count($dateArgs) > 0) {
06399       $holidayCountedArray = $holidayDates = array();
06400       foreach ($dateArgs as $holidayDate) {
06401         if ((!is_null($holidayDate)) && (trim($holidayDate) > '')) {
06402           if (is_string($holidayDate = self::_getDateValue($holidayDate))) {
06403             return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06404           }
06405           if (self::DAYOFWEEK($holidayDate,3) < 5) {
06406             $holidayDates[] = $holidayDate;
06407           }
06408         }
06409       }
06410       if ($decrementing) {
06411         rsort($holidayDates, SORT_NUMERIC);
06412       } else {
06413         sort($holidayDates, SORT_NUMERIC);
06414       }
06415       foreach ($holidayDates as $holidayDate) {
06416         if ($decrementing) {
06417           if (($holidayDate <= $startDate) && ($holidayDate >= $endDate)) {
06418             if (!in_array($holidayDate,$holidayCountedArray)) {
06419               --$endDate;
06420               $holidayCountedArray[] = $holidayDate;
06421             }
06422           }
06423         } else {
06424           if (($holidayDate >= $startDate) && ($holidayDate <= $endDate)) {
06425             if (!in_array($holidayDate,$holidayCountedArray)) {
06426               ++$endDate;
06427               $holidayCountedArray[] = $holidayDate;
06428             }
06429           }
06430         }
06431         //  Adjust the calculated end date if it falls over a weekend
06432         $endDoW = self::DAYOFWEEK($endDate,3);
06433         if ($endDoW >= 5) {
06434           $endDate += ($decrementing) ? -$endDoW + 4: 7 - $endDoW;
06435         }
06436 
06437       }
06438     }
06439 
06440     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
06441       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) $endDate;
06442                           break;
06443       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($endDate);
06444                           break;
06445       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($endDate);
06446                           break;
06447     }
06448   } //  function WORKDAY()
06449

06457   public static function DAYOFMONTH($dateValue = 1) {
06458     $dateValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue);
06459 
06460     if (is_string($dateValue = self::_getDateValue($dateValue))) {
06461       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06462     } elseif ($dateValue == 0.0) {
06463       return 0;
06464     } elseif ($dateValue < 0.0) {
06465       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06466     }
06467 
06468     // Execute function
06469     $PHPDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($dateValue);
06470 
06471     return (int) $PHPDateObject->format('j');
06472   } //  function DAYOFMONTH()

06481   public static function DAYOFWEEK($dateValue = 1, $style = 1) {
06482     $dateValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue);
06483     $style    = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($style));
06484 
06485     if (is_string($dateValue = self::_getDateValue($dateValue))) {
06486       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06487     } elseif ($dateValue < 0.0) {
06488       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06489     }
06490 
06491     // Execute function
06492     $PHPDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($dateValue);
06493     $DoW = $PHPDateObject->format('w');
06494 
06495     $firstDay = 1;
06496     switch ($style) {
06497       case 1: ++$DoW;
06498           break;
06499       case 2: if ($DoW == 0) { $DoW = 7; }
06500           break;
06501       case 3: if ($DoW == 0) { $DoW = 7; }
06502           $firstDay = 0;
06503           --$DoW;
06504           break;
06505       default:
06506     }
06507     if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_EXCEL) {
06508       //  Test for Excel's 1900 leap year, and introduce the error as required
06509       if (($PHPDateObject->format('Y') == 1900) && ($PHPDateObject->format('n') <= 2)) {
06510         --$DoW;
06511         if ($DoW < $firstDay) {
06512           $DoW += 7;
06513         }
06514       }
06515     }
06516 
06517     return (int) $DoW;
06518   } //  function DAYOFWEEK()

06528   public static function WEEKOFYEAR($dateValue = 1, $method = 1) {
06529     $dateValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue);
06530     $method   = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($method));
06531 
06532     if (!is_numeric($method)) {
06533       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06534     } elseif (($method < 1) || ($method > 2)) {
06535       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06536     }
06537 
06538     if (is_string($dateValue = self::_getDateValue($dateValue))) {
06539       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06540     } elseif ($dateValue < 0.0) {
06541       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06542     }
06543 
06544     // Execute function
06545     $PHPDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($dateValue);
06546     $dayOfYear = $PHPDateObject->format('z');
06547     $dow = $PHPDateObject->format('w');
06548     $PHPDateObject->modify('-'.$dayOfYear.' days');
06549     $dow = $PHPDateObject->format('w');
06550     $daysInFirstWeek = 7 - (($dow + (2 - $method)) % 7);
06551     $dayOfYear -= $daysInFirstWeek;
06552     $weekOfYear = ceil($dayOfYear / 7) + 1;
06553 
06554     return (int) $weekOfYear;
06555   } //  function WEEKOFYEAR()

06608   public static function HOUROFDAY($timeValue = 0) {
06609     $timeValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($timeValue);
06610 
06611     if (!is_numeric($timeValue)) {
06612       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06613         $testVal = strtok($timeValue,'/-: ');
06614         if (strlen($testVal) < strlen($timeValue)) {
06615           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06616         }
06617       }
06618       $timeValue = self::_getTimeValue($timeValue);
06619       if (is_string($timeValue)) {
06620         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06621       }
06622     }
06623     // Execute function
06624     if ($timeValue >= 1) {
06625       $timeValue = fmod($timeValue,1);
06626     } elseif ($timeValue < 0.0) {
06627       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06628     }
06629     $timeValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($timeValue);
06630 
06631     return (int) gmdate('G',$timeValue);
06632   } //  function HOUROFDAY()

06645       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06646         $testVal = strtok($timeValue,'/-: ');
06647         if (strlen($testVal) < strlen($timeValue)) {
06648           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06649         }
06650       }
06651       $timeValue = self::_getTimeValue($timeValue);
06652       if (is_string($timeValue)) {
06653         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];

06655     }
06656     // Execute function
06657     if ($timeValue >= 1) {
06658       $timeValue = fmod($timeValue,1);
06659     } elseif ($timeValue < 0.0) {
06660       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06661     }
06662     $timeValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($timeValue);

06674   public static function SECONDOFMINUTE($timeValue = 0) {
06675     $timeValue  = self::flattenSingleValue($timeValue);
06676 
06677     if (!is_numeric($timeValue)) {
06678       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06679         $testVal = strtok($timeValue,'/-: ');
06680         if (strlen($testVal) < strlen($timeValue)) {
06681           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06682         }
06683       }
06684       $timeValue = self::_getTimeValue($timeValue);
06685       if (is_string($timeValue)) {
06686         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06687       }
06688     }
06689     // Execute function
06690     if ($timeValue >= 1) {
06691       $timeValue = fmod($timeValue,1);
06692     } elseif ($timeValue < 0.0) {
06693       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06694     }
06695     $timeValue = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP($timeValue);
06696 
06697     return (int) gmdate('s',$timeValue);
06698   } //  function SECONDOFMINUTE()
06699 
06700 
06701   private static function _adjustDateByMonths($dateValue = 0, $adjustmentMonths = 0) {
06702     // Execute function
06703     $PHPDateObject = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($dateValue);
06704     $oMonth = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('m');
06705     $oYear = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('Y');
06706 
06707     $adjustmentMonthsString = (string) $adjustmentMonths;
06708     if ($adjustmentMonths > 0) {
06709       $adjustmentMonthsString = '+'.$adjustmentMonths;
06710     }
06711     if ($adjustmentMonths != 0) {
06712       $PHPDateObject->modify($adjustmentMonthsString.' months');
06713     }
06714     $nMonth = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('m');
06715     $nYear = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('Y');
06716 
06717     $monthDiff = ($nMonth - $oMonth) + (($nYear - $oYear) * 12);
06718     if ($monthDiff != $adjustmentMonths) {
06719       $adjustDays = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('d');
06720       $adjustDaysString = '-'.$adjustDays.' days';
06721       $PHPDateObject->modify($adjustDaysString);
06722     }
06723     return $PHPDateObject;
06724   } //  function _adjustDateByMonths()
06725 
06726 
06737   public static function EDATE($dateValue = 1, $adjustmentMonths = 0) {
06738     $dateValue      = self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue);
06739     $adjustmentMonths = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($adjustmentMonths));
06740 
06741     if (!is_numeric($adjustmentMonths)) {
06742       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06743     }
06744 
06745     if (is_string($dateValue = self::_getDateValue($dateValue))) {
06746       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06747     }
06748 
06749     // Execute function
06750     $PHPDateObject = self::_adjustDateByMonths($dateValue,$adjustmentMonths);
06751 
06752     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
06753       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($PHPDateObject);
06754                           break;
06755       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP(PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($PHPDateObject));
06756                           break;
06757       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return $PHPDateObject;
06758                           break;
06759     }
06760   } //  function EDATE()

06773   public static function EOMONTH($dateValue = 1, $adjustmentMonths = 0) {
06774     $dateValue      = self::flattenSingleValue($dateValue);
06775     $adjustmentMonths = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($adjustmentMonths));
06776 
06777     if (!is_numeric($adjustmentMonths)) {
06778       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06779     }
06780 
06781     if (is_string($dateValue = self::_getDateValue($dateValue))) {
06782       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06783     }
06784 
06785     // Execute function
06786     $PHPDateObject = self::_adjustDateByMonths($dateValue,$adjustmentMonths+1);
06787     $adjustDays = (int) $PHPDateObject->format('d');
06788     $adjustDaysString = '-'.$adjustDays.' days';
06789     $PHPDateObject->modify($adjustDaysString);
06790 
06791     switch (self::getReturnDateType()) {
06792       case self::RETURNDATE_EXCEL     : return (float) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($PHPDateObject);
06793                           break;
06794       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_NUMERIC : return (integer) PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHP(PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($PHPDateObject));
06795                           break;
06796       case self::RETURNDATE_PHP_OBJECT  : return $PHPDateObject;
06797                           break;
06798     }
06799   } //  function EOMONTH()

06811   public static function TRUNC($value = 0, $number_digits = 0) {
06812     $value      = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
06813     $number_digits  = self::flattenSingleValue($number_digits);
06814 
06815     // Validate parameters
06816     if ($number_digits < 0) {
06817       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06818     }
06819 
06820     // Truncate
06821     if ($number_digits > 0) {
06822       $value = $value * pow(10, $number_digits);
06823     }
06824     $value = intval($value);
06825     if ($number_digits > 0) {
06826       $value = $value / pow(10, $number_digits);
06827     }
06828 
06829     // Return
06830     return $value;
06831   } //  function TRUNC()

06842   public static function POWER($x = 0, $y = 2) {
06843     $x  = self::flattenSingleValue($x);
06844     $y  = self::flattenSingleValue($y);
06845 
06846     // Validate parameters
06847     if ($x == 0 && $y <= 0) {
06848       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
06849     }
06850 
06851     // Return
06852     return pow($x, $y);
06853   } //  function POWER()

06856   private static function _nbrConversionFormat($xVal,$places) {
06857     if (!is_null($places)) {
06858       if (strlen($xVal) <= $places) {
06859         return substr(str_pad($xVal,$places,'0',STR_PAD_LEFT),-10);
06860       } else {
06861         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06862       }
06863     }
06864 
06865     return substr($xVal,-10);
06866   } //  function _nbrConversionFormat()

06877   public static function BINTODEC($x) {
06878     $x  = self::flattenSingleValue($x);
06879 
06880     if (is_bool($x)) {
06881       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
06882         $x = (int) $x;
06883       } else {
06884         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06885       }
06886     }
06887     if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06888       $x = floor($x);
06889     }
06890     $x = (string) $x;
06891     if (strlen($x) > preg_match_all('/[01]/',$x,$out)) {
06892       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06893     }
06894     if (strlen($x) > 10) {
06895       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06896     } elseif (strlen($x) == 10) {
06897       //  Two's Complement
06898       $x = substr($x,-9);
06899       return '-'.(512-bindec($x));
06900     }
06901     return bindec($x);
06902   } //  function BINTODEC()

06913   public static function BINTOHEX($x, $places=null) {
06914     $x  = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($x));
06915     $places = self::flattenSingleValue($places);
06916 
06917     if (is_bool($x)) {
06918       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
06919         $x = (int) $x;
06920       } else {
06921         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06922       }
06923     }
06924     if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06925       $x = floor($x);
06926     }
06927     $x = (string) $x;
06928     if (strlen($x) > preg_match_all('/[01]/',$x,$out)) {
06929       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06930     }
06931     if (strlen($x) > 10) {
06932       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06933     } elseif (strlen($x) == 10) {
06934       //  Two's Complement
06935       return str_repeat('F',8).substr(strtoupper(dechex(bindec(substr($x,-9)))),-2);
06936     }
06937     $hexVal = (string) strtoupper(dechex(bindec($x)));
06938 
06939     return self::_nbrConversionFormat($hexVal,$places);
06940   } //  function BINTOHEX()

06959         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06960       }
06961     }
06962     if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
06963       $x = floor($x);
06964     }
06965     $x = (string) $x;
06966     if (strlen($x) > preg_match_all('/[01]/',$x,$out)) {

06968     }

06970       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
06971     } elseif (strlen($x) == 10) {

06989   public static function DECTOBIN($x, $places=null) {
06990     $x  = self::flattenSingleValue($x);
06991     $places = self::flattenSingleValue($places);
06992 
06993     if (is_bool($x)) {
06994       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
06995         $x = (int) $x;
06996       } else {
06997         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
06998       }
06999     }
07000     $x = (string) $x;
07001     if (strlen($x) > preg_match_all('/[-0123456789.]/',$x,$out)) {
07002       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
07003     }
07004     $x = (string) floor($x);
07005     $r = decbin($x);
07006     if (strlen($r) == 32) {
07007       //  Two's Complement
07008       $r = substr($r,-10);
07009     } elseif (strlen($r) > 11) {
07010       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07011     }
07012 
07013     return self::_nbrConversionFormat($r,$places);
07014   } //  function DECTOBIN()

07228 
07229   public static function _parseComplex($complexNumber) {
07230     $workString = (string) $complexNumber;
07231 
07232     $realNumber = $imaginary = 0;
07233     //  Extract the suffix, if there is one
07234     $suffix = substr($workString,-1);
07235     if (!is_numeric($suffix)) {
07236       $workString = substr($workString,0,-1);
07237     } else {
07238       $suffix = '';
07239     }
07240 
07241     //  Split the input into its Real and Imaginary components
07242     $leadingSign = 0;
07243     if (strlen($workString) > 0) {
07244       $leadingSign = (($workString{0} == '+') || ($workString{0} == '-')) ? 1 : 0;
07245     }
07246     $power = '';
07247     $realNumber = strtok($workString, '+-');
07248     if (strtoupper(substr($realNumber,-1)) == 'E') {
07249       $power = strtok('+-');
07250       ++$leadingSign;
07251     }
07252 
07253     $realNumber = substr($workString,0,strlen($realNumber)+strlen($power)+$leadingSign);
07254 
07255     if ($suffix != '') {
07256       $imaginary = substr($workString,strlen($realNumber));
07257 
07258       if (($imaginary == '') && (($realNumber == '') || ($realNumber == '+') || ($realNumber == '-'))) {
07259         $imaginary = $realNumber.'1';
07260         $realNumber = '0';
07261       } else if ($imaginary == '') {
07262         $imaginary = $realNumber;
07263         $realNumber = '0';
07264       } elseif (($imaginary == '+') || ($imaginary == '-')) {
07265         $imaginary .= '1';
07266       }
07267     }
07268 
07269     $complexArray = array( 'real'   => $realNumber,
07270                  'imaginary'  => $imaginary,
07271                  'suffix'   => $suffix
07272                );
07273 
07274     return $complexArray;
07275   } //  function _parseComplex()
07276 
07277 
07278   private static function _cleanComplex($complexNumber) {
07279     if ($complexNumber{0} == '+') $complexNumber = substr($complexNumber,1);
07280     if ($complexNumber{0} == '0') $complexNumber = substr($complexNumber,1);
07281     if ($complexNumber{0} == '.') $complexNumber = '0'.$complexNumber;
07282     if ($complexNumber{0} == '+') $complexNumber = substr($complexNumber,1);
07283     return $complexNumber;
07284   }
07285 
07286 
07297   public static function COMPLEX($realNumber=0.0, $imaginary=0.0, $suffix='i') {
07298     $realNumber = (is_null($realNumber))  ? 0.0 : (float) self::flattenSingleValue($realNumber);
07299     $imaginary  = (is_null($imaginary))   ? 0.0 : (float) self::flattenSingleValue($imaginary);
07300     $suffix   = (is_null($suffix))    ? 'i' : self::flattenSingleValue($suffix);
07301 
07302     if (((is_numeric($realNumber)) && (is_numeric($imaginary))) &&
07303       (($suffix == 'i') || ($suffix == 'j') || ($suffix == ''))) {
07304       if ($suffix == '') $suffix = 'i';
07305       if ($realNumber == 0.0) {
07306         if ($imaginary == 0.0) {
07307           return (string) '0';
07308         } elseif ($imaginary == 1.0) {
07309           return (string) $suffix;
07310         } elseif ($imaginary == -1.0) {
07311           return (string) '-'.$suffix;
07312         }
07313         return (string) $imaginary.$suffix;
07314       } elseif ($imaginary == 0.0) {
07315         return (string) $realNumber;
07316       } elseif ($imaginary == 1.0) {
07317         return (string) $realNumber.'+'.$suffix;
07318       } elseif ($imaginary == -1.0) {
07319         return (string) $realNumber.'-'.$suffix;
07320       }
07321       if ($imaginary > 0) { $imaginary = (string) '+'.$imaginary; }
07322       return (string) $realNumber.$imaginary.$suffix;
07323     }
07324     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
07325   } //  function COMPLEX()
07326 
07327 
07336   public static function IMAGINARY($complexNumber) {
07337     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07338 
07339     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07340     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07341       return $parsedComplex;
07342     }
07343     return $parsedComplex['imaginary'];
07344   } //  function IMAGINARY()

07374   public static function IMABS($complexNumber) {
07375     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07376 
07377     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07378     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07379       return $parsedComplex;
07380     }
07381     return sqrt(($parsedComplex['real'] * $parsedComplex['real']) + ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary']));
07382   } //  function IMABS()
