07384 
07393   public static function IMARGUMENT($complexNumber) {
07394     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07395 
07396     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07397     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07398       return $parsedComplex;
07399     }
07400 
07401     if ($parsedComplex['real'] == 0.0) {
07402       if ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0) {
07403         return 0.0;
07404       } elseif($parsedComplex['imaginary'] < 0.0) {
07405         return M_PI / -2;
07406       } else {
07407         return M_PI / 2;
07408       }
07409     } elseif ($parsedComplex['real'] > 0.0) {
07410       return atan($parsedComplex['imaginary'] / $parsedComplex['real']);
07411     } elseif ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] < 0.0) {
07412       return 0 - (M_PI - atan(abs($parsedComplex['imaginary']) / abs($parsedComplex['real'])));
07413     } else {
07414       return M_PI - atan($parsedComplex['imaginary'] / abs($parsedComplex['real']));
07415     }
07416   } //  function IMARGUMENT()
07417 
07418 
07427   public static function IMCONJUGATE($complexNumber) {
07428     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07429 
07430     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07431 
07432     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07433       return $parsedComplex;
07434     }
07435 
07436     if ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0) {
07437       return $parsedComplex['real'];
07438     } else {
07439       return self::_cleanComplex(self::COMPLEX($parsedComplex['real'], 0 - $parsedComplex['imaginary'], $parsedComplex['suffix']));
07440     }
07441   } //  function IMCONJUGATE()
07442 
07443 
07452   public static function IMCOS($complexNumber) {
07453     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07454 
07455     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07456     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07457       return $parsedComplex;
07458     }
07459 
07460     if ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0) {
07461       return cos($parsedComplex['real']);
07462     } else {
07463       return self::IMCONJUGATE(self::COMPLEX(cos($parsedComplex['real']) * cosh($parsedComplex['imaginary']),sin($parsedComplex['real']) * sinh($parsedComplex['imaginary']),$parsedComplex['suffix']));
07464     }
07465   } //  function IMCOS()
07466 
07467 
07476   public static function IMSIN($complexNumber) {
07477     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07478 
07479     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07480     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07481       return $parsedComplex;
07482     }
07483 
07484     if ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0) {
07485       return sin($parsedComplex['real']);
07486     } else {
07487       return self::COMPLEX(sin($parsedComplex['real']) * cosh($parsedComplex['imaginary']),cos($parsedComplex['real']) * sinh($parsedComplex['imaginary']),$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07488     }
07489   } //  function IMSIN()
07490 
07491 
07500   public static function IMSQRT($complexNumber) {
07501     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07502 
07503     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07504     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07505       return $parsedComplex;
07506     }
07507 
07508     $theta = self::IMARGUMENT($complexNumber);
07509     $d1 = cos($theta / 2);
07510     $d2 = sin($theta / 2);
07511     $r = sqrt(sqrt(($parsedComplex['real'] * $parsedComplex['real']) + ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary'])));
07512 
07513     if ($parsedComplex['suffix'] == '') {
07514       return self::COMPLEX($d1 * $r,$d2 * $r);
07515     } else {
07516       return self::COMPLEX($d1 * $r,$d2 * $r,$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07517     }
07518   } //  function IMSQRT()
07519 
07520 
07529   public static function IMLN($complexNumber) {
07530     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07531 
07532     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07533     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07534       return $parsedComplex;
07535     }
07536 
07537     if (($parsedComplex['real'] == 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07538       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07539     }
07540 
07541     $logR = log(sqrt(($parsedComplex['real'] * $parsedComplex['real']) + ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary'])));
07542     $t = self::IMARGUMENT($complexNumber);
07543 
07544     if ($parsedComplex['suffix'] == '') {
07545       return self::COMPLEX($logR,$t);
07546     } else {
07547       return self::COMPLEX($logR,$t,$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07548     }
07549   } //  function IMLN()
07550 
07551 
07560   public static function IMLOG10($complexNumber) {
07561     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07562 
07563     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07564     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07565       return $parsedComplex;
07566     }
07567 
07568     if (($parsedComplex['real'] == 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07569       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07570     } elseif (($parsedComplex['real'] > 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07571       return log10($parsedComplex['real']);
07572     }
07573 
07574     return self::IMPRODUCT(log10(EULER),self::IMLN($complexNumber));
07575   } //  function IMLOG10()
07576 
07577 
07586   public static function IMLOG2($complexNumber) {
07587     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07588 
07589     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07590     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07591       return $parsedComplex;
07592     }
07593 
07594     if (($parsedComplex['real'] == 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07595       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07596     } elseif (($parsedComplex['real'] > 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07597       return log($parsedComplex['real'],2);
07598     }
07599 
07600     return self::IMPRODUCT(log(EULER,2),self::IMLN($complexNumber));
07601   } //  function IMLOG2()
07602 
07603 
07612   public static function IMEXP($complexNumber) {
07613     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07614 
07615     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07616     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07617       return $parsedComplex;
07618     }
07619 
07620     if (($parsedComplex['real'] == 0.0) && ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0)) {
07621       return '1';
07622     }
07623 
07624     $e = exp($parsedComplex['real']);
07625     $eX = $e * cos($parsedComplex['imaginary']);
07626     $eY = $e * sin($parsedComplex['imaginary']);
07627 
07628     if ($parsedComplex['suffix'] == '') {
07629       return self::COMPLEX($eX,$eY);
07630     } else {
07631       return self::COMPLEX($eX,$eY,$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07632     }
07633   } //  function IMEXP()
07634 
07635 
07644   public static function IMPOWER($complexNumber,$realNumber) {
07645     $complexNumber  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber);
07646     $realNumber   = self::flattenSingleValue($realNumber);
07647 
07648     if (!is_numeric($realNumber)) {
07649       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
07650     }
07651 
07652     $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber);
07653     if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07654       return $parsedComplex;
07655     }
07656 
07657     $r = sqrt(($parsedComplex['real'] * $parsedComplex['real']) + ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary']));
07658     $rPower = pow($r,$realNumber);
07659     $theta = self::IMARGUMENT($complexNumber) * $realNumber;
07660     if ($theta == 0) {
07661       return 1;
07662     } elseif ($parsedComplex['imaginary'] == 0.0) {
07663       return self::COMPLEX($rPower * cos($theta),$rPower * sin($theta),$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07664     } else {
07665       return self::COMPLEX($rPower * cos($theta),$rPower * sin($theta),$parsedComplex['suffix']);
07666     }
07667   } //  function IMPOWER()
07668 
07669 
07679   public static function IMDIV($complexDividend,$complexDivisor) {
07680     $complexDividend  = self::flattenSingleValue($complexDividend);
07681     $complexDivisor = self::flattenSingleValue($complexDivisor);
07682 
07683     $parsedComplexDividend = self::_parseComplex($complexDividend);
07684     if (!is_array($parsedComplexDividend)) {
07685       return $parsedComplexDividend;
07686     }
07687 
07688     $parsedComplexDivisor = self::_parseComplex($complexDivisor);
07689     if (!is_array($parsedComplexDivisor)) {
07690       return $parsedComplexDividend;
07691     }
07692 
07693     if (($parsedComplexDividend['suffix'] != '') && ($parsedComplexDivisor['suffix'] != '') &&
07694       ($parsedComplexDividend['suffix'] != $parsedComplexDivisor['suffix'])) {
07695       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07696     }
07697     if (($parsedComplexDividend['suffix'] != '') && ($parsedComplexDivisor['suffix'] == '')) {
07698       $parsedComplexDivisor['suffix'] = $parsedComplexDividend['suffix'];
07699     }
07700 
07701     $d1 = ($parsedComplexDividend['real'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['real']) + ($parsedComplexDividend['imaginary'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['imaginary']);
07702     $d2 = ($parsedComplexDividend['imaginary'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['real']) - ($parsedComplexDividend['real'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['imaginary']);
07703     $d3 = ($parsedComplexDivisor['real'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['real']) + ($parsedComplexDivisor['imaginary'] * $parsedComplexDivisor['imaginary']);
07704 
07705     $r = $d1/$d3;
07706     $i = $d2/$d3;
07707 
07708     if ($i > 0.0) {
07709       return self::_cleanComplex($r.'+'.$i.$parsedComplexDivisor['suffix']);
07710     } elseif ($i < 0.0) {
07711       return self::_cleanComplex($r.$i.$parsedComplexDivisor['suffix']);
07712     } else {
07713       return $r;
07714     }
07715   } //  function IMDIV()
07716 
07717 
07727   public static function IMSUB($complexNumber1,$complexNumber2) {
07728     $complexNumber1 = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber1);
07729     $complexNumber2 = self::flattenSingleValue($complexNumber2);
07730 
07731     $parsedComplex1 = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber1);
07732     if (!is_array($parsedComplex1)) {
07733       return $parsedComplex1;
07734     }
07735 
07736     $parsedComplex2 = self::_parseComplex($complexNumber2);
07737     if (!is_array($parsedComplex2)) {
07738       return $parsedComplex2;
07739     }
07740 
07741     if ((($parsedComplex1['suffix'] != '') && ($parsedComplex2['suffix'] != '')) &&
07742       ($parsedComplex1['suffix'] != $parsedComplex2['suffix'])) {
07743       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07744     } elseif (($parsedComplex1['suffix'] == '') && ($parsedComplex2['suffix'] != '')) {
07745       $parsedComplex1['suffix'] = $parsedComplex2['suffix'];
07746     }
07747 
07748     $d1 = $parsedComplex1['real'] - $parsedComplex2['real'];
07749     $d2 = $parsedComplex1['imaginary'] - $parsedComplex2['imaginary'];
07750 
07751     return self::COMPLEX($d1,$d2,$parsedComplex1['suffix']);
07752   } //  function IMSUB()
07753 
07754 
07763   public static function IMSUM() {
07764     // Return value
07765     $returnValue = self::_parseComplex('0');
07766     $activeSuffix = '';
07767 
07768     // Loop through the arguments
07769     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
07770     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
07771       $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($arg);
07772       if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07773         return $parsedComplex;
07774       }
07775 
07776       if ($activeSuffix == '') {
07777         $activeSuffix = $parsedComplex['suffix'];
07778       } elseif (($parsedComplex['suffix'] != '') && ($activeSuffix != $parsedComplex['suffix'])) {
07779         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
07780       }
07781 
07782       $returnValue['real'] += $parsedComplex['real'];
07783       $returnValue['imaginary'] += $parsedComplex['imaginary'];
07784     }
07785 
07786     if ($returnValue['imaginary'] == 0.0) { $activeSuffix = ''; }
07787     return self::COMPLEX($returnValue['real'],$returnValue['imaginary'],$activeSuffix);
07788   } //  function IMSUM()
07789 
07790 
07799   public static function IMPRODUCT() {
07800     // Return value
07801     $returnValue = self::_parseComplex('1');
07802     $activeSuffix = '';
07803 
07804     // Loop through the arguments
07805     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
07806     foreach ($aArgs as $arg) {
07807       $parsedComplex = self::_parseComplex($arg);
07808       if (!is_array($parsedComplex)) {
07809         return $parsedComplex;
07810       }
07811       $workValue = $returnValue;
07812       if (($parsedComplex['suffix'] != '') && ($activeSuffix == '')) {
07813         $activeSuffix = $parsedComplex['suffix'];
07814       } elseif (($parsedComplex['suffix'] != '') && ($activeSuffix != $parsedComplex['suffix'])) {
07815         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
07816       }
07817       $returnValue['real'] = ($workValue['real'] * $parsedComplex['real']) - ($workValue['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary']);
07818       $returnValue['imaginary'] = ($workValue['real'] * $parsedComplex['imaginary']) + ($workValue['imaginary'] * $parsedComplex['real']);
07819     }
07820 
07821     if ($returnValue['imaginary'] == 0.0) { $activeSuffix = ''; }
07822     return self::COMPLEX($returnValue['real'],$returnValue['imaginary'],$activeSuffix);
07823   } //  function IMPRODUCT()

08513   public static function CONVERTUOM($value, $fromUOM, $toUOM) {
08514     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
08515     $fromUOM  = self::flattenSingleValue($fromUOM);
08516     $toUOM    = self::flattenSingleValue($toUOM);
08517 
08518     if (!is_numeric($value)) {
08519       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08520     }
08521     $fromMultiplier = 1;
08522     if (isset(self::$_conversionUnits[$fromUOM])) {
08523       $unitGroup1 = self::$_conversionUnits[$fromUOM]['Group'];
08524     } else {
08525       $fromMultiplier = substr($fromUOM,0,1);
08526       $fromUOM = substr($fromUOM,1);
08527       if (isset(self::$_conversionMultipliers[$fromMultiplier])) {
08528         $fromMultiplier = self::$_conversionMultipliers[$fromMultiplier]['multiplier'];
08529       } else {
08530         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
08531       }
08532       if ((isset(self::$_conversionUnits[$fromUOM])) && (self::$_conversionUnits[$fromUOM]['AllowPrefix'])) {
08533         $unitGroup1 = self::$_conversionUnits[$fromUOM]['Group'];
08534       } else {
08535         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
08536       }
08537     }
08538     $value *= $fromMultiplier;
08539 
08540     $toMultiplier = 1;
08541     if (isset(self::$_conversionUnits[$toUOM])) {
08542       $unitGroup2 = self::$_conversionUnits[$toUOM]['Group'];
08543     } else {
08544       $toMultiplier = substr($toUOM,0,1);
08545       $toUOM = substr($toUOM,1);
08546       if (isset(self::$_conversionMultipliers[$toMultiplier])) {
08547         $toMultiplier = self::$_conversionMultipliers[$toMultiplier]['multiplier'];
08548       } else {
08549         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
08550       }
08551       if ((isset(self::$_conversionUnits[$toUOM])) && (self::$_conversionUnits[$toUOM]['AllowPrefix'])) {
08552         $unitGroup2 = self::$_conversionUnits[$toUOM]['Group'];
08553       } else {
08554         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
08555       }
08556     }
08557     if ($unitGroup1 != $unitGroup2) {
08558       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
08559     }
08560 
08561     if ($fromUOM == $toUOM) {
08562       return 1.0;
08563     } elseif ($unitGroup1 == 'Temperature') {
08564       if (($fromUOM == 'F') || ($fromUOM == 'fah')) {
08565         if (($toUOM == 'F') || ($toUOM == 'fah')) {
08566           return 1.0;
08567         } else {
08568           $value = (($value - 32) / 1.8);
08569           if (($toUOM == 'K') || ($toUOM == 'kel')) {
08570             $value += 273.15;
08571           }
08572           return $value;
08573         }
08574       } elseif ((($fromUOM == 'K') || ($fromUOM == 'kel')) &&
08575             (($toUOM == 'K') || ($toUOM == 'kel'))) {
08576             return 1.0;
08577       } elseif ((($fromUOM == 'C') || ($fromUOM == 'cel')) &&
08578             (($toUOM == 'C') || ($toUOM == 'cel'))) {
08579           return 1.0;
08580       }
08581       if (($toUOM == 'F') || ($toUOM == 'fah')) {
08582         if (($fromUOM == 'K') || ($fromUOM == 'kel')) {
08583           $value -= 273.15;
08584         }
08585         return ($value * 1.8) + 32;
08586       }
08587       if (($toUOM == 'C') || ($toUOM == 'cel')) {
08588         return $value - 273.15;
08589       }
08590       return $value + 273.15;
08591     }
08592     return ($value * self::$_unitConversions[$unitGroup1][$fromUOM][$toUOM]) / $toMultiplier;
08593   } //  function CONVERTUOM()

08605   public static function BESSELI($x, $n) {
08606     $x  = (is_null($x)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($x);
08607     $n  = (is_null($n)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($n);
08608 
08609     if ((is_numeric($x)) && (is_numeric($n))) {
08610       $n  = floor($n);
08611       if ($n < 0) {
08612         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08613       }
08614       $f_2_PI = 2 * M_PI;
08615 
08616       if (abs($x) <= 30) {
08617         $fTerm = pow($x / 2, $n) / self::FACT($n);
08618         $nK = 1;
08619         $fResult = $fTerm;
08620         $fSqrX = ($x * $x) / 4;
08621         do {
08622           $fTerm *= $fSqrX;
08623           $fTerm /= ($nK * ($nK + $n));
08624           $fResult += $fTerm;
08625         } while ((abs($fTerm) > 1e-10) && (++$nK < 100));
08626       } else {
08627         $fXAbs = abs($x);
08628         $fResult = exp($fXAbs) / sqrt($f_2_PI * $fXAbs);
08629         if (($n && 1) && ($x < 0)) {
08630           $fResult = -$fResult;
08631         }
08632       }
08633       return $fResult;
08634     }
08635     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08636   } //  function BESSELI()
08637 
08638 
08648   public static function BESSELJ($x, $n) {
08649     $x  = (is_null($x)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($x);
08650     $n  = (is_null($n)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($n);
08651 
08652     if ((is_numeric($x)) && (is_numeric($n))) {
08653       $n  = floor($n);
08654       if ($n < 0) {
08655         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08656       }
08657       $f_PI_DIV_2 = M_PI / 2;
08658       $f_PI_DIV_4 = M_PI / 4;
08659 
08660       $fResult = 0;
08661       if (abs($x) <= 30) {
08662         $fTerm = pow($x / 2, $n) / self::FACT($n);
08663         $nK = 1;
08664         $fResult = $fTerm;
08665         $fSqrX = ($x * $x) / -4;
08666         do {
08667           $fTerm *= $fSqrX;
08668           $fTerm /= ($nK * ($nK + $n));
08669           $fResult += $fTerm;
08670         } while ((abs($fTerm) > 1e-10) && (++$nK < 100));
08671       } else {
08672         $fXAbs = abs($x);
08673         $fResult = sqrt(M_2DIVPI / $fXAbs) * cos($fXAbs - $n * $f_PI_DIV_2 - $f_PI_DIV_4);
08674         if (($n && 1) && ($x < 0)) {
08675           $fResult = -$fResult;
08676         }
08677       }
08678       return $fResult;
08679     }
08680     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08681   } //  function BESSELJ()
08682 
08683 
08684   private static function _Besselk0($fNum) {
08685     if ($fNum <= 2) {
08686       $fNum2 = $fNum * 0.5;
08687       $y = ($fNum2 * $fNum2);
08688       $fRet = -log($fNum2) * self::BESSELI($fNum, 0) +
08689           (-0.57721566 + $y * (0.42278420 + $y * (0.23069756 + $y * (0.3488590e-1 + $y * (0.262698e-2 + $y *
08690           (0.10750e-3 + $y * 0.74e-5))))));
08691     } else {
08692       $y = 2 / $fNum;
08693       $fRet = exp(-$fNum) / sqrt($fNum) *
08694           (1.25331414 + $y * (-0.7832358e-1 + $y * (0.2189568e-1 + $y * (-0.1062446e-1 + $y *
08695           (0.587872e-2 + $y * (-0.251540e-2 + $y * 0.53208e-3))))));
08696     }
08697     return $fRet;
08698   } //  function _Besselk0()
08699 
08700 
08701   private static function _Besselk1($fNum) {
08702     if ($fNum <= 2) {
08703       $fNum2 = $fNum * 0.5;
08704       $y = ($fNum2 * $fNum2);
08705       $fRet = log($fNum2) * self::BESSELI($fNum, 1) +
08706           (1 + $y * (0.15443144 + $y * (-0.67278579 + $y * (-0.18156897 + $y * (-0.1919402e-1 + $y *
08707           (-0.110404e-2 + $y * (-0.4686e-4))))))) / $fNum;
08708     } else {
08709       $y = 2 / $fNum;
08710       $fRet = exp(-$fNum) / sqrt($fNum) *
08711           (1.25331414 + $y * (0.23498619 + $y * (-0.3655620e-1 + $y * (0.1504268e-1 + $y * (-0.780353e-2 + $y *
08712           (0.325614e-2 + $y * (-0.68245e-3)))))));
08713     }
08714     return $fRet;
08715   } //  function _Besselk1()
08716 
08717 
08727   public static function BESSELK($x, $ord) {
08728     $x    = (is_null($x))   ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($x);
08729     $ord  = (is_null($ord)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($ord);
08730 
08731     if ((is_numeric($x)) && (is_numeric($ord))) {
08732       if (($ord < 0) || ($x == 0.0)) {
08733         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08734       }
08735 
08736       switch(floor($ord)) {
08737         case 0 :  return self::_Besselk0($x);
08738               break;
08739         case 1 :  return self::_Besselk1($x);
08740               break;
08741         default : $fTox = 2 / $x;
08742               $fBkm = self::_Besselk0($x);
08743               $fBk  = self::_Besselk1($x);
08744               for ($n = 1; $n < $ord; ++$n) {
08745                 $fBkp = $fBkm + $n * $fTox * $fBk;
08746                 $fBkm = $fBk;
08747                 $fBk  = $fBkp;
08748               }
08749       }
08750       return $fBk;
08751     }
08752     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08753   } //  function BESSELK()
08754 
08755 
08756   private static function _Bessely0($fNum) {
08757     if ($fNum < 8.0) {
08758       $y = ($fNum * $fNum);
08759       $f1 = -2957821389.0 + $y * (7062834065.0 + $y * (-512359803.6 + $y * (10879881.29 + $y * (-86327.92757 + $y * 228.4622733))));
08760       $f2 = 40076544269.0 + $y * (745249964.8 + $y * (7189466.438 + $y * (47447.26470 + $y * (226.1030244 + $y))));
08761       $fRet = $f1 / $f2 + M_2DIVPI * self::BESSELJ($fNum, 0) * log($fNum);
08762     } else {
08763       $z = 8.0 / $fNum;
08764       $y = ($z * $z);
08765       $xx = $fNum - 0.785398164;
08766       $f1 = 1 + $y * (-0.1098628627e-2 + $y * (0.2734510407e-4 + $y * (-0.2073370639e-5 + $y * 0.2093887211e-6)));
08767       $f2 = -0.1562499995e-1 + $y * (0.1430488765e-3 + $y * (-0.6911147651e-5 + $y * (0.7621095161e-6 + $y * (-0.934945152e-7))));
08768       $fRet = sqrt(M_2DIVPI / $fNum) * (sin($xx) * $f1 + $z * cos($xx) * $f2);
08769     }
08770     return $fRet;
08771   } //  function _Bessely0()
08772 
08773 
08774   private static function _Bessely1($fNum) {
08775     if ($fNum < 8.0) {
08776       $y = ($fNum * $fNum);
08777       $f1 = $fNum * (-0.4900604943e13 + $y * (0.1275274390e13 + $y * (-0.5153438139e11 + $y * (0.7349264551e9 + $y *
08778         (-0.4237922726e7 + $y * 0.8511937935e4)))));
08779       $f2 = 0.2499580570e14 + $y * (0.4244419664e12 + $y * (0.3733650367e10 + $y * (0.2245904002e8 + $y *
08780         (0.1020426050e6 + $y * (0.3549632885e3 + $y)))));
08781       $fRet = $f1 / $f2 + M_2DIVPI * ( self::BESSELJ($fNum, 1) * log($fNum) - 1 / $fNum);
08782     } else {
08783       $z = 8.0 / $fNum;
08784       $y = ($z * $z);
08785       $xx = $fNum - 2.356194491;
08786       $f1 = 1 + $y * (0.183105e-2 + $y * (-0.3516396496e-4 + $y * (0.2457520174e-5 + $y * (-0.240337019e6))));
08787       $f2 = 0.04687499995 + $y * (-0.2002690873e-3 + $y * (0.8449199096e-5 + $y * (-0.88228987e-6 + $y * 0.105787412e-6)));
08788       $fRet = sqrt(M_2DIVPI / $fNum) * (sin($xx) * $f1 + $z * cos($xx) * $f2);
08789       #i12430# ...but this seems to work much better.
08790 //      $fRet = sqrt(M_2DIVPI / $fNum) * sin($fNum - 2.356194491);
08791     }
08792     return $fRet;
08793   } //  function _Bessely1()

08795 
08805   public static function BESSELY($x, $ord) {
08806     $x    = (is_null($x))   ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($x);
08807     $ord  = (is_null($ord)) ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($ord);
08808 
08809     if ((is_numeric($x)) && (is_numeric($ord))) {
08810       if (($ord < 0) || ($x == 0.0)) {
08811         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08812       }
08813 
08814       switch(floor($ord)) {
08815         case 0 :  return self::_Bessely0($x);
08816               break;
08817         case 1 :  return self::_Bessely1($x);
08818               break;
08819         default:  $fTox = 2 / $x;
08820               $fBym = self::_Bessely0($x);
08821               $fBy  = self::_Bessely1($x);
08822               for ($n = 1; $n < $ord; ++$n) {
08823                 $fByp = $n * $fTox * $fBy - $fBym;
08824                 $fBym = $fBy;
08825                 $fBy  = $fByp;
08826               }
08827       }
08828       return $fBy;
08829     }
08830     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08831   } //  function BESSELY()

08867 
08868   //
08869   //  Private method to calculate the erf value
08870   //
08871   private static $_two_sqrtpi = 1.128379167095512574;
08872 
08873   private static function _erfVal($x) {
08874     if (abs($x) > 2.2) {
08875       return 1 - self::_erfcVal($x);
08876     }
08877     $sum = $term = $x;
08878     $xsqr = ($x * $x);
08879     $j = 1;
08880     do {
08881       $term *= $xsqr / $j;
08882       $sum -= $term / (2 * $j + 1);
08883       ++$j;
08884       $term *= $xsqr / $j;
08885       $sum += $term / (2 * $j + 1);
08886       ++$j;
08887       if ($sum == 0.0) {
08888         break;
08889       }
08890     } while (abs($term / $sum) > PRECISION);
08891     return self::$_two_sqrtpi * $sum;
08892   } //  function _erfVal()
08893 
08894 
08905   public static function ERF($lower, $upper = null) {
08906     $lower  = self::flattenSingleValue($lower);
08907     $upper  = self::flattenSingleValue($upper);
08908 
08909     if (is_numeric($lower)) {
08910       if ($lower < 0) {
08911         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08912       }
08913       if (is_null($upper)) {
08914         return self::_erfVal($lower);
08915       }
08916       if (is_numeric($upper)) {
08917         if ($upper < 0) {
08918           return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08919         }
08920         return self::_erfVal($upper) - self::_erfVal($lower);
08921       }
08922     }
08923     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08924   } //  function ERF()
08925 
08926 
08927   //
08928   //  Private method to calculate the erfc value
08929   //
08930   private static $_one_sqrtpi = 0.564189583547756287;
08931 
08932   private static function _erfcVal($x) {
08933     if (abs($x) < 2.2) {
08934       return 1 - self::_erfVal($x);
08935     }
08936     if ($x < 0) {
08937       return 2 - self::erfc(-$x);
08938     }
08939     $a = $n = 1;
08940     $b = $c = $x;
08941     $d = ($x * $x) + 0.5;
08942     $q1 = $q2 = $b / $d;
08943     $t = 0;
08944     do {
08945       $t = $a * $n + $b * $x;
08946       $a = $b;
08947       $b = $t;
08948       $t = $c * $n + $d * $x;
08949       $c = $d;
08950       $d = $t;
08951       $n += 0.5;
08952       $q1 = $q2;
08953       $q2 = $b / $d;
08954     } while ((abs($q1 - $q2) / $q2) > PRECISION);
08955     return self::$_one_sqrtpi * exp(-$x * $x) * $q2;
08956   } //  function _erfcVal()
08957 
08958 
08967   public static function ERFC($x) {
08968     $x  = self::flattenSingleValue($x);
08969 
08970     if (is_numeric($x)) {
08971       if ($x < 0) {
08972         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
08973       }
08974       return self::_erfcVal($x);
08975     }
08976     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
08977   } //  function ERFC()

08996       return mb_convert_case($mixedCaseString, MB_CASE_LOWER, 'UTF-8');
08997     } else {
08998       return strtoupper($mixedCaseString);
08999     }
09000   } //  function LOWERCASE()

09061   public static function DOLLAR($value = 0, $decimals = 2) {
09062     $value    = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
09063     $decimals = is_null($decimals) ? 0 : self::flattenSingleValue($decimals);
09064 
09065     // Validate parameters
09066     if (!is_numeric($value) || !is_numeric($decimals)) {
09067       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09068     }
09069     $decimals = floor($decimals);
09070 
09071     if ($decimals > 0) {
09072       return money_format('%.'.$decimals.'n',$value);
09073     } else {
09074       $round = pow(10,abs($decimals));
09075       if ($value < 0) { $round = 0-$round; }
09076       $value = self::MROUND($value,$round);
09077       //  The implementation of money_format used if the standard PHP function is not available can't handle decimal places of 0,
09078       //    so we display to 1 dp and chop off that character and the decimal separator using substr
09079       return substr(money_format('%.1n',$value),0,-2);
09080     }
09081   } //  function DOLLAR()

09083 
09094   public static function DOLLARDE($fractional_dollar = Null, $fraction = 0) {
09095     $fractional_dollar  = self::flattenSingleValue($fractional_dollar);
09096     $fraction     = (int)self::flattenSingleValue($fraction);
09097 
09098     // Validate parameters
09099     if (is_null($fractional_dollar) || $fraction < 0) {
09100       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09101     }
09102     if ($fraction == 0) {
09103       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
09104     }
09105 
09106     $dollars = floor($fractional_dollar);
09107     $cents = fmod($fractional_dollar,1);
09108     $cents /= $fraction;
09109     $cents *= pow(10,ceil(log10($fraction)));
09110     return $dollars + $cents;
09111   } //  function DOLLARDE()

09124   public static function DOLLARFR($decimal_dollar = Null, $fraction = 0) {
09125     $decimal_dollar = self::flattenSingleValue($decimal_dollar);
09126     $fraction   = (int)self::flattenSingleValue($fraction);
09127 
09128     // Validate parameters
09129     if (is_null($decimal_dollar) || $fraction < 0) {
09130       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09131     }
09132     if ($fraction == 0) {
09133       return self::$_errorCodes['divisionbyzero'];
09134     }
09135 
09136     $dollars = floor($decimal_dollar);
09137     $cents = fmod($decimal_dollar,1);
09138     $cents *= $fraction;
09139     $cents *= pow(10,-ceil(log10($fraction)));
09140     return $dollars + $cents;
09141   } //  function DOLLARFR()

09153   public static function EFFECT($nominal_rate = 0, $npery = 0) {
09154     $nominal_rate = self::flattenSingleValue($nominal_rate);
09155     $npery      = (int)self::flattenSingleValue($npery);
09156 
09157     // Validate parameters
09158     if ($nominal_rate <= 0 || $npery < 1) {
09159       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09160     }
09161 
09162     return pow((1 + $nominal_rate / $npery), $npery) - 1;
09163   } //  function EFFECT()

09175   public static function NOMINAL($effect_rate = 0, $npery = 0) {
09176     $effect_rate  = self::flattenSingleValue($effect_rate);
09177     $npery      = (int)self::flattenSingleValue($npery);
09178 
09179     // Validate parameters
09180     if ($effect_rate <= 0 || $npery < 1) {
09181       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09182     }
09183 
09184     // Calculate
09185     return $npery * (pow($effect_rate + 1, 1 / $npery) - 1);
09186   } //  function NOMINAL()

09201   public static function PV($rate = 0, $nper = 0, $pmt = 0, $fv = 0, $type = 0) {
09202     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09203     $nper = self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09204     $pmt  = self::flattenSingleValue($pmt);
09205     $fv   = self::flattenSingleValue($fv);
09206     $type = self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09207 
09208     // Validate parameters
09209     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09210       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09211     }
09212 
09213     // Calculate
09214     if (!is_null($rate) && $rate != 0) {
09215       return (-$pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) * ((pow(1 + $rate, $nper) - 1) / $rate) - $fv) / pow(1 + $rate, $nper);
09216     } else {
09217       return -$fv - $pmt * $nper;
09218     }
09219   } //  function PV()
09220 
09221 
09234   public static function FV($rate = 0, $nper = 0, $pmt = 0, $pv = 0, $type = 0) {
09235     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09236     $nper = self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09237     $pmt  = self::flattenSingleValue($pmt);
09238     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09239     $type = self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09240 
09241     // Validate parameters
09242     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09243       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09244     }
09245 
09246     // Calculate
09247     if (!is_null($rate) && $rate != 0) {
09248       return -$pv * pow(1 + $rate, $nper) - $pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) * (pow(1 + $rate, $nper) - 1) / $rate;
09249     } else {
09250       return -$pv - $pmt * $nper;
09251     }
09252   } //  function FV()
09253

09259   public static function FVSCHEDULE($principal, $schedule) {
09260     $principal  = self::flattenSingleValue($principal);
09261     $schedule = self::flattenArray($schedule);
09262 
09263     foreach($schedule as $n) {
09264       $principal *= 1 + $n;
09265     }
09266 
09267     return $principal;
09268   } //  function FVSCHEDULE()

09283   public static function PMT($rate = 0, $nper = 0, $pv = 0, $fv = 0, $type = 0) {
09284     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09285     $nper = self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09286     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09287     $fv   = self::flattenSingleValue($fv);
09288     $type = self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09289 
09290     // Validate parameters
09291     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09292       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09293     }
09294 
09295     // Calculate
09296     if (!is_null($rate) && $rate != 0) {
09297       return (-$fv - $pv * pow(1 + $rate, $nper)) / (1 + $rate * $type) / ((pow(1 + $rate, $nper) - 1) / $rate);
09298     } else {
09299       return (-$pv - $fv) / $nper;
09300     }
09301   } //  function PMT()
09302 
09303 
09316   public static function NPER($rate = 0, $pmt = 0, $pv = 0, $fv = 0, $type = 0) {
09317     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09318     $pmt  = self::flattenSingleValue($pmt);
09319     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09320     $fv   = self::flattenSingleValue($fv);
09321     $type = self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09322 
09323     // Validate parameters
09324     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09325       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09326     }
09327 
09328     // Calculate
09329     if (!is_null($rate) && $rate != 0) {
09330       if ($pmt == 0 && $pv == 0) {
09331         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09332       }
09333       return log(($pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) / $rate - $fv) / ($pv + $pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) / $rate)) / log(1 + $rate);
09334     } else {
09335       if ($pmt == 0) {
09336         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09337       }
09338       return (-$pv -$fv) / $pmt;
09339     }
09340   } //  function NPER()

09344   private static function _interestAndPrincipal($rate=0, $per=0, $nper=0, $pv=0, $fv=0, $type=0) {
09345     $pmt = self::PMT($rate, $nper, $pv, $fv, $type);
09346     $capital = $pv;
09347     for ($i = 1; $i<= $per; ++$i) {
09348       $interest = ($type && $i == 1)? 0 : -$capital * $rate;
09349       $principal = $pmt - $interest;
09350       $capital += $principal;
09351     }
09352     return array($interest, $principal);
09353   } //  function _interestAndPrincipal()

09369   public static function IPMT($rate, $per, $nper, $pv, $fv = 0, $type = 0) {
09370     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09371     $per  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($per);
09372     $nper = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09373     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09374     $fv   = self::flattenSingleValue($fv);
09375     $type = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09376 
09377     // Validate parameters
09378     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09379       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09380     }
09381     if ($per <= 0 || $per > $nper) {
09382       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09383     }
09384 
09385     // Calculate
09386     $interestAndPrincipal = self::_interestAndPrincipal($rate, $per, $nper, $pv, $fv, $type);
09387     return $interestAndPrincipal[0];
09388   } //  function IPMT()

09405   public static function CUMIPMT($rate, $nper, $pv, $start, $end, $type = 0) {
09406     $rate = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09407     $nper = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09408     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09409     $start  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($start);
09410     $end  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($end);
09411     $type = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09412 
09413     // Validate parameters
09414     if ($type != 0 && $type != 1) {
09415       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09416     }
09417     if ($start < 1 || $start > $end) {
09418       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09419     }
09420 
09421     // Calculate
09422     $interest = 0;
09423     for ($per = $start; $per <= $end; ++$per) {
09424       $interest += self::IPMT($rate, $per, $nper, $pv, 0, $type);
09425     }
09426 
09427     return $interest;
09428   } //  function CUMIPMT()

09493       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];

09522   public static function ISPMT() {
09523     // Return value
09524     $returnValue = 0;
09525 
09526     // Get the parameters
09527     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
09528     $interestRate = array_shift($aArgs);
09529     $period = array_shift($aArgs);
09530     $numberPeriods = array_shift($aArgs);
09531     $principleRemaining = array_shift($aArgs);
09532 
09533     // Calculate
09534     $principlePayment = ($principleRemaining * 1.0) / ($numberPeriods * 1.0);
09535     for($i=0; $i <= $period; ++$i) {
09536       $returnValue = $interestRate * $principleRemaining * -1;
09537       $principleRemaining -= $principlePayment;
09538       // principle needs to be 0 after the last payment, don't let floating point screw it up
09539       if($i == $numberPeriods) {
09540         $returnValue = 0;
09541       }
09542     }
09543     return($returnValue);
09544   } //  function ISPMT()

09546 
09556   public static function NPV() {
09557     // Return value
09558     $returnValue = 0;
09559 
09560     // Loop through arguments
09561     $aArgs = self::flattenArray(func_get_args());
09562 
09563     // Calculate
09564     $rate = array_shift($aArgs);
09565     for ($i = 1; $i <= count($aArgs); ++$i) {
09566       // Is it a numeric value?
09567       if (is_numeric($aArgs[$i - 1])) {
09568         $returnValue += $aArgs[$i - 1] / pow(1 + $rate, $i);
09569       }
09570     }
09571 
09572     // Return
09573     return $returnValue;
09574   } //  function NPV()

09576 
09587   public static function XNPV($rate, $values, $dates) {
09588     if ((!is_array($values)) || (!is_array($dates))) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09589     $values = self::flattenArray($values);
09590     $dates  = self::flattenArray($dates);
09591     $valCount = count($values);
09592     if ($valCount != count($dates)) return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09593 
09594     $xnpv = 0.0;
09595     for ($i = 0; $i < $valCount; ++$i) {
09596       $xnpv += $values[$i] / pow(1 + $rate, self::DATEDIF($dates[0],$dates[$i],'d') / 365);
09597     }
09598     return (is_finite($xnpv) ? $xnpv : self::$_errorCodes['value']);
09599   } //  function XNPV()

09601 
09602   public static function IRR($values, $guess = 0.1) {
09603     if (!is_array($values)) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09604     $values = self::flattenArray($values);
09605     $guess = self::flattenSingleValue($guess);
09606 
09607     // create an initial range, with a root somewhere between 0 and guess
09608     $x1 = 0.0;
09609     $x2 = $guess;
09610     $f1 = self::NPV($x1, $values);
09611     $f2 = self::NPV($x2, $values);
09612     for ($i = 0; $i < FINANCIAL_MAX_ITERATIONS; ++$i) {
09613       if (($f1 * $f2) < 0.0) break;
09614       if (abs($f1) < abs($f2)) {
09615         $f1 = self::NPV($x1 += 1.6 * ($x1 - $x2), $values);
09616       } else {
09617         $f2 = self::NPV($x2 += 1.6 * ($x2 - $x1), $values);
09618       }
09619     }
09620     if (($f1 * $f2) > 0.0) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09621 
09622     $f = self::NPV($x1, $values);
09623     if ($f < 0.0) {
09624       $rtb = $x1;
09625       $dx = $x2 - $x1;
09626     } else {
09627       $rtb = $x2;
09628       $dx = $x1 - $x2;
09629     }
09630 
09631     for ($i = 0;  $i < FINANCIAL_MAX_ITERATIONS; ++$i) {
09632       $dx *= 0.5;
09633       $x_mid = $rtb + $dx;
09634       $f_mid = self::NPV($x_mid, $values);
09635       if ($f_mid <= 0.0) $rtb = $x_mid;
09636       if ((abs($f_mid) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION) || (abs($dx) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION)) return $x_mid;
09637     }
09638     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09639   } //  function IRR()
09640 
09641 
09642   public static function MIRR($values, $finance_rate, $reinvestment_rate) {
09643     if (!is_array($values)) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09644     $values       = self::flattenArray($values);
09645     $finance_rate   = self::flattenSingleValue($finance_rate);
09646     $reinvestment_rate  = self::flattenSingleValue($reinvestment_rate);
09647     $n = count($values);
09648 
09649     $rr = 1.0 + $reinvestment_rate;
09650     $fr = 1.0 + $finance_rate;
09651 
09652     $npv_pos = $npv_neg = 0.0;
09653     foreach($values as $i => $v) {
09654       if ($v >= 0) {
09655         $npv_pos += $v / pow($rr, $i);
09656       } else {
09657         $npv_neg += $v / pow($fr, $i);
09658       }
09659     }
09660 
09661     if (($npv_neg == 0) || ($npv_pos == 0) || ($reinvestment_rate <= -1)) {
09662       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09663     }
09664 
09665     $mirr = pow((-$npv_pos * pow($rr, $n))
09666         / ($npv_neg * ($rr)), (1.0 / ($n - 1))) - 1.0;
09667 
09668     return (is_finite($mirr) ? $mirr : self::$_errorCodes['value']);
09669   } //  function MIRR()
09670 
09671 
09672   public static function XIRR($values, $dates, $guess = 0.1) {
09673     if ((!is_array($values)) && (!is_array($dates))) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09674     $values = self::flattenArray($values);
09675     $dates  = self::flattenArray($dates);
09676     $guess = self::flattenSingleValue($guess);
09677     if (count($values) != count($dates)) return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09678 
09679     // create an initial range, with a root somewhere between 0 and guess
09680     $x1 = 0.0;
09681     $x2 = $guess;
09682     $f1 = self::XNPV($x1, $values, $dates);
09683     $f2 = self::XNPV($x2, $values, $dates);
09684     for ($i = 0; $i < FINANCIAL_MAX_ITERATIONS; ++$i) {
09685       if (($f1 * $f2) < 0.0) break;
09686       if (abs($f1) < abs($f2)) {
09687         $f1 = self::XNPV($x1 += 1.6 * ($x1 - $x2), $values, $dates);
09688       } else {
09689         $f2 = self::XNPV($x2 += 1.6 * ($x2 - $x1), $values, $dates);
09690       }
09691     }
09692     if (($f1 * $f2) > 0.0) return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09693 
09694     $f = self::XNPV($x1, $values, $dates);
09695     if ($f < 0.0) {
09696       $rtb = $x1;
09697       $dx = $x2 - $x1;
09698     } else {
09699       $rtb = $x2;
09700       $dx = $x1 - $x2;
09701     }
09702 
09703     for ($i = 0;  $i < FINANCIAL_MAX_ITERATIONS; ++$i) {
09704       $dx *= 0.5;
09705       $x_mid = $rtb + $dx;
09706       $f_mid = self::XNPV($x_mid, $values, $dates);
09707       if ($f_mid <= 0.0) $rtb = $x_mid;
09708       if ((abs($f_mid) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION) || (abs($dx) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION)) return $x_mid;
09709     }
09710     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09711   }
09712 
09713 
09718   public static function RATE($nper, $pmt, $pv, $fv = 0.0, $type = 0, $guess = 0.1) {
09719     $nper = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($nper);
09720     $pmt  = self::flattenSingleValue($pmt);
09721     $pv   = self::flattenSingleValue($pv);
09722     $fv   = (is_null($fv))  ? 0.0 : self::flattenSingleValue($fv);
09723     $type = (is_null($type))  ? 0   : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($type);
09724     $guess  = (is_null($guess)) ? 0.1 : self::flattenSingleValue($guess);
09725 
09726     $rate = $guess;
09727     if (abs($rate) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION) {
09728       $y = $pv * (1 + $nper * $rate) + $pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) * $nper + $fv;
09729     } else {
09730       $f = exp($nper * log(1 + $rate));
09731       $y = $pv * $f + $pmt * (1 / $rate + $type) * ($f - 1) + $fv;
09732     }
09733     $y0 = $pv + $pmt * $nper + $fv;
09734     $y1 = $pv * $f + $pmt * (1 / $rate + $type) * ($f - 1) + $fv;
09735 
09736     // find root by secant method
09737     $i  = $x0 = 0.0;
09738     $x1 = $rate;
09739     while ((abs($y0 - $y1) > FINANCIAL_PRECISION) && ($i < FINANCIAL_MAX_ITERATIONS)) {
09740       $rate = ($y1 * $x0 - $y0 * $x1) / ($y1 - $y0);
09741       $x0 = $x1;
09742       $x1 = $rate;
09743 
09744       if (abs($rate) < FINANCIAL_PRECISION) {
09745         $y = $pv * (1 + $nper * $rate) + $pmt * (1 + $rate * $type) * $nper + $fv;
09746       } else {
09747         $f = exp($nper * log(1 + $rate));
09748         $y = $pv * $f + $pmt * (1 / $rate + $type) * ($f - 1) + $fv;
09749       }
09750 
09751       $y0 = $y1;
09752       $y1 = $y;
09753       ++$i;
09754     }
09755     return $rate;
09756   } //  function RATE()
09757 
09758 
09774   public static function DB($cost, $salvage, $life, $period, $month=12) {
09775     $cost   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
09776     $salvage  = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
09777     $life   = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($life);
09778     $period   = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($period);
09779     $month    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($month);
09780 
09781     //  Validate
09782     if ((is_numeric($cost)) && (is_numeric($salvage)) && (is_numeric($life)) && (is_numeric($period)) && (is_numeric($month))) {
09783       if ($cost == 0) {
09784         return 0.0;
09785       } elseif (($cost < 0) || (($salvage / $cost) < 0) || ($life <= 0) || ($period < 1) || ($month < 1)) {
09786         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09787       }
09788       //  Set Fixed Depreciation Rate
09789       $fixedDepreciationRate = 1 - pow(($salvage / $cost), (1 / $life));
09790       $fixedDepreciationRate = round($fixedDepreciationRate, 3);
09791 
09792       //  Loop through each period calculating the depreciation
09793       $previousDepreciation = 0;
09794       for ($per = 1; $per <= $period; ++$per) {
09795         if ($per == 1) {
09796           $depreciation = $cost * $fixedDepreciationRate * $month / 12;
09797         } elseif ($per == ($life + 1)) {
09798           $depreciation = ($cost - $previousDepreciation) * $fixedDepreciationRate * (12 - $month) / 12;
09799         } else {
09800           $depreciation = ($cost - $previousDepreciation) * $fixedDepreciationRate;
09801         }
09802         $previousDepreciation += $depreciation;
09803       }
09804       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
09805         $depreciation = round($depreciation,2);
09806       }
09807       return $depreciation;
09808     }
09809     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09810   } //  function DB()
09811 
09812 
09826   public static function DDB($cost, $salvage, $life, $period, $factor=2.0) {
09827     $cost   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
09828     $salvage  = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
09829     $life   = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($life);
09830     $period   = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($period);
09831     $factor   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($factor);
09832 
09833     //  Validate
09834     if ((is_numeric($cost)) && (is_numeric($salvage)) && (is_numeric($life)) && (is_numeric($period)) && (is_numeric($factor))) {
09835       if (($cost <= 0) || (($salvage / $cost) < 0) || ($life <= 0) || ($period < 1) || ($factor <= 0.0) || ($period > $life)) {
09836         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09837       }
09838       //  Set Fixed Depreciation Rate
09839       $fixedDepreciationRate = 1 - pow(($salvage / $cost), (1 / $life));
09840       $fixedDepreciationRate = round($fixedDepreciationRate, 3);
09841 
09842       //  Loop through each period calculating the depreciation
09843       $previousDepreciation = 0;
09844       for ($per = 1; $per <= $period; ++$per) {
09845         $depreciation = min( ($cost - $previousDepreciation) * ($factor / $life), ($cost - $salvage - $previousDepreciation) );
09846         $previousDepreciation += $depreciation;
09847       }
09848       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) {
09849         $depreciation = round($depreciation,2);
09850       }
09851       return $depreciation;
09852     }
09853     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09854   } //  function DDB()

09857   private static function _daysPerYear($year,$basis) {
09858     switch ($basis) {
09859       case 0 :
09860       case 2 :
09861       case 4 :
09862         $daysPerYear = 360;
09863         break;
09864       case 3 :
09865         $daysPerYear = 365;
09866         break;
09867       case 1 :
09868         if (self::_isLeapYear($year)) {
09869           $daysPerYear = 366;
09870         } else {
09871           $daysPerYear = 365;
09872         }
09873         break;
09874       default :
09875         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09876     }
09877     return $daysPerYear;
09878   } //  function _daysPerYear()

09899   public static function ACCRINT($issue, $firstinter, $settlement, $rate, $par=1000, $frequency=1, $basis=0) {
09900     $issue    = self::flattenSingleValue($issue);
09901     $firstinter = self::flattenSingleValue($firstinter);
09902     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
09903     $rate   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09904     $par    = (is_null($par))   ? 1000 :  (float) self::flattenSingleValue($par);
09905     $frequency  = (is_null($frequency)) ? 1 :     (int) self::flattenSingleValue($frequency);
09906     $basis    = (is_null($basis))   ? 0 :   (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
09907 
09908     //  Validate
09909     if ((is_numeric($rate)) && (is_numeric($par))) {
09910       if (($rate <= 0) || ($par <= 0)) {
09911         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09912       }
09913       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $settlement, $basis);
09914       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement)) {
09915         return $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement;
09916       }
09917 
09918       return $par * $rate * $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement;
09919     }
09920     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
09921   } //  function ACCRINT()

09941   public static function ACCRINTM($issue, $settlement, $rate, $par=1000, $basis=0) {
09942     $issue    = self::flattenSingleValue($issue);
09943     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
09944     $rate   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09945     $par    = (is_null($par)) ? 1000 :  (float) self::flattenSingleValue($par);
09946     $basis    = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 :   (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
09947 
09948     //  Validate
09949     if ((is_numeric($rate)) && (is_numeric($par))) {
09950       if (($rate <= 0) || ($par <= 0)) {
09951         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
09952       }
09953       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $settlement, $basis);
09954       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement)) {
09955         return $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement;

09963   public static function AMORDEGRC($cost, $purchased, $firstPeriod, $salvage, $period, $rate, $basis=0) {
09964     $cost     = self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
09965     $purchased    = self::flattenSingleValue($purchased);
09966     $firstPeriod  = self::flattenSingleValue($firstPeriod);
09967     $salvage    = self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
09968     $period     = floor(self::flattenSingleValue($period));
09969     $rate     = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
09970     $basis      = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
09971 
09972     $fUsePer = 1.0 / $rate;
09973 
09974     if ($fUsePer < 3.0) {
09975       $amortiseCoeff = 1.0;
09976     } elseif ($fUsePer < 5.0) {
09977       $amortiseCoeff = 1.5;
09978     } elseif ($fUsePer <= 6.0) {
09979       $amortiseCoeff = 2.0;
09980     } else {
09981       $amortiseCoeff = 2.5;
09982     }
09983 
09984     $rate *= $amortiseCoeff;
09985 //    $fNRate = floor((self::YEARFRAC($purchased, $firstPeriod, $basis) * $rate * $cost) + 0.5);
09986     $fNRate = round(self::YEARFRAC($purchased, $firstPeriod, $basis) * $rate * $cost,0);
09987     $cost -= $fNRate;
09988     $fRest = $cost - $salvage;
09989 
09990     for ($n = 0; $n < $period; ++$n) {
09991 //      $fNRate = floor(($rate * $cost) + 0.5);
09992       $fNRate = round($rate * $cost,0);
09993       $fRest -= $fNRate;
09994 
09995       if ($fRest < 0.0) {
09996         switch ($period - $n) {
09997           case 0  :
09998           case 1  :
09999 //                return floor(($cost * 0.5) + 0.5);
10000                 return round($cost * 0.5,0);
10001                 break;
10002           default : return 0.0;
10003                 break;
10004         }
10005       }
10006       $cost -= $fNRate;
10007     }
10008     return $fNRate;
10009   } //  function AMORDEGRC()

10012   public static function AMORLINC($cost, $purchased, $firstPeriod, $salvage, $period, $rate, $basis=0) {
10013     $cost     = self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
10014     $purchased    = self::flattenSingleValue($purchased);
10015     $firstPeriod  = self::flattenSingleValue($firstPeriod);
10016     $salvage    = self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
10017     $period     = self::flattenSingleValue($period);
10018     $rate     = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
10019     $basis      = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10020 
10021     $fOneRate = $cost * $rate;
10022     $fCostDelta = $cost - $salvage;
10023     //  Note, quirky variation for leap years on the YEARFRAC for this function
10024     $purchasedYear = self::YEAR($purchased);
10025     $yearFrac = self::YEARFRAC($purchased, $firstPeriod, $basis);
10026     if (($basis == 1) && ($yearFrac < 1) && (self::_isLeapYear($purchasedYear))) {
10027       $yearFrac *= 365 / 366;
10028     }
10029     $f0Rate = $yearFrac * $rate * $cost;
10030     $nNumOfFullPeriods = intval(($cost - $salvage - $f0Rate) / $fOneRate);
10031 
10032     if ($period == 0) {
10033       return $f0Rate;
10034     } elseif ($period <= $nNumOfFullPeriods) {
10035       return $fOneRate;
10036     } elseif ($period == ($nNumOfFullPeriods + 1)) {
10037             return ($fCostDelta - $fOneRate * $nNumOfFullPeriods - $f0Rate);
10038     } else {
10039       return 0.0;
10040     }
10041   } //  function AMORLINC()

10055   private static function _coupFirstPeriodDate($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $next) {
10056     $months = 12 / $frequency;
10057 
10058     $result = PHPExcel_Shared_Date::ExcelToPHPObject($maturity);
10059     $eom = self::_lastDayOfMonth($result);
10060 
10061     while ($settlement < PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($result)) {
10062       $result->modify('-'.$months.' months');
10063     }
10064     if ($next) {
10065       $result->modify('+'.$months.' months');
10066     }
10067 
10068     if ($eom) {
10069       $result->modify('-1 day');
10070     }
10071 
10072     return PHPExcel_Shared_Date::PHPToExcel($result);
10073   } //  function _coupFirstPeriodDate()

10076   private static function _validFrequency($frequency) {
10077     if (($frequency == 1) || ($frequency == 2) || ($frequency == 4)) {
10078       return true;
10079     }
10080     if ((self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_GNUMERIC) &&
10081       (($frequency == 6) || ($frequency == 12))) {
10082       return true;
10083     }
10084     return false;
10085   } //  function _validFrequency()

10087   public static function COUPDAYS($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis=0) {
10088     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10089     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10090     $frequency  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($frequency);
10091     $basis    = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10092 
10093     if (is_string($settlement = self::_getDateValue($settlement))) {
10094       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10095     }
10096     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10097       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10098     }
10099 
10100     if (($settlement > $maturity) ||
10101       (!self::_validFrequency($frequency)) ||
10102       (($basis < 0) || ($basis > 4))) {
10103       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10104     }
10105 
10106     switch ($basis) {
10107       case 3: // Actual/365
10108           return 365 / $frequency;
10109       case 1: // Actual/actual
10110           if ($frequency == 1) {
10111             $daysPerYear = self::_daysPerYear(self::YEAR($maturity),$basis);
10112             return ($daysPerYear / $frequency);
10113           } else {
10114             $prev = self::_coupFirstPeriodDate($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, False);
10115             $next = self::_coupFirstPeriodDate($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, True);
10116             return ($next - $prev);
10117           }
10118       default: // US (NASD) 30/360, Actual/360 or European 30/360
10119           return 360 / $frequency;
10120     }
10121     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10122   } //  function COUPDAYS()

10125   public static function COUPDAYBS($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis=0) {
10126     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10127     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10128     $frequency  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($frequency);
10129     $basis    = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10130 
10131     if (is_string($settlement = self::_getDateValue($settlement))) {
10132       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10133     }
10134     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10135       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10136     }
10137 
10138     if (($settlement > $maturity) ||
10139       (!self::_validFrequency($frequency)) ||
10140       (($basis < 0) || ($basis > 4))) {
10141       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10142     }
10143 
10144     $daysPerYear = self::_daysPerYear(self::YEAR($settlement),$basis);
10145     $prev = self::_coupFirstPeriodDate($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, False);
10146 
10147     return self::YEARFRAC($prev, $settlement, $basis) * $daysPerYear;
10148   } //  function COUPDAYBS()

10223   public static function COUPNUM($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis=0) {
10224     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10225     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10226     $frequency  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($frequency);
10227     $basis    = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10228 
10229     if (is_string($settlement = self::_getDateValue($settlement))) {
10230       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10231     }
10232     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10233       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10234     }
10235 
10236     if (($settlement > $maturity) ||
10237       (!self::_validFrequency($frequency)) ||
10238       (($basis < 0) || ($basis > 4))) {
10239       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10240     }
10241 
10242     $settlement = self::_coupFirstPeriodDate($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, True);
10243     $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis) * 365;
10244 
10245     switch ($frequency) {
10246       case 1: // annual payments
10247           return ceil($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / 360);
10248       case 2: // half-yearly
10249           return ceil($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / 180);
10250       case 4: // quarterly
10251           return ceil($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / 90);
10252       case 6: // bimonthly
10253           return ceil($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / 60);
10254       case 12: // monthly
10255           return ceil($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / 30);
10256     }
10257     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10258   } //  function COUPNUM()

10260 
10261   public static function PRICE($settlement, $maturity, $rate, $yield, $redemption, $frequency, $basis=0) {
10262     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10263     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10264     $rate   = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
10265     $yield    = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($yield);
10266     $redemption = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($redemption);
10267     $frequency  = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($frequency);
10268     $basis    = (is_null($basis)) ? 0 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10269 
10270     if (is_string($settlement = self::_getDateValue($settlement))) {
10271       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10272     }
10273     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10274       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10275     }
10276 
10277     if (($settlement > $maturity) ||
10278       (!self::_validFrequency($frequency)) ||
10279       (($basis < 0) || ($basis > 4))) {
10280       return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10281     }
10282 
10283     $dsc = self::COUPDAYSNC($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis);
10284     $e = self::COUPDAYS($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis);
10285     $n = self::COUPNUM($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis);
10286     $a = self::COUPDAYBS($settlement, $maturity, $frequency, $basis);
10287 
10288     $baseYF = 1.0 + ($yield / $frequency);
10289     $rfp  = 100 * ($rate / $frequency);
10290     $de = $dsc / $e;
10291 
10292     $result = $redemption / pow($baseYF, (--$n + $de));
10293     for($k = 0; $k <= $n; ++$k) {
10294       $result += $rfp / (pow($baseYF, ($k + $de)));
10295     }
10296     $result -= $rfp * ($a / $e);
10297 
10298     return $result;
10299   } //  function PRICE()

10301 
10321   public static function DISC($settlement, $maturity, $price, $redemption, $basis=0) {
10322     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10323     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10324     $price    = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($price);
10325     $redemption = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($redemption);
10326     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10327 
10328     //  Validate
10329     if ((is_numeric($price)) && (is_numeric($redemption)) && (is_numeric($basis))) {
10330       if (($price <= 0) || ($redemption <= 0)) {
10331         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10332       }
10333       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10334       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10335         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10336       }
10337 
10338       return ((1 - $price / $redemption) / $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10339     }
10340     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10341   } //  function DISC()

10363   public static function PRICEDISC($settlement, $maturity, $discount, $redemption, $basis=0) {
10364     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10365     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10366     $discount = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($discount);
10367     $redemption = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($redemption);
10368     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10369 
10370     //  Validate
10371     if ((is_numeric($discount)) && (is_numeric($redemption)) && (is_numeric($basis))) {
10372       if (($discount <= 0) || ($redemption <= 0)) {
10373         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10374       }
10375       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10376       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10377         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10378       }
10379 
10380       return $redemption * (1 - $discount * $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10381     }
10382     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10383   } //  function PRICEDISC()

10385 
10406   public static function PRICEMAT($settlement, $maturity, $issue, $rate, $yield, $basis=0) {
10407     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10408     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10409     $issue    = self::flattenSingleValue($issue);
10410     $rate   = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
10411     $yield    = self::flattenSingleValue($yield);
10412     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10413 
10414     //  Validate
10415     if (is_numeric($rate) && is_numeric($yield)) {
10416       if (($rate <= 0) || ($yield <= 0)) {
10417         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10418       }
10419       $daysPerYear = self::_daysPerYear(self::YEAR($settlement),$basis);
10420       if (!is_numeric($daysPerYear)) {
10421         return $daysPerYear;
10422       }
10423       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $settlement, $basis);
10424       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement)) {
10425         return $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement;
10426       }
10427       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement *= $daysPerYear;
10428       $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $maturity, $basis);
10429       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity)) {
10430         return $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity;
10431       }
10432       $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity *= $daysPerYear;
10433       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10434       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10435         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10436       }
10437       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity *= $daysPerYear;
10438 
10439       return ((100 + (($daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity / $daysPerYear) * $rate * 100)) /
10440            (1 + (($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity / $daysPerYear) * $yield)) -
10441            (($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement / $daysPerYear) * $rate * 100));
10442     }
10443     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10444   } //  function PRICEMAT()

10466   public static function RECEIVED($settlement, $maturity, $investment, $discount, $basis=0) {
10467     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10468     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10469     $investment = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($investment);
10470     $discount = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($discount);
10471     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10472 
10473     //  Validate
10474     if ((is_numeric($investment)) && (is_numeric($discount)) && (is_numeric($basis))) {
10475       if (($investment <= 0) || ($discount <= 0)) {
10476         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10477       }
10478       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10479       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10480         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10481       }
10482 
10483       return $investment / ( 1 - ($discount * $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity));
10484     }
10485     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10486   } //  function RECEIVED()

10508   public static function INTRATE($settlement, $maturity, $investment, $redemption, $basis=0) {
10509     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10510     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10511     $investment = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($investment);
10512     $redemption = (float) self::flattenSingleValue($redemption);
10513     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10514 
10515     //  Validate
10516     if ((is_numeric($investment)) && (is_numeric($redemption)) && (is_numeric($basis))) {
10517       if (($investment <= 0) || ($redemption <= 0)) {
10518         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10519       }
10520       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10521       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10522         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10523       }
10524 
10525       return (($redemption / $investment) - 1) / ($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10526     }
10527     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10528   } //  function INTRATE()

10543   public static function TBILLEQ($settlement, $maturity, $discount) {
10544     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10545     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10546     $discount = self::flattenSingleValue($discount);
10547 
10548     //  Use TBILLPRICE for validation
10549     $testValue = self::TBILLPRICE($settlement, $maturity, $discount);
10550     if (is_string($testValue)) {
10551       return $testValue;
10552     }
10553 
10554     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10555       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10556     }
10557 
10558     if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
10559       ++$maturity;
10560       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity) * 360;
10561     } else {
10562       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = (self::_getDateValue($maturity) - self::_getDateValue($settlement));
10563     }
10564 
10565     return (365 * $discount) / (360 - $discount * $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10566   } //  function TBILLEQ()

10581   public static function TBILLPRICE($settlement, $maturity, $discount) {
10582     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10583     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10584     $discount = self::flattenSingleValue($discount);
10585 
10586     if (is_string($maturity = self::_getDateValue($maturity))) {
10587       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10588     }
10589 
10590     //  Validate
10591     if (is_numeric($discount)) {
10592       if ($discount <= 0) {
10593         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10594       }
10595 
10596       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
10597         ++$maturity;
10598         $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity) * 360;
10599         if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10600           return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10601         }
10602       } else {
10603         $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = (self::_getDateValue($maturity) - self::_getDateValue($settlement));
10604       }
10605 
10606       if ($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity > 360) {
10607         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10608       }
10609 
10610       $price = 100 * (1 - (($discount * $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity) / 360));
10611       if ($price <= 0) {
10612         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10613       }
10614       return $price;
10615     }
10616     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10617   } //  function TBILLPRICE()

10632   public static function TBILLYIELD($settlement, $maturity, $price) {
10633     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10634     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10635     $price    = self::flattenSingleValue($price);
10636 
10637     //  Validate
10638     if (is_numeric($price)) {
10639       if ($price <= 0) {
10640         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10641       }
10642 
10643       if (self::$compatibilityMode == self::COMPATIBILITY_OPENOFFICE) {
10644         ++$maturity;
10645         $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity) * 360;
10646         if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10647           return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10648         }
10649       } else {
10650         $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = (self::_getDateValue($maturity) - self::_getDateValue($settlement));
10651       }
10652 
10653       if ($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity > 360) {
10654         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10655       }
10656 
10657       return ((100 - $price) / $price) * (360 / $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10658     }
10659     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10660   } //  function TBILLYIELD()

10673   public static function SLN($cost, $salvage, $life) {
10674     $cost   = self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
10675     $salvage  = self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
10676     $life   = self::flattenSingleValue($life);
10677 
10678     // Calculate
10679     if ((is_numeric($cost)) && (is_numeric($salvage)) && (is_numeric($life))) {
10680       if ($life < 0) {
10681         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10682       }
10683       return ($cost - $salvage) / $life;
10684     }
10685     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];

10709   public static function YIELDMAT($settlement, $maturity, $issue, $rate, $price, $basis=0) {
10710     $settlement = self::flattenSingleValue($settlement);
10711     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10712     $issue    = self::flattenSingleValue($issue);
10713     $rate   = self::flattenSingleValue($rate);
10714     $price    = self::flattenSingleValue($price);
10715     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10716 
10717     //  Validate
10718     if (is_numeric($rate) && is_numeric($price)) {
10719       if (($rate <= 0) || ($price <= 0)) {
10720         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10721       }
10722       $daysPerYear = self::_daysPerYear(self::YEAR($settlement),$basis);
10723       if (!is_numeric($daysPerYear)) {
10724         return $daysPerYear;
10725       }
10726       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $settlement, $basis);
10727       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement)) {
10728         return $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement;
10729       }
10730       $daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement *= $daysPerYear;
10731       $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($issue, $maturity, $basis);
10732       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity)) {
10733         return $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity;
10734       }
10735       $daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity *= $daysPerYear;
10736       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity = self::YEARFRAC($settlement, $maturity, $basis);
10737       if (!is_numeric($daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity)) {
10738         return $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity;
10739       }
10740       $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity *= $daysPerYear;
10741 
10742       return ((1 + (($daysBetweenIssueAndMaturity / $daysPerYear) * $rate) - (($price / 100) + (($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement / $daysPerYear) * $rate))) /
10743            (($price / 100) + (($daysBetweenIssueAndSettlement / $daysPerYear) * $rate))) *
10744            ($daysPerYear / $daysBetweenSettlementAndMaturity);
10745     }
10746     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10747   } //  function YIELDMAT()

10771     $maturity = self::flattenSingleValue($maturity);
10772     $price    = self::flattenSingleValue($price);
10773     $redemption = self::flattenSingleValue($redemption);
10774     $basis    = (int) self::flattenSingleValue($basis);
10775 
10776     //  Validate
10777     if (is_numeric($price) && is_numeric($redemption)) {
10778       if (($price <= 0) || ($redemption <= 0)) {
10779         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
10780       }
10781       $daysPerYear = self::_daysPerYear(self::YEAR($settlement),$basis);
10782       if (!is_numeric($daysPerYear)) {

10815   public static function CELL_ADDRESS($row, $column, $relativity=1, $referenceStyle=True, $sheetText='') {
10816     $row    = self::flattenSingleValue($row);
10817     $column   = self::flattenSingleValue($column);
10818     $relativity = self::flattenSingleValue($relativity);
10819     $sheetText  = self::flattenSingleValue($sheetText);
10820 
10821     if (($row < 1) || ($column < 1)) {
10822       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10823     }
10824 
10825     if ($sheetText > '') {
10826       if (strpos($sheetText,' ') !== False) { $sheetText = "'".$sheetText."'"; }
10827       $sheetText .='!';
10828     }
10829     if ((!is_bool($referenceStyle)) || $referenceStyle) {
10830       $rowRelative = $columnRelative = '$';
10831       $column = PHPExcel_Cell::stringFromColumnIndex($column-1);
10832       if (($relativity == 2) || ($relativity == 4)) { $columnRelative = ''; }
10833       if (($relativity == 3) || ($relativity == 4)) { $rowRelative = ''; }
10834       return $sheetText.$columnRelative.$column.$rowRelative.$row;
10835     } else {
10836       if (($relativity == 2) || ($relativity == 4)) { $column = '['.$column.']'; }
10837       if (($relativity == 3) || ($relativity == 4)) { $row = '['.$row.']'; }
10838       return $sheetText.'R'.$row.'C'.$column;
10839     }
10840   } //  function CELL_ADDRESS()

10854   public static function COLUMN($cellAddress=Null) {
10855     if (is_null($cellAddress) || trim($cellAddress) === '') { return 0; }
10856 
10857     if (is_array($cellAddress)) {
10858       foreach($cellAddress as $columnKey => $value) {
10859         $columnKey = preg_replace('/[^a-z]/i','',$columnKey);
10860         return (integer) PHPExcel_Cell::columnIndexFromString($columnKey);
10861       }
10862     } else {
10863       if (strpos($cellAddress,'!') !== false) {
10864         list($sheet,$cellAddress) = explode('!',$cellAddress);
10865       }
10866       if (strpos($cellAddress,':') !== false) {
10867         list($startAddress,$endAddress) = explode(':',$cellAddress);
10868         $startAddress = preg_replace('/[^a-z]/i','',$startAddress);
10869         $endAddress = preg_replace('/[^a-z]/i','',$endAddress);
10870         $returnValue = array();
10871         do {
10872           $returnValue[] = (integer) PHPExcel_Cell::columnIndexFromString($startAddress);
10873         } while ($startAddress++ != $endAddress);
10874         return $returnValue;
10875       } else {
10876         $cellAddress = preg_replace('/[^a-z]/i','',$cellAddress);
10877         return (integer) PHPExcel_Cell::columnIndexFromString($cellAddress);
10878       }
10879     }
10880   } //  function COLUMN()

10891   public static function COLUMNS($cellAddress=Null) {
10892     if (is_null($cellAddress) || $cellAddress === '') {
10893       return 1;
10894     } elseif (!is_array($cellAddress)) {
10895       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
10896     }
10897 
10898     $x = array_keys($cellAddress);
10899     $x = array_shift($x);
10900     $isMatrix = (is_numeric($x));
10901     list($columns,$rows) = PHPExcel_Calculation::_getMatrixDimensions($cellAddress);
10902 
10903     if ($isMatrix) {
10904       return $rows;
10905     } else {
10906       return $columns;
10907     }
10908   } //  function COLUMNS()
