10922   public static function ROW($cellAddress=Null) {
10923     if (is_null($cellAddress) || trim($cellAddress) === '') { return 0; }
10924 
10925     if (is_array($cellAddress)) {
10926       foreach($cellAddress as $columnKey => $rowValue) {
10927         foreach($rowValue as $rowKey => $cellValue) {
10928           return (integer) preg_replace('/[^0-9]/i','',$rowKey);
10929         }
10930       }
10931     } else {
10932       if (strpos($cellAddress,'!') !== false) {
10933         list($sheet,$cellAddress) = explode('!',$cellAddress);
10934       }
10935       if (strpos($cellAddress,':') !== false) {
10936         list($startAddress,$endAddress) = explode(':',$cellAddress);
10937         $startAddress = preg_replace('/[^0-9]/','',$startAddress);
10938         $endAddress = preg_replace('/[^0-9]/','',$endAddress);
10939         $returnValue = array();
10940         do {
10941           $returnValue[][] = (integer) $startAddress;
10942         } while ($startAddress++ != $endAddress);
10943         return $returnValue;
10944       } else {
10945         list($cellAddress) = explode(':',$cellAddress);
10946         return (integer) preg_replace('/[^0-9]/','',$cellAddress);
10947       }
10948     }
10949   } //  function ROW()

10987   public static function INDIRECT($cellAddress=Null, PHPExcel_Cell $pCell = null) {
10988     $cellAddress  = self::flattenSingleValue($cellAddress);
10989     if (is_null($cellAddress) || $cellAddress === '') {
10990       return self::REF();
10991     }
10992 
10993     $cellAddress1 = $cellAddress;
10994     $cellAddress2 = NULL;
10995     if (strpos($cellAddress,':') !== false) {
10996       list($cellAddress1,$cellAddress2) = explode(':',$cellAddress);
10997     }
10998 
10999     if ((!preg_match('/^'.PHPExcel_Calculation::CALCULATION_REGEXP_CELLREF.'$/i', $cellAddress1, $matches)) ||
11000       ((!is_null($cellAddress2)) && (!preg_match('/^'.PHPExcel_Calculation::CALCULATION_REGEXP_CELLREF.'$/i', $cellAddress2, $matches)))) {
11001       return self::REF();
11002     }
11003 
11004     if (strpos($cellAddress,'!') !== false) {
11005       list($sheetName,$cellAddress) = explode('!',$cellAddress);
11006       $pSheet = $pCell->getParent()->getParent()->getSheetByName($sheetName);
11007     } else {
11008       $pSheet = $pCell->getParent();
11009     }
11010 
11011     return PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->extractCellRange($cellAddress, $pSheet, False);
11012   } //  function INDIRECT()

11037   public static function OFFSET($cellAddress=Null,$rows=0,$columns=0,$height=null,$width=null) {
11038     $rows   = self::flattenSingleValue($rows);
11039     $columns  = self::flattenSingleValue($columns);
11040     $height   = self::flattenSingleValue($height);
11041     $width    = self::flattenSingleValue($width);
11042     if ($cellAddress == Null) {
11043       return 0;
11044     }
11045 
11046     $args = func_get_args();
11047     $pCell = array_pop($args);
11048     if (!is_object($pCell)) {
11049       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11050     }
11051 
11052     $sheetName = null;
11053     if (strpos($cellAddress,"!")) {
11054       list($sheetName,$cellAddress) = explode("!",$cellAddress);
11055     }
11056     if (strpos($cellAddress,":")) {
11057       list($startCell,$endCell) = explode(":",$cellAddress);
11058     } else {
11059       $startCell = $endCell = $cellAddress;
11060     }
11061     list($startCellColumn,$startCellRow) = PHPExcel_Cell::coordinateFromString($startCell);
11062     list($endCellColumn,$endCellRow) = PHPExcel_Cell::coordinateFromString($endCell);
11063 
11064     $startCellRow += $rows;
11065     $startCellColumn = PHPExcel_Cell::columnIndexFromString($startCellColumn) - 1;
11066     $startCellColumn += $columns;
11067 
11068     if (($startCellRow <= 0) || ($startCellColumn < 0)) {
11069       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11070     }
11071     $endCellColumn = PHPExcel_Cell::columnIndexFromString($endCellColumn) - 1;
11072     if (($width != null) && (!is_object($width))) {
11073       $endCellColumn = $startCellColumn + $width - 1;
11074     } else {
11075       $endCellColumn += $columns;
11076     }
11077     $startCellColumn = PHPExcel_Cell::stringFromColumnIndex($startCellColumn);
11078 
11079     if (($height != null) && (!is_object($height))) {
11080       $endCellRow = $startCellRow + $height - 1;
11081     } else {
11082       $endCellRow += $rows;
11083     }
11084 
11085     if (($endCellRow <= 0) || ($endCellColumn < 0)) {
11086       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11087     }
11088     $endCellColumn = PHPExcel_Cell::stringFromColumnIndex($endCellColumn);
11089 
11090     $cellAddress = $startCellColumn.$startCellRow;
11091     if (($startCellColumn != $endCellColumn) || ($startCellRow != $endCellRow)) {
11092       $cellAddress .= ':'.$endCellColumn.$endCellRow;
11093     }
11094 
11095     if ($sheetName !== null) {
11096       $pSheet = $pCell->getParent()->getParent()->getSheetByName($sheetName);
11097     } else {
11098       $pSheet = $pCell->getParent();
11099     }
11100 
11101     return PHPExcel_Calculation::getInstance()->extractCellRange($cellAddress, $pSheet, False);
11102   } //  function OFFSET()

11105   public static function CHOOSE() {
11106     $chooseArgs = func_get_args();
11107     $chosenEntry = self::flattenArray(array_shift($chooseArgs));
11108     $entryCount = count($chooseArgs) - 1;
11109 
11110     if(is_array($chosenEntry)) {
11111       $chosenEntry = array_shift($chosenEntry);
11112     }
11113     if ((is_numeric($chosenEntry)) && (!is_bool($chosenEntry))) {
11114       --$chosenEntry;
11115     } else {
11116       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11117     }
11118     $chosenEntry = floor($chosenEntry);
11119     if (($chosenEntry <= 0) || ($chosenEntry > $entryCount)) {
11120       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11121     }
11122 
11123     if (is_array($chooseArgs[$chosenEntry])) {
11124       return self::flattenArray($chooseArgs[$chosenEntry]);
11125     } else {
11126       return $chooseArgs[$chosenEntry];
11127     }
11128   } //  function CHOOSE()

11141   public static function MATCH($lookup_value, $lookup_array, $match_type=1) {
11142     $lookup_array = self::flattenArray($lookup_array);
11143     $lookup_value = self::flattenSingleValue($lookup_value);
11144     $match_type = (is_null($match_type)) ? 1 : (int) self::flattenSingleValue($match_type);
11145     //  MATCH is not case sensitive
11146     $lookup_value = strtolower($lookup_value);
11147 
11148     //  lookup_value type has to be number, text, or logical values
11149     if ((!is_numeric($lookup_value)) && (!is_string($lookup_value)) && (!is_bool($lookup_value))) {
11150       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11151     }
11152 
11153     //  match_type is 0, 1 or -1
11154     if (($match_type !== 0) && ($match_type !== -1) && ($match_type !== 1)) {
11155       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11156     }
11157 
11158     //  lookup_array should not be empty
11159     $lookupArraySize = count($lookup_array);
11160     if ($lookupArraySize <= 0) {
11161       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11162     }
11163 
11164     //  lookup_array should contain only number, text, or logical values, or empty (null) cells
11165     foreach($lookup_array as $i => $lookupArrayValue) {
11166       //  check the type of the value
11167       if ((!is_numeric($lookupArrayValue)) && (!is_string($lookupArrayValue)) &&
11168         (!is_bool($lookupArrayValue)) && (!is_null($lookupArrayValue))) {
11169         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11170       }
11171       //  convert strings to lowercase for case-insensitive testing
11172       if (is_string($lookupArrayValue)) {
11173         $lookup_array[$i] = strtolower($lookupArrayValue);
11174       }
11175       if ((is_null($lookupArrayValue)) && (($match_type == 1) || ($match_type == -1))) {
11176         $lookup_array = array_slice($lookup_array,0,$i-1);
11177       }
11178     }
11179 
11180     // if match_type is 1 or -1, the list has to be ordered
11181     if ($match_type == 1) {
11182       asort($lookup_array);
11183       $keySet = array_keys($lookup_array);
11184     } elseif($match_type == -1) {
11185       arsort($lookup_array);
11186       $keySet = array_keys($lookup_array);
11187     }
11188 
11189     // **
11190     // find the match
11191     // **
11192     // loop on the cells
11193 //    var_dump($lookup_array);
11194 //    echo '<br />';
11195     foreach($lookup_array as $i => $lookupArrayValue) {
11196       if (($match_type == 0) && ($lookupArrayValue == $lookup_value)) {
11197         //  exact match
11198         return ++$i;
11199       } elseif (($match_type == -1) && ($lookupArrayValue <= $lookup_value)) {
11200 //        echo '$i = '.$i.' => ';
11201 //        var_dump($lookupArrayValue);
11202 //        echo '<br />';
11203 //        echo 'Keyset = ';
11204 //        var_dump($keySet);
11205 //        echo '<br />';
11206         $i = array_search($i,$keySet);
11207 //        echo '$i='.$i.'<br />';
11208         // if match_type is -1 <=> find the smallest value that is greater than or equal to lookup_value
11209         if ($i < 1){
11210           // 1st cell was allready smaller than the lookup_value
11211           break;
11212         } else {
11213           // the previous cell was the match
11214           return $keySet[$i-1]+1;
11215         }
11216       } elseif (($match_type == 1) && ($lookupArrayValue >= $lookup_value)) {
11217 //        echo '$i = '.$i.' => ';
11218 //        var_dump($lookupArrayValue);
11219 //        echo '<br />';
11220 //        echo 'Keyset = ';
11221 //        var_dump($keySet);
11222 //        echo '<br />';
11223         $i = array_search($i,$keySet);
11224 //        echo '$i='.$i.'<br />';
11225         // if match_type is 1 <=> find the largest value that is less than or equal to lookup_value
11226         if ($i < 1){
11227           // 1st cell was allready bigger than the lookup_value
11228           break;
11229         } else {
11230           // the previous cell was the match
11231           return $keySet[$i-1]+1;
11232         }
11233       }
11234     }
11235 
11236     //  unsuccessful in finding a match, return #N/A error value
11237     return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11238   } //  function MATCH()
11239

11252   public static function INDEX($arrayValues,$rowNum = 0,$columnNum = 0) {
11253 
11254     if (($rowNum < 0) || ($columnNum < 0)) {
11255       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11256     }
11257 
11258     if (!is_array($arrayValues)) {
11259       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11260     }
11261 
11262     $rowKeys = array_keys($arrayValues);
11263     $columnKeys = @array_keys($arrayValues[$rowKeys[0]]);
11264 
11265     if ($columnNum > count($columnKeys)) {
11266       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11267     } elseif ($columnNum == 0) {
11268       if ($rowNum == 0) {
11269         return $arrayValues;
11270       }
11271       $rowNum = $rowKeys[--$rowNum];
11272       $returnArray = array();
11273       foreach($arrayValues as $arrayColumn) {
11274         if (is_array($arrayColumn)) {
11275           if (isset($arrayColumn[$rowNum])) {
11276             $returnArray[] = $arrayColumn[$rowNum];
11277           } else {
11278             return $arrayValues[$rowNum];
11279           }
11280         } else {
11281           return $arrayValues[$rowNum];
11282         }
11283       }
11284       return $returnArray;
11285     }
11286     $columnNum = $columnKeys[--$columnNum];
11287     if ($rowNum > count($rowKeys)) {
11288       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11289     } elseif ($rowNum == 0) {
11290       return $arrayValues[$columnNum];
11291     }
11292     $rowNum = $rowKeys[--$rowNum];
11293 
11294     return $arrayValues[$rowNum][$columnNum];
11295   } //  function INDEX()

11313   public static function N($value) {
11314     while (is_array($value)) {
11315       $value = array_shift($value);
11316     }
11317 
11318     switch (gettype($value)) {
11319       case 'double' :
11320       case 'float'  :
11321       case 'integer'  :
11322         return $value;
11323         break;
11324       case 'boolean'  :
11325         return (integer) $value;
11326         break;
11327       case 'string' :
11328         //  Errors
11329         if ((strlen($value) > 0) && ($value{0} == '#')) {
11330           return $value;
11331         }
11332         break;
11333     }
11334     return 0;
11335   } //  function N()

11352   public static function TYPE($value) {
11353     $value  = self::flattenArrayIndexed($value);
11354     if (is_array($value) && (count($value) > 1)) {
11355       $a = array_keys($value);
11356       $a = array_pop($a);
11357       //  Range of cells is an error
11358       if (self::isCellValue($a)) {
11359         return 16;
11360       //  Test for Matrix
11361       } elseif (self::isMatrixValue($a)) {
11362         return 64;
11363       }
11364     } elseif(count($value) == 0) {
11365       //  Empty Cell
11366       return 1;
11367     }
11368     $value  = self::flattenSingleValue($value);
11369 
11370     if ((is_float($value)) || (is_int($value))) {
11371         return 1;
11372     } elseif(is_bool($value)) {
11373         return 4;
11374     } elseif(is_array($value)) {
11375         return 64;
11376         break;
11377     } elseif(is_string($value)) {
11378       //  Errors
11379       if ((strlen($value) > 0) && ($value{0} == '#')) {
11380         return 16;
11381       }
11382       return 2;
11383     }
11384     return 0;
11385   } //  function TYPE()

11399   public static function SYD($cost, $salvage, $life, $period) {
11400     $cost   = self::flattenSingleValue($cost);
11401     $salvage  = self::flattenSingleValue($salvage);
11402     $life   = self::flattenSingleValue($life);
11403     $period   = self::flattenSingleValue($period);
11404 
11405     // Calculate
11406     if ((is_numeric($cost)) && (is_numeric($salvage)) && (is_numeric($life)) && (is_numeric($period))) {
11407       if (($life < 1) || ($period > $life)) {
11408         return self::$_errorCodes['num'];
11409       }
11410       return (($cost - $salvage) * ($life - $period + 1) * 2) / ($life * ($life + 1));
11411     }
11412     return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11413   } //  function SYD()

11424   public static function TRANSPOSE($matrixData) {
11425     $returnMatrix = array();
11426     if (!is_array($matrixData)) { $matrixData = array(array($matrixData)); }
11427 
11428     $column = 0;
11429     foreach($matrixData as $matrixRow) {
11430       $row = 0;
11431       foreach($matrixRow as $matrixCell) {
11432         $returnMatrix[$row][$column] = $matrixCell;
11433         ++$row;
11434       }
11435       ++$column;
11436     }
11437     return $returnMatrix;
11438   } //  function TRANSPOSE()

11448   public static function MMULT($matrixData1,$matrixData2) {
11449     $matrixAData = $matrixBData = array();
11450     if (!is_array($matrixData1)) { $matrixData1 = array(array($matrixData1)); }
11451     if (!is_array($matrixData2)) { $matrixData2 = array(array($matrixData2)); }
11452 
11453     $rowA = 0;
11454     foreach($matrixData1 as $matrixRow) {
11455       $columnA = 0;
11456       foreach($matrixRow as $matrixCell) {
11457         if ((is_string($matrixCell)) || ($matrixCell === null)) {
11458           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11459         }
11460         $matrixAData[$rowA][$columnA] = $matrixCell;
11461         ++$columnA;
11462       }
11463       ++$rowA;
11464     }
11465     try {
11466       $matrixA = new Matrix($matrixAData);
11467       $rowB = 0;
11468       foreach($matrixData2 as $matrixRow) {
11469         $columnB = 0;
11470         foreach($matrixRow as $matrixCell) {
11471           if ((is_string($matrixCell)) || ($matrixCell === null)) {
11472             return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11473           }
11474           $matrixBData[$rowB][$columnB] = $matrixCell;
11475           ++$columnB;
11476         }
11477         ++$rowB;
11478       }
11479       $matrixB = new Matrix($matrixBData);
11480 
11481       if (($rowA != $columnB) || ($rowB != $columnA)) {
11482         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11483       }
11484 
11485       return $matrixA->times($matrixB)->getArray();
11486     } catch (Exception $ex) {
11487       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11488     }
11489   } //  function MMULT()

11498   public static function MINVERSE($matrixValues) {
11499     $matrixData = array();
11500     if (!is_array($matrixValues)) { $matrixValues = array(array($matrixValues)); }
11501 
11502     $row = $maxColumn = 0;
11503     foreach($matrixValues as $matrixRow) {
11504       $column = 0;
11505       foreach($matrixRow as $matrixCell) {
11506         if ((is_string($matrixCell)) || ($matrixCell === null)) {
11507           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11508         }
11509         $matrixData[$column][$row] = $matrixCell;
11510         ++$column;
11511       }
11512       if ($column > $maxColumn) { $maxColumn = $column; }
11513       ++$row;
11514     }
11515     if ($row != $maxColumn) { return self::$_errorCodes['value']; }
11516 
11517     try {
11518       $matrix = new Matrix($matrixData);
11519       return $matrix->inverse()->getArray();
11520     } catch (Exception $ex) {
11521       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11522     }
11523   } //  function MINVERSE()

11532   public static function MDETERM($matrixValues) {
11533     $matrixData = array();
11534     if (!is_array($matrixValues)) { $matrixValues = array(array($matrixValues)); }
11535 
11536     $row = $maxColumn = 0;
11537     foreach($matrixValues as $matrixRow) {
11538       $column = 0;
11539       foreach($matrixRow as $matrixCell) {
11540         if ((is_string($matrixCell)) || ($matrixCell === null)) {
11541           return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11542         }
11543         $matrixData[$column][$row] = $matrixCell;
11544         ++$column;
11545       }
11546       if ($column > $maxColumn) { $maxColumn = $column; }
11547       ++$row;
11548     }
11549     if ($row != $maxColumn) { return self::$_errorCodes['value']; }
11550 
11551     try {
11552       $matrix = new Matrix($matrixData);
11553       return $matrix->det();
11554     } catch (Exception $ex) {
11555       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11556     }
11557   } //  function MDETERM()

11566   public static function SUMPRODUCT() {
11567     $arrayList = func_get_args();
11568 
11569     $wrkArray = self::flattenArray(array_shift($arrayList));
11570     $wrkCellCount = count($wrkArray);
11571 
11572     foreach($arrayList as $matrixData) {
11573       $array2 = self::flattenArray($matrixData);
11574       $count = count($array2);
11575       if ($wrkCellCount != $count) {
11576         return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11577       }
11578 
11579       foreach ($array2 as $i => $val) {
11580         if (((is_numeric($wrkArray[$i])) && (!is_string($wrkArray[$i]))) &&
11581           ((is_numeric($val)) && (!is_string($val)))) {
11582           $wrkArray[$i] *= $val;
11583         }
11584       }
11585     }
11586 
11587     return array_sum($wrkArray);
11588   } //  function SUMPRODUCT()

11597   public static function SUMX2MY2($matrixData1,$matrixData2) {
11598     $array1 = self::flattenArray($matrixData1);
11599     $array2 = self::flattenArray($matrixData2);
11600     $count1 = count($array1);
11601     $count2 = count($array2);
11602     if ($count1 < $count2) {
11603       $count = $count1;
11604     } else {
11605       $count = $count2;
11606     }
11607 
11608     $result = 0;
11609     for ($i = 0; $i < $count; ++$i) {
11610       if (((is_numeric($array1[$i])) && (!is_string($array1[$i]))) &&
11611         ((is_numeric($array2[$i])) && (!is_string($array2[$i])))) {
11612         $result += ($array1[$i] * $array1[$i]) - ($array2[$i] * $array2[$i]);
11613       }
11614     }
11615 
11616     return $result;
11617   } //  function SUMX2MY2()

11640         ((is_numeric($array2[$i])) && (!is_string($array2[$i])))) {

11655   public static function SUMXMY2($matrixData1,$matrixData2) {

11657     $array2 = self::flattenArray($matrixData2);

11660     if ($count1 < $count2) {
11661       $count = $count1;
11662     } else {
11663       $count = $count2;

11665

11667     for ($i = 0; $i < $count; ++$i) {
11668       if (((is_numeric($array1[$i])) && (!is_string($array1[$i]))) &&
11669         ((is_numeric($array2[$i])) && (!is_string($array2[$i])))) {
11670         $result += ($array1[$i] - $array2[$i]) * ($array1[$i] - $array2[$i]);

11678   private static function _vlookupSort($a,$b) {
11679     $f = array_keys($a);
11680     $firstColumn = array_shift($f);
11681     if (strtolower($a[$firstColumn]) == strtolower($b[$firstColumn])) {
11682       return 0;
11683     }
11684     return (strtolower($a[$firstColumn]) < strtolower($b[$firstColumn])) ? -1 : 1;
11685   } //  function _vlookupSort()

11697   public static function VLOOKUP($lookup_value, $lookup_array, $index_number, $not_exact_match=true) {
11698     $lookup_value = self::flattenSingleValue($lookup_value);
11699     $index_number = self::flattenSingleValue($index_number);
11700     $not_exact_match  = self::flattenSingleValue($not_exact_match);
11701 
11702     // index_number must be greater than or equal to 1
11703     if ($index_number < 1) {
11704       return self::$_errorCodes['value'];
11705     }
11706 
11707     // index_number must be less than or equal to the number of columns in lookup_array
11708     if ((!is_array($lookup_array)) || (count($lookup_array) < 1)) {
11709       return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11710     } else {
11711       $f = array_keys($lookup_array);
11712       $firstRow = array_pop($f);
11713       if ((!is_array($lookup_array[$firstRow])) || ($index_number > count($lookup_array[$firstRow]))) {
11714         return self::$_errorCodes['reference'];
11715       } else {
11716         $columnKeys = array_keys($lookup_array[$firstRow]);
11717         $returnColumn = $columnKeys[--$index_number];
11718         $firstColumn = array_shift($columnKeys);
11719       }
11720     }
11721 
11722     if (!$not_exact_match) {
11723       uasort($lookup_array,array('self','_vlookupSort'));
11724     }
11725 
11726     $rowNumber = $rowValue = False;
11727     foreach($lookup_array as $rowKey => $rowData) {
11728       if (strtolower($rowData[$firstColumn]) > strtolower($lookup_value)) {
11729         break;
11730       }
11731       $rowNumber = $rowKey;
11732       $rowValue = $rowData[$firstColumn];
11733     }
11734 
11735     if ($rowNumber !== false) {
11736       if ((!$not_exact_match) && ($rowValue != $lookup_value)) {
11737         //  if an exact match is required, we have what we need to return an appropriate response
11738         return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11739       } else {
11740         //  otherwise return the appropriate value
11741         return $lookup_array[$rowNumber][$returnColumn];
11742       }
11743     }
11744 
11745     return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11746   } //  function VLOOKUP()
11747 
11748 
11757   public static function LOOKUP($lookup_value, $lookup_vector, $result_vector=null) {
11758     $lookup_value = self::flattenSingleValue($lookup_value);
11759 
11760     if (!is_array($lookup_vector)) {
11761       return self::$_errorCodes['na'];
11762     }
11763     $lookupRows = count($lookup_vector);
11764     $l = array_keys($lookup_vector);
11765     $l = array_shift($l);
11766     $lookupColumns = count($lookup_vector[$l]);
11767     if ((($lookupRows == 1) && ($lookupColumns > 1)) || (($lookupRows == 2) && ($lookupColumns != 2))) {
11768       $lookup_vector = self::TRANSPOSE($lookup_vector);
11769       $lookupRows = count($lookup_vector);
11770       $l = array_keys($lookup_vector);
11771       $lookupColumns = count($lookup_vector[array_shift($l)]);
11772     }
11773 
11774     if (is_null($result_vector)) {
11775       $result_vector = $lookup_vector;
11776     }
11777     $resultRows = count($result_vector);
11778     $l = array_keys($result_vector);
11779     $l = array_shift($l);
11780     $resultColumns = count($result_vector[$l]);
11781     if ((($resultRows == 1) && ($resultColumns > 1)) || (($resultRows == 2) && ($resultColumns != 2))) {
11782       $result_vector = self::TRANSPOSE($result_vector);
11783       $resultRows = count($result_vector);
11784       $r = array_keys($result_vector);
11785       $resultColumns = count($result_vector[array_shift($r)]);
11786     }
11787 
11788     if ($lookupRows == 2) {
11789       $result_vector = array_pop($lookup_vector);
11790       $lookup_vector = array_shift($lookup_vector);
11791     }
11792     if ($lookupColumns != 2) {
11793       foreach($lookup_vector as &$value) {
11794         if (is_array($value)) {
11795           $k = array_keys($value);
11796           $key1 = $key2 = array_shift($k);
11797           $key2++;
11798           $dataValue1 = $value[$key1];
11799         } else {
11800           $key1 = 0;
11801           $key2 = 1;
11802           $dataValue1 = $value;
11803         }
11804         $dataValue2 = array_shift($result_vector);
11805         if (is_array($dataValue2)) {
11806           $dataValue2 = array_shift($dataValue2);
11807         }
11808         $value = array($key1 => $dataValue1, $key2 => $dataValue2);
11809       }
11810       unset($value);
11811     }
11812 
11813     return self::VLOOKUP($lookup_value,$lookup_vector,2);
11814   } //  function LOOKUP()
11815 
11816 
11823   public static function flattenArray($array) {
11824     if (!is_array($array)) {
11825       return (array) $array;
11826     }
11827 
11828     $arrayValues = array();
11829     foreach ($array as $value) {
11830       if (is_array($value)) {
11831         foreach ($value as $val) {
11832           if (is_array($val)) {
11833             foreach ($val as $v) {
11834               $arrayValues[] = $v;
11835             }
11836           } else {
11837             $arrayValues[] = $val;
11838           }
11839         }
11840       } else {
11841         $arrayValues[] = $value;
11842       }
11843     }
11844 
11845     return $arrayValues;
11846   } //  function flattenArray()
11847 
11848 
11855   public static function flattenArrayIndexed($array) {
11856     if (!is_array($array)) {
11857       return (array) $array;
11858     }
11859 
11860     $arrayValues = array();
11861     foreach ($array as $k1 => $value) {
11862       if (is_array($value)) {
11863         foreach ($value as $k2 => $val) {
11864           if (is_array($val)) {
11865             foreach ($val as $k3 => $v) {
11866               $arrayValues[$k1.'.'.$k2.'.'.$k3] = $v;
11867             }
11868           } else {
11869             $arrayValues[$k1.'.'.$k2] = $val;
11870           }
11871         }
11872       } else {
11873         $arrayValues[$k1] = $value;
11874       }
11875     }
11876 
11877     return $arrayValues;
11878   } //  function flattenArrayIndexed()
11879 
11880 
11887   public static function flattenSingleValue($value = '') {
11888     while (is_array($value)) {
11889       $value = array_pop($value);
11890     }
11891 
11892     return $value;
11893   } //  function flattenSingleValue()

11898 //
11899 //  There are a few mathematical functions that aren't available on all versions of PHP for all platforms
11900 //  These functions aren't available in Windows implementations of PHP prior to version 5.3.0
11901 //  So we test if they do exist for this version of PHP/operating platform; and if not we create them
11902 //
11903 if (!function_exists('acosh')) {
11904   function acosh($x) {
11905     return 2 * log(sqrt(($x + 1) / 2) + sqrt(($x - 1) / 2));
11906   } //  function acosh()
11907 }
11908 
11909 if (!function_exists('asinh')) {
11910   function asinh($x) {
11911     return log($x + sqrt(1 + $x * $x));
11912   } //  function asinh()
11913 }
11914 
11915 if (!function_exists('atanh')) {
11916   function atanh($x) {
11917     return (log(1 + $x) - log(1 - $x)) / 2;
11918   } //  function atanh()
11919 }
11920 
11921 if (!function_exists('money_format')) {
11922   function money_format($format, $number) {
11923     $regex = array( '/%((?:[\^!\-]|\+|\(|\=.)*)([0-9]+)?(?:#([0-9]+))?',
11924              '(?:\.([0-9]+))?([in%])/'
11925             );
11926     $regex = implode('', $regex);
11927     if (setlocale(LC_MONETARY, null) == '') {
11928       setlocale(LC_MONETARY, '');
11929     }
11930     $locale = localeconv();
11931     $number = floatval($number);
11932     if (!preg_match($regex, $format, $fmatch)) {
11933       trigger_error("No format specified or invalid format", E_USER_WARNING);
11934       return $number;
11935     }
11936     $flags = array( 'fillchar'  => preg_match('/\=(.)/', $fmatch[1], $match) ? $match[1] : ' ',
11937             'nogroup' => preg_match('/\^/', $fmatch[1]) > 0,
11938             'usesignal' => preg_match('/\+|\(/', $fmatch[1], $match) ? $match[0] : '+',
11939             'nosimbol'  => preg_match('/\!/', $fmatch[1]) > 0,
11940             'isleft'  => preg_match('/\-/', $fmatch[1]) > 0
11941             );
11942     $width  = trim($fmatch[2]) ? (int)$fmatch[2] : 0;
11943     $left = trim($fmatch[3]) ? (int)$fmatch[3] : 0;
11944     $right  = trim($fmatch[4]) ? (int)$fmatch[4] : $locale['int_frac_digits'];
11945     $conversion = $fmatch[5];
11946     $positive = true;
11947     if ($number < 0) {
11948       $positive = false;
11949       $number *= -1;
11950     }
11951     $letter = $positive ? 'p' : 'n';
11952     $prefix = $suffix = $cprefix = $csuffix = $signal = '';
11953     if (!$positive) {
11954       $signal = $locale['negative_sign'];
11955       switch (true) {
11956         case $locale['n_sign_posn'] == 0 || $flags['usesignal'] == '(':
11957           $prefix = '(';
11958           $suffix = ')';
11959           break;
11960         case $locale['n_sign_posn'] == 1:
11961           $prefix = $signal;
11962           break;
11963         case $locale['n_sign_posn'] == 2:
11964           $suffix = $signal;
11965           break;
11966         case $locale['n_sign_posn'] == 3:
11967           $cprefix = $signal;
11968           break;
11969         case $locale['n_sign_posn'] == 4:
11970           $csuffix = $signal;
11971           break;
11972       }
11973     }
11974     if (!$flags['nosimbol']) {
11975       $currency = $cprefix;
11976       $currency .= ($conversion == 'i' ? $locale['int_curr_symbol'] : $locale['currency_symbol']);
11977       $currency .= $csuffix;
11978       $currency = iconv('ISO-8859-1','UTF-8',$currency);
11979     } else {
11980       $currency = '';
11981     }
11982     $space = $locale["{$letter}_sep_by_space"] ? ' ' : '';
11983 
11984     $number = number_format($number, $right, $locale['mon_decimal_point'], $flags['nogroup'] ? '' : $locale['mon_thousands_sep'] );
11985     $number = explode($locale['mon_decimal_point'], $number);
11986 
11987     $n = strlen($prefix) + strlen($currency);
11988     if ($left > 0 && $left > $n) {
11989       if ($flags['isleft']) {
11990         $number[0] .= str_repeat($flags['fillchar'], $left - $n);
11991       } else {
11992         $number[0] = str_repeat($flags['fillchar'], $left - $n) . $number[0];
11993       }
11994     }
11995     $number = implode($locale['mon_decimal_point'], $number);
11996     if ($locale["{$letter}_cs_precedes"]) {
11997       $number = $prefix . $currency . $space . $number . $suffix;
11998     } else {
11999       $number = $prefix . $number . $space . $currency . $suffix;
12000     }
12001     if ($width > 0) {
12002       $number = str_pad($number, $width, $flags['fillchar'], $flags['isleft'] ? STR_PAD_RIGHT : STR_PAD_LEFT);
12003     }
12004     $format = str_replace($fmatch[0], $number, $format);
12005     return $format;
12006   } //  function money_format()
12007 }

12010 //
12011 //  Strangely, PHP doesn't have a mb_str_replace multibyte function
12012 //  As we'll only ever use this function with UTF-8 characters, we can simply "hard-code" the character set
12013 //
12014 if ((!function_exists('mb_str_replace')) &&
12015   (function_exists('mb_substr')) && (function_exists('mb_strlen')) && (function_exists('mb_strpos'))) {
12016   function mb_str_replace($search, $replace, $subject) {
12017     if(is_array($subject)) {
12018       $ret = array();
12019       foreach($subject as $key => $val) {
12020         $ret[$key] = mb_str_replace($search, $replace, $val);
12021       }
12022       return $ret;
12023     }
12024 
12025     foreach((array) $search as $key => $s) {
12026       if($s == '') {
12027         continue;
12028       }
12029       $r = !is_array($replace) ? $replace : (array_key_exists($key, $replace) ? $replace[$key] : '');
12030       $pos = mb_strpos($subject, $s, 0, 'UTF-8');
12031       while($pos !== false) {
12032         $subject = mb_substr($subject, 0, $pos, 'UTF-8') . $r . mb_substr($subject, $pos + mb_strlen($s, 'UTF-8'), 65535, 'UTF-8');
12033         $pos = mb_strpos($subject, $s, $pos + mb_strlen($r, 'UTF-8'), 'UTF-8');
12034       }
12035     }
12036     return $subject;
12037   }
12038 }
